Srinivasamakhi Vedantadesika: Dasavidhahetunirupana (part of the Vaikhanasasutratatparyacintamani)
Based on (pp. 1-122) the of the Devanāgarī-ed. by R. Parthasarathi Bhattacarya:
Śrīvaikhānasagṛhyasūtra (= DHN[D]); 2 vols., Akulamannāḍu, 1967 (reprint Tirupati, 1997/98).


Input by Ute Hüsken



PLAIN VERSION (without notes)



STRUCTURE OF REFERENCES:
[nn.nn] = pagination of R. Pārthasārathi Bhaṭṭācārya's edition (at the beginning of the line)





FURTHER NOTES BY THE CONTRIBUTOR:
Die in eckige Klammern gesetzten Angaben im Text sowie die Anmerkungen sind Ergänzungen von Ute Hüsken.
Die Angaben aus dem Inhaltsverzeichnis der Devanāgarī-Edition sind in eckigen Klammern als Zwischenüberschriften in den Text eingefügt.
Die Quellennachweise bei Zitaten stehen in eckigen Klammern am rechten Rand oder in den Anmerkungen - dort ohne eckige Klammern.
Abweichende Lesarten der älteren Telugu-Ausgabe des Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa (Abk.: DHN[T]; s.u.) sowie der zitierten Texte sind gelegentlich in Anmerkungen notiert, jedoch nicht durchgängig.

Wird im Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa durch kurze Zitate auf längere Textzusammenhänge Bezug genommen, sind diese - sofern verifiziert - an der ersten Stelle ihres Vorkommens vollständig in den Anmerkungen zitiert. An weiteren Stellen wird auf das erste Zitat verwiesen. Die Verse sind in der vorliegenden Textwiedergabe der Ausgabe folgend eingerückt, Daṇḍas im Prosa-Text durch Punkte und Kommata ersetzt.

Das Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa liegt in zwei Editionen vor, die beide von dem Vaikhānasa-Gelehrten Pārthasārathi Bhaṭṭācārya besorgt wurden. Die erste Edition erschien 1931 in Telugu-Schrift und umfaßt als Grundtext nur das Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa.
Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa by Śrīnivāsa Dīkṣita [in Telugu-script], ed. as Śrīvaikhānasasūtratātparyacintāmaṇidhṛto Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇākhyo bhāgaḥ, with Sanskrit-commentary and explanations in Telugu by Rompicarla Bhattar Srinivasa Aiyangar, Igavaripalem, 1931 (Śrīvaikhānasagranthamālā, Anubandha 5).

Wenngleich dieser Telugu-Druck an vielen Stellen die vermutlich richtigere Lesart enthält und die darin gegebenen Zitate den zitierten Texten in der uns heute gedruckt vorliegenden Form häufig näherkommen, ist der Textwiedergabe in der vorliegenden Arbeit die 36 Jahre später erschienene Devanāgarī-Edition zugrunde gelegt, da der Telugu-Druck an vielen Stellen nicht mehr lesbar ist. Zudem ist die ältere Telugu-Edition des Textes weltweit nur in wenigen Bibliotheken vorhanden und wegen der Brüchigkeit des Papiers kaum zu benutzen. Selbst im vorbildlich restaurierten Exemplar der Niedersächsischen Staats-und Universitätsbibliothek Göttingen (Signatur A 2000 A 35512) sind etliche Passagen unleserlich. Der Edition von 1931 in Telugu-Schrift ist neben dem Text des Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa auch der Sanskrit-Kommentar Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇavyākhyāna (Abk.: DHNV) und eine Telugu-Erläuterung des Herausgebers beigegeben. Zudem enthält das Werk noch einen Zitatindex von 13 Seiten, so daß das Buch insgesamt stattliche 748 Druckseiten umfaßt. Der Umfang des Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇavyākhyāna übertrifft dabei den des Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa selbst bei weitem. Im Vorwort dieser Ausgabe äußert der Herausgeber sich nicht zu den der Edition zugrunde liegenden Manuskripten.
In der zweiten Edition von 1967 gab Pārthasārathi Bhaṭṭācārya das Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa zusammen mit dem Tātparyacintāmaṇi in zwei Bänden in Devanāgarī-Schrift heraus. Der Text dieser Ausgabe umfaßt 122 Druckseiten. Im Vorwort gibt Pārthasārathi Bhaṭṭācārya zu den dabei benutzten Manuskripten lediglich an, daß sie ihm sämtlich von Vaikhānasa-Familien zur Verfügung gestellt worden seien, und daß alle Manuskripte hinsichtlich der Fehler und Auslassungen identisch seien ("Introduction", S. v). Es ist davon auszugehen, daß er für diese Edition mindestens drei Handschriften konsultierte, die ihm drei Personen aus Andhra Pradesh (Ākuḷamannāḍu, Tirupati, Nallūru) überließen ("Introduction", S. viii). Da Pārthasārathi Bhaṭṭācārya seine Telugu-Edition des Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa von 1931 mit keinem Wort erwähnt, bleibt unklar, ob er ganz andere Manuskripte verwendete oder ob die textliche Basis beider Editionen identisch ist.

Daśavidhahetunirūpaṇa

     [maṅgalācaraṇam]

[1.1]     śrīmadvikhanasa mahāgurave namaḥ /
[1.2]     śrī śrīnivāsa parabrahmaṇe namaḥ //
[1.3-4]     śrī śrīnivāsamakhikṛte śrīvaikhānasagṛhyasūtratātparyacintāmaṇau daśavidhahetunirūpaṇam
[1.5]     vaikhānasakulodbhūtaṃ veṅkaṭeśārcanāratam /
[1.6]     vedāntadeśikaṃ vande śrīnivāsāryadīkṣitam //
[1.7]     śrīveṅkaṭeśam akhileśam anantam ādyaṃ kāruṇyavāridhim aśeṣasurais suvandyam /
[1.8]     vande samastajagatāṃ sthitisṛṣṭihetuṃ mānyān gurūṃś ca śataśo bhṛgukaśyapādīn //
[1.9]     śrutismṛtinadīpūrṇaṃ śāstrakallolasaṅkulam /
[1.10]     viṣṇubhaktyudakaṃ śuddhaṃ vande vaikhānasārṇavam //
[1.11]     yenānyakḷptasūtrāṇāṃ netraṃ nistimirīkṛtam /
[1.12]     sūtraṃ vaikhānasaṃ hy etat caturvargaphalapradam //
[1.13]     śrutismṛtītihāsādyaiḥ pratipāditavaibhavām /
[1.14]     paramātmaparāṃ vande sūtropaniṣadaṃ parām //

     [vyākhyānakartṛgotranāmādi]

[1.15]     śrīmatkauśikavaṃśyena govindācāryasūnunā /
[1.16]     śrīveṅkaṭeśapādābjasaparyāsu ratātmanā //
[1.17]     śrutismṛtipurāṇādisiddhamārgānuvartinā /
[1.18]     pūrvācāryaparikṣuṇṇasampradāyānuyāyinā //
[1.19]     vedāntācāryavaryeṇa śrīnivāsāryayajvanā /
[1.20]     vaikhānasasya sūtrasya vyākhyā samyak prakāśyate //



[vikhānasasūtrasya tadanuyāyināṃ ca sarvotkṛṣṭatve daśavidhahetūnāṃ nirdeśaḥ]

[2.1-3]     atha satyatvādisamastakalyāṇaguṇaviśiṣṭāt parabrahmaṇaḥ śrīmannārāyaṇād utpannena vikhanaśśabdavācyena caturmukhabrahmaṇā praṇītasya vaikhānasasūtrasya sarvasūtrottamatve tatsūtroktadharmānuṣṭhātṝṇāṃ sarvotkṛṣṭatamatve ca daśavidhahetavo nirūpyante.
[2.4]     yathā:
[2.5-9]     akhilajagatkāraṇabhūtena vikhanasā praṇītatvāt. sarvasūtrāṇām āditvāt. sarvakarmasu śrutimārgānusāritvāt. samantrakasarvakriyāpratipādakatvāt. niṣekasaṃskārādimatvāt. aṣṭādaśaśārīrasaṃskārapratipādakatvāt. sāṅgakriyākalāpavattvāt. manvādyaiḥ svīkṛtatvāt. akhilajagadekakāraṇabhūtaśrīmannārāyaṇaikaparatvāt. etatsūtroktadharmānuṣṭhānavatām eva bhagavatpriyatamatvopapatteś ca. iti.
[2.10-12]     ebhir hetubhir asya sūtrasya sarvasūtrottamatvaṃ etatsūtroktadharmānuṣṭhānād eva vaikhānasānāṃ sarvebhyaḥ śreṣṭhatamatvāñ ca śrutismṛtipurāṇādimukhena pratipādyate. tatrādau akhilajagatkāraṇabhūtena vikhanasā praṇītatvād iti hetur nirūpyate.
[2.13]     vikhanaśśabdārthanirṇayaḥ

     [nārāyaṇasya vikhano vaikhānasādiśabdavācyatvam]

[2.14]     vikhanā nāma kaścid ṛṣiḥ, uta nārāyaṇaḥ? nārāyaṇa eva kevalaṃ.
[2.15-16]     munimātrasya vaikhānasaśabdavācyatvena pratipādanābhāvāt. paramātmano nārāyaṇasya vikhano vaikhānasādiśabdavācyatvaṃ śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣv avagamyate. yathā:
[2.17]     khilaśrutau: "dhenur vahāṇām aditis surāṇāṃ brahmā ṛbhūṇāṃ vikhanā munīnām".
[2.18-19]     iti śruyate. ayam arthaḥ. vahānāṃ ataḍudādīnāṃ dhenuḥ utpattikāraṇam. surāṇāṃ indrādīnām aditiḥ. ṛbhūṇāṃ:
[2.20]     "sādhyā viśve ca vasavo maruto ṛbhavas tathā /
[2.21]     tathaivāṅgiraso rudrā ādityāś ca tathaiva ca /
[2.22]     ete devagaṇāś cāṣṭau manvantaragaṇeśvarāḥ //"
[2.23]     iti bhṛgūktānāṃ sādhyādīnāṃ brahmā. munīnāṃ muniśabdavācyānāṃ vikhanāḥ.
[2.24]     brahmaṇo muniśabdavācyatvaṃ bhārate cāvagamyate
[2.25]     "niśāṃ suptvātha bhagavān kṣapānte pratyabuddhyata / [MBh 13, App. 3.265]

[3.1]     paścād buddhvā sasarjāpaḥ tāsu vīryam avāsṛjat // [MBh 13, App. 3.266]
[3.2]     tad aṇḍam abhavad dhaimaṃ sahasrāṃśusamaprabham / [MBh 13, App. 3.267]
[3.3]     ahaṅkṛtyā tatas tasmin sasarja prabhur īśvaraḥ / [MBh 13, App. 3.268]
[3.4]     hiraṇyagarbhaṃ viśvātmā brahmāṇaṃ jalajaṃ munim //" iti [MBh 13, App. 3.269]
[3.5]     aṇḍabahutvābhiprāyeṇa munīnām iti bahuvacanam. yathā
[3.6]     "aṇḍānān tu sahasrāṇāṃ sahasrāṇy ayutāni ca /
[3.7]     īdṛśānām anantānāṃ koṭikoṭiśatāni ce//"ti smaraṇāt.
[3.8]     niśā cātra pralayaḥ, sā etāvatīti kutrāvagamyata iti cet.
[3.9]     mahābhārate: "caturyugasahasrāṇi caturyugaśatāni ca / [MBh 13, App. 3.261]
[3.10]     prāhuḥ kalpasahasran tu brāhmaṇās tattvadarśinaḥ / [MBh 13, App. 3.262]
[3.11]     daśakalpasahasrāṇi apy ayas sā mahāniśā //" iti. [MBh 13, App. 3.263]
[3.12-13]     anayā khilaśrutyā bhagavato vikhanaśśabdavācyatvaṃ katham avagamyata iti cet ucyate.

     [itihāsapurāṇābhyām eva vedārthasya nirṇeyatvam]

[3.14]     "durbodhā vaidikāś śabdā prakīrṇatvāc ca ye khilāḥ /
[3.15]     tadjñais ta eva spaṣṭārthāḥ smṛtitantre pratiṣṭhitāḥ //" iti
[3.16]     "yadi vidyāc caturvedān sāṅgopaniṣadān dvijaḥ /
[3.17]     na cet purāṇasadvidyā na vedārthavicakṣaṇaḥ //" iti
[3.18]     "itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ vedaṃ samupabṛhmayet /
[3.19]     bibhety alpaśruvād vedo mām ayaṃ pratariṣyati //" iti ca [MBh 1.1.204]
[3.20-21]     smaraṇāt itihāsapurāṇābhyām evārthanirṇayaḥ kartavyaḥ. bhārate mokṣadharme nāradastutau:
[3.22-23]     "namas te devadeveśa" ity ārabhya stotramadhye "phenapācārya vālakhilya vikhano vikhanasa vaikhānasācārya abhagnayoga abhagnaparisaṅkhyāna" iti.
[3.24]     tatraiva: "yat tasminn upalabhyaṃ te tat tejas tat trayīmayam /
[3.25]     tad vaikhānaḥ paraṃ brahma iti vedavido viduḥ //" iti coktam. [MBh ]



     [vikhanaśśabdanirvacanam]

[4.1-2] tathā nāmasahasrādhyāye "vaikhānas sāmagāyanaḥ"" iti smaryate.

     [jagatsṛṣṭiprayojanam]

[4.3]     pañcarātre ātmasaṃhitāyām:
[4.4]     "mahābhūtena bhūtena vyāptaṃ vikhanasā jagat /
[4.5]     tam eva śaraṇaṃ gaccha jagatkāraṇam acyutam //" [Ātmasaṃhitā]
[4.6]     iti śāṇḍilyena śatānandam abhilakṣyoktam.
[4.7]     vaikhānase ānandasaṃhitāyāṃ:
[4.8]     "vedāntatattvamīmāṃsākhananaṃ kṛtavāt hariḥ /
[4.9]     nāmnā vikhanasaṃ prāhur yañ ca vaikhānasaṃ tathā //" iti proktam. [ĀS ]
[4.10-12]     atra khananaśabdena saṅkalpa ucyate. "so 'kāmayata. bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa tapo 'tayata" ityādi śrutibhyaḥ. avāptasamastakāmasyāpi bhagavataḥ sṛṣṭikārye pravṛttir bhavati.

     [samaṣṭisṛṣṭilakṣaṇam]

[4.13]     nanu satyavādisamastakalyāṇaguṇaviśiṣṭasya bhagavataḥ.
[4.14]     "aiśvaryasya samagrasya vīryasya yaśasaḥ śriyaḥ /
[4.15]     jñānavairāgyayoś caiva ṣaṇṇāṃ bhaga itīraṇā //"
[4.16]     iti samagraṣāḍguṇyaparipūrṇasya avāptasamastakāmasya kimarthaṃ sṛṣṭyadikam iti cet ucyate.
[4.17]     "aprameyo 'niyojyaś ca yatra kāmagamo vaśī / [MBh 2, App. 21.1605]
[4.18]     modate bhagavān bhūtaiḥ bālaḥ kīḍanakair iva //" [MBh 2, App. 21.1606]
[4.19]     ityādi bhāratavacanānusāreṇa līlārtham eveti.
[4.20]     jagadsṛṣṭyādilīlānubhavārthaṃ bhagavatā samaṣṭisṛṣṭer anantaraṃ vyaṣṭisṛṣṭau
[4.21-22]     devamanuṣyādivividhaviśeṣasṛṣṭyarthaṃ caturmukhasṛṣṭiṃ prati dhyānaṃ kṛtam. eṣā cidacidātmikā sṛṣṭiḥ bhagavatā kriyate. vyaṣṭisṛṣṭis tu brahmaṇā. samaṣṭisṛṣṭir nāma:
[4.23]     "bhūtais tu pañcabhiḥ prāṇaiḥ svāntair daśabhir indriyaiḥ /
[4.24]     caturviṃśāti tattvāni sāṅkhyaśāstravido viduḥ //



[5.1]     mahān kālaḥ pradhānañ ca māyāvidyā ca pūruṣaḥ /
[5.2]     iti paurāṇikāḥ prāhuḥ triṃśattatvāni tais saha //"

     [vyaṣṭisṛṣṭilakṣaṇam]

[5.3-9]     iti vacanāt tattvasṛṣṭir ity avagamyate. "svāntair" ity anena "mano buddhir ahaṅkāraś cittañ ca karaṇāny amī" ity antaḥkaraṇacatuṣṭayam ucyate. vyaṣṭisṛṣṭir nāma: aṇḍāntarvartibhūtajātasṛṣṭiḥ. "ajām ekāṃ lohitaśuklakṛṣṇām" "nityo nityānām cetanaś cetanānām". ityādi śrutibhiḥ nityatvena śrutānāṃ prakṛtipuruṣānāṃ sṛṣṭir nāma pralayadaśāyāṃ sūkṣmarūpeṇa avibhaktanāmarūpeṇa ca paramātmany ekībhūtānāṃ sṛṣṭikāle paramātmano 'nupraveśānantaraṃ sthūlarūpavatvaṃ vibhaktanāmarūpabhāktvañ ca. "tat sṛṣṭvā". "tad evānuprāviśat. tad anupraviśya. sac ca tyac cābhavat" ityādi śruteḥ.
[5.10]     viṣṇupurāṇe: "tad etad akṣayaṃ nityaṃ jaganmunivarākhilam /
[5.11]     avirbhāvatirobhāvajanmanāśavikalpavat // [ViṣṇuP ]
[5.12]     prakṛtiṃ puruṣañ caiva praviśyātmecchayā hariḥ /
[5.13]     kṣobhayāmāsa samprāpte sargakāle vyayāpyayau //" iti [ViṣṇuP ]
[5.14]     gītāsu: "prakṛtiṃ puruṣam caiva viddhy anādī ubhāv api /" [BhGī = MBh 6.35.19ab]
[5.15]     mama yonir mahad brahma tasmin garbhaṃ dadhāmy aham /
[5.16]     sambhavas sarvabhūtānāṃ tato bhavati bhārata //" [BhGī = MBh 6.36.3]

     [aṇḍotpattyādiprakāraḥ]

[5.17-21]     iti coktarītyā sṛṣṭikāle jagadyonibhūtaṃ "mahabrahma" tadīyaṃ prakṛtyākhyam ācidvastu yat, tasmin cetanākhyaṃ garbhaṃ yojayati. tatkṛtāc cidacitsaṃsargāt devādisthāvarāntānām acinmiśrāṇāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ sambhavo bhavati. evam eva paramātmanā pañcīkṛtānāṃ bhūtānāṃ anyonyasaṃyogādinā aṇḍoptattyādikaṃ śrīviṣṇupurāṇe pratipādyate. yathā:
[5.22]     "ākāśavāyutejāṃsi salilaṃ pṛthivī tathā /
[5.23]     śabdādibhir guṇair bahmasaṃyuktāny uttarottaraiḥ // [ViṣṇuP 1.2.46]
[5.24]     śāntā ghorāś ca mūḍhāś ca viśeṣās tena te smṛtāḥ /
[5.25]     nānāvīryāḥ pṛthagbhūtāḥ tataḥ te saṃhatiṃ vinā // [ViṣṇuP ]




[6.1]     nāśaknuvan prajāḥ sraṣṭum asamāgamya kṛtsnaśaḥ /
[6.2]     sametyānyonyasaṃyogaṃ parasparasamāśrayāḥ // [Viṣṇu.P ]
[6.3]     ekasaṅghātalakṣyāś ca saṃprāpyaikyamaśeṣataḥ / [ViṣṇuP 1.2.49cd]
[6.4]     puruṣādhiṣṭhitatvāc cāpy avyaktānugraheṇa ca // [ViṣṇuP 1.2.50ab]
[6.5]     mahadādyā viśeṣāntā hy aṇḍam utpādayanti te /
[6.6]     tatkrameṇa prabuddhaṃ taj jalabudbudavatsamam /
[6.7]     bhūtebhyo 'ṇḍaṃ mahābuddhe pravṛddham udakeśayam /
[6.8]     prākṛtaṃ brahmarūpasya viṣṇoḥ sthānam anuttamam // [Viṣṇu.P 1.2.51]
[6.9]     tatrāvyaktasvarūpo 'sau vyaktarūpī jagatpatiḥ /
[6.10]     viṣṇur brahmasvarūpeṇa svayam eva vyavasthitaḥ //" [ViṣṇuP ]
[6.11]     ity ārabhya
[6.12]     "tasminn aṇḍe 'bhavad brahmā sadevāsuramānuṣaḥ //" [ViṣṇuP 1.2.54]
[6.13-14]     ityādibhiḥ samaṣṭisṛṣṭyādikam uktam. viśeṣeṇa vyaṣṭisṛṣṭāv api brahmaṇo 'ṇḍādiṣūtpattiprakāraḥ śrūyate. yathā:
[6.15-21]     mahopaniṣadi: "athāto mahopaniṣadaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ. eko ha vai nārāyaṇa āsīd" ity ārabhya "tasya dhyānāntassthasya yajñastomam ucyate. tasmin caturdaśapuruṣā jāyante. ekā kanyā. daśendriyāṇi mana ekādaśaṃ tejo dvādaśam ahaṅkāraḥ trayodaśaḥ praṇāś caturdaśaḥ ātmā pañcadaśaḥ buddhir bhūtāni pañca tanmātrāṇi pañca mahābhūtāni ca sa ekaḥ pañcaviṃśaḥ puruṣaḥ." "atha punar eva nārāyaṇas so 'nyatkāmo manasā dhyāyata tasya dhyānāntassthasya lalāṭāt svedo 'patat, ta imāḥ pratatā āpaḥ, tāsu tejaḥ, tat tejo hiraṇmayam aṇḍam tatra brahmā caturmukho 'jāyata." iti.

     [brahmaṇo 'ṇḍādiṣūtpattiprakāraḥ]

[6.22]     yajuṣi: "sa prajāpatir ekaḥ puṣkaraparṇe samabhavat" iti ca.
[6.23]     manau: evaṃ "apa eva sasarjādau tāsu vīryam avāsṛjat //" ity ārabhya [ManuDhŚ 1.8cd]
[6.24]     "tasmin jajñe svayaṃ brahmā sarvalokapitāmahaḥ //" iti [ManuDhŚ 1.9cd]





[7.1]     bhārate: "svapatas tasya devasya padmaṃ sūryasamaprabham /
[7.2]     nābhyāṃ vinissṛtam abhūt tatrotpannaḥ prajāpatiḥ //" iti ca smaryate. [MBh 3.194.11]
[7.3-4]     nanu nābhyām aṇḍe cotpattir ekasya katham upapadyata iti cet - tat kalpāntara iti vaktayam. taduktaṃ hayaśira upākhyāne:

     [ekasya brahmaṇaḥ nābhyām aṇḍe ca utpattiḥ]

[7.5]     "tvatto me mānasaṃ janma prathamaṃ dvijapūjitam /
[7.6]     cākṣuṣaṃ vai dvitīyaṃ me āsīj janma purātanam //
[7.7]     tvatprasādāc ca me janma tṛtīyaṃ vācikaṃ mahat /
[7.8]     tvatto me śrāvaṇañ cāpi caturthaṃ janma vai prabho //
[7.9]     nāsikyañ caiva me janma tvattaḥ pañcamam ucyate /
[7.10]     aṇḍajañ cāpi me janma tvattaḥ ṣaṣṭhaṃ vinirmittam //
[7.11]     idan tu saptamaṃ janma padmajaṃ me 'mitaprabha /" iti.

     [caturmukhasya vaikhānasādiśabdavācyatvam]

[7.12-14]     atas samastajagajjanmasthitidhvaṃsamahānandaikahetoḥ bhagavataḥ parabrahmaṇo nārāyaṇasya vaikhānasādiśabdavācyatvasambhavāt tannābhinalinasañjātasya brahmaṇo 'pi "aṅgād aṅgād" iti mantroktaprakāreṇa bhāratādipratipāditarītyā ca vaikhānasādiśabdavācyatvam upapadyate.
[7.15]     śāntiparvaṇi: "viśeṣeṇākhanat yasmāt bhāvanāmunisṛṣṭaye /
[7.16]     tasmād vikhanaso nāma sa āsīd aṇḍajaḥ priyaḥ //" iti [MBh ]
[7.17]     tatraiva: "sraṣṭuṃ sa tu samudyukto brahmayonimayaḥ prabhuḥ /
[7.18]     khanitvā cātmanātmānaṃ dharmādiguṇasaṃyutam /
[7.19]     dhyānam āviśya yogena hy āsīd vikhanaso muniḥ //" iti [MBh ]
[7.20-21]     śrībhāgavate: "na khalu gopikānandano bhavān akhiladehinām antarātmadṛk /
[7.22-23]     vikhanasārthito viśvaguptaye sakha udeyivān sāttvatāṃ kule //" iti [BhāgavataP 10.31.4]

     [śrīraṅge vaikhānasārcanam]

[7.24]     gārūḍe - śrīraṅgamāhātmye:
[7.25]     "brahmāpi divyahaṃsena sitameghopamena ca /
[7.26]     pṛṣṭhato 'nuyayau viṣṇuṃ vastreṇocchādya cānanam //




[8.1]     tatrārcako mahābhāgo bhagavān vikhanās tadā /
[8.2]     dadau prasādaṃ devānāṃ raṅganāthābhyanujñayā //" iti [GaruḍaP ]
[8.3]     śrīvaikhānase - ānandasaṃhitāyām:
[8.4]     "antarhitānāṃ khananād vedānān tu viśeṣataḥ /
[8.5]     sa vibhuḥ procyate sarvaiḥ vikhanā brahmavādibhiḥ /
[8.6]     vaikhānasaś ca bhagavān procyate sa pitāmahaḥ //" iti [ĀS ]
[8.7]     vyāsanighaṇṭau: "vikhanasañ ca vidhātāraṃ viriñca taṃ caturmukham /" iti
[8.8]     "nābhijanmāṇḍajaḥ pūrvo vikhanāḥ kamalāsanaḥ //
[8.9]     śatānandaś śatadhṛtis satyako haṃsavāhanaḥ /
[8.10]     padmāsano vikhanasaś cāharmukhaḥ itīritaḥ //" iti ca pratipāditam.
[8.11-12]     evaṃ kāryakāraṇayor abhedāvagamāt pramāṇabāhulyāc ca bhagavati nārāyaṇe caturmukhe ca vaikhānasaśabdaprayogaprakāraḥ pratipāditaḥ.
[8.13]     vaikhānasānām utpattiprakāraḥ

     [śrutyuktaḥ vaikhānasānām utpattiprakāraḥ]

[8.14-23]     vaikhānasānām utpattiḥ viśeṣeṇa śrūyate. yajuṣi āruṇaketuke iṣṭakopadhānakathanānuvāke sṛṣṭiprakaraṇe - "āpo vā idam āsan salilam eva. sa prajāpatir ekaḥ puṣkaraparṇe samabhavat. tasyāntar manasi kāmas samavartata. idaṃ sṛjeyam iti" ity ārabhya "sa tapas taptvā. śarīram adhūnuta. tasya yan māṃsam āsīt. tato 'ruṇāḥ ketavo vātaraśanā ṛṣaya udatiṣṭhan. ye 'nakhāḥ te vaikhānasāḥ. ye vālāḥ te vālakhilyāḥ." iti. asyārthaḥ. samaṣṭisṛṣṭer anantaraṃ vyaṣṭisṛṣṭau caturmukhaḥ devamanuṣyādivividhaviśeṣasṛṣṭyarthaṃ matsyādirūpeṇāvatariṣyamāṇasya bhagavato nārāyaṇasya paramavaidikatvena sampratipannaśrīvaikhānasabhagavacchāstramārgeṇa samārādhdanarthañ ca svātmatulyāḥ prajās sambhaveyur iti svāntaryāmiṇaṃ paramātmānaṃ dhyonenānukṛtavān ayam evārtho brāhmāṇḍe 'py ucyate
[8.24]     "om ity ekākṣaraṃ brahma vyāharan saṃsmaran harim /
[8.25]     padmāsanastho bhagavān paramaṃ tapa āsthitaḥ //" [BrahmāṇḍaP ]




     [sanakādisṛṣṭiprakāraḥ]

[9.1-5]     ity ārabhya brahmaṇā brahuśaḥ kṛtaṃ tapaścaraṇam uktam. tapaścaraṇakāle sākṣātkṛtabhagavatsvarūpavaibhavānubhavātiśayāt bhagavaddattasṛṣṭiśaktilābhāt tadupajanitaviśeṣavegāc ca pulakitasarvāṅgaḥ śarīram adhūnuta - kampam akarot. "tasya yan māṃsam āsīd" māṃsaṃ mānasam iti yāvat. "arthāt prakaraṇāl liṅgād aucityād arthanirṇayaḥ" ity arthādibhiḥ samīcīnārthanirṇayavidhānāt "akṣarasāmyān nirbrūyād" iti niruktavidhānāñ ca.
[9.6-10]     tathā ca tasya manaḥ paramātmani saṃsaktam āsīd iti yat, tena hetunā tadanugrahas samajani. tenānugṛhītāt brahmaṇaḥ "ketavo vātaraśanāḥ ṛṣayaḥ udatiṣṭhan". "aruṇāḥ" paramātmani vasantaḥ taditararaviktāḥ "ketavaḥ" ucchritasvabhāvāḥ paramātmapravaṇānām agresarāḥ "vātaraśanā" digvāsasaḥ "ṛṣayaḥ" sarvārthadarśinaḥ sanakādayaḥ "udatiṣṭhan" utkṛṣya samabhavan iti.
[9.11]     idaṃ viṣṇupurāṇe 'pi: "sanandanādayo ye ca pūrvaṃ sṛṣṭās tu vedhasā /
[9.12]     na te lokeṣv asajjanta nirapekṣāḥ prajāvidhau // [ViṣṇuP 1.7.9]
[9.13]     sarve te yogino jātā vītarāgā vimatsarāḥ /
[9.14]     teṣv evaṃ nirapekṣeṣu lokasṛṣṭau mahātmanaḥ //" ityādinā pratipāditam. [ViṣṇuP 1.7.10]
[9.15-19]     sa prajāpatiḥ evaṃvidhān svakāryāsādhakān tān dṛṣṭvā kiñcid viṣādam āpannaḥ punar api svakāraṇaṃ bhagavantaṃ dhyānaprayāyeṇa khananenātoṣat. "ye nakhā" ityādi. bhagavadanugrahavikasite prajāpater manasi vaikhānasā nāma ṛṣayas sambhūtāḥ atra "ye nakhā" ity atra ādyantavarṇaviparyayo bhavati. "kaśyapaḥ paśyako bhavatī"tivat "khanā ity etat nakhā" iti viparyastam iti yāvat.
[9.20]     "suptiṅupagrahaliṅganarāṇāṃ kālahalacsvarakartṛyaṅañ ca /
[9.21]     vyatyayam icchiti śāstrakṛd eṣāṃ so 'pi ca siddhyati bāhulakena //"
[9.22-24]     iti, "bahulaṃ chandasī"ti cātra praṇāman. atra "anakhā" iti cchittvā kecid evam ūcuḥ. anakhā ity anena saumyendriyavatvaṃ uktam iti.





     [vaikhānasānām ācāryapuruṣatvam]

[10.1-3]     evañ ca sati "saumyaṃ jitendriyaṃ" "suprasannendriyaṃ" ityādinā bhagavacchāstreṣv ācāryalakṣaṇasya pratipāditatvāt "vaikhānasa vikhanasācarya" iti. viṣṇor ācāryatvena śāntyparvaṇy abhihitatvāt.
[10.4]     "vikhanā iti viṣṇus tajjā vaikhānasāḥ smṛtāḥ / [KrA 36.28cd]
[10.5]     viṣṇor eva samutpannā bhṛgvādyā munayas tathā //"

     [vaikhānasānām triśuklatvam]

[10.6-7]     iti vacanāt, "guros sānavṛttir vaikhānasa" iti bodhāyanasūtre uktatvāc ca bhāgavatādiṣu pratipāditam "ācāryapuṃstvam eteṣāṃ vaikhānasānām eve"ty avagamyate.
[10.8-9]     yadvā "anaghā" iti pāṭhaḥ. anena triśuklatvaṃ sūcyate. janma vidyā karma ceti. advārakatvena bhagavataḥ caturmukhāc coptattiśravaṇāt,
[10.10]     "tatkarma yan na bandhāya sā vidyā yā vimuktaye /
[10.11]     āyāsāyāparaṃ karma vidyānyā śilpanaipuṇam //"
[10.12-13]     ity uktarītyā advārakabhagavatsvarūpajñānatadārādhanavidhipratipādakaśāstraniṣṭhatvena ca eṣāṃ triśuklatvam. śuklavatām evādhikyaṃ āraṇyaparvaṇi prathamādhyāye pratipāditam. yathā:
[10.14]     "yeṣāṃ trīṇy avadātāni yonirvidyā ca karma ca /
[10.15]     te sevyās tais samāsyā hi śāstrebhyo 'pi garīyasī //" ti [MBh 3.1.25]

     [ānandasaṃhitānusāreṇa vaikhānasotpattyādikam]

[10.16]     śrīvaikhānase ānandasaṃhitāyāṃ vikhanasotpattyādikaṃ pratipāditam:
[10.17]     "atha sasmāra bhagavān viśvasṛṣṭyartham acyutaḥ /
[10.18]     dhātāraṃ viśvanirmāṇacaturaṃ caturānanam // [ĀS 4.6]
[10.19]     smaraṇānantarād eva prādur āsīt puraḥ prabhoḥ /
[10.20]     dhātā samastajagatām utpattikaraṇakṣamaḥ // [Ā.S 4.7]
[10.21]     taṃ prāha bhagavān viṣṇuḥ praṇataṃ purataḥ sthitam /
[10.22] śrībhagavān uvāca: brahman tvayā jagat sarvaṃ kartavyaṃ sacarācaram // [ĀS 4.8]
[10.23]     loke vihartum icchāmi yad ahaṃ padmasambhava /
[10.24]     tatas tvatsṛṣṭajagatām avicchinnapravṛttaye /



[11.1]     dharmasaṃrakṣaṇārthāya vedaśāstrārthasiddhaye // [ĀS 4.9]
[11.2]     alasā alpasattvāś ca manuṣyās svalpabuddhayaḥ /
[11.3]     te paravyūhavibhavān ātmānāñ ca na menire // [ĀS 4.10]

     [ānandasaṃhitānusāreṇa sanakādisṛṣṭiḥ]

[11.4]     saulabhyāya tu bhaktānāṃ sarvalokānukampayā // [ĀS 4.11cd]
[11.5]     arcāvatārarūpeṇa loke 'smiṃś caturānana /
[11.6]     avatāraṃ kariṣyāmi mahyā lakṣmyā samanvitaḥ // [Ā.S 4.12]
[11.7]     madarcāyai sṛja brahman sṛṣṭyādau munisattamaṃ / [ĀS 4.13ab]
[11.8]     ity ājñaptas tadā brahmā muhūrtaṃ tat sisṛkṣayā /
[11.9]     cintayāmāsa tatkarmā kṣaṇam ekaṃ mahāmuniḥ // [ĀS 4.14]
[11.10]     ūcuḥ na śaknuyām evaṃ sraṣṭum icchan tathāvidham /
[11.11]     tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā devadevo haris svayam // [Ā.S ]
[11.12]     cintayāmāsa deveśaḥ svanirmalatarātmani /
[11.13]     vedāntatattvamīmāṃsā khananaṃ kṛtavān hariḥ // [ĀS 4.15]
[11.14]     nāmnā vikhanasaṃ cakre tatpadānvarthayogataḥ /
[11.15]     tathā cintayatas tasya manaso dvau babhūvatuḥ // [ĀS 4.18]
[11.16]     saṅkalpadharmau sannamya prāñjaliṃ purataḥ sthitam / [ĀS 4.19ab?]
[11.17]     brahmāṇam abravīd viṣṇur bhūtasṛṣṭyantahetave (kārakaṃ) /
[11.18]     saṅkalpadharmau bhavatas tava sṛṣṭyantahetave //
[11.19]     śuddhasattvasamutpanno nirmito 'yaṃ tavāgrataḥ // [ĀS 4.35cd]
[11.20]     muniśreṣṭho mahātejā matkāryakaraṇakṣamaḥ / [ĀS 4.36ab?]
[11.21]     matkāryasādhakān eva tvaṃ vai sraṣṭum athārhasi //
[11.22]     hṛṣīkeśasya tadvākyaṃ bhyādhāya kṛtañjaliḥ /
[11.23]     caturmukhaś cāpi tathā sanakādimunīśvarān /
[11.24]     dhyāyan mukhaiś caturbhis tu kramād asṛjad abjabhūḥ //




     [ānandasaṃhitānusāreṇa dakṣādimunidaśakasṛṣṭiḥ]

[12.1]     sanatkumārañ ca tathā sanakañ ca sanātanam /

     [ānandasaṃhitānusāreṇa vaikhānasasya muniśreṣṭhatvam]

[17.1]     (bhṛg ity eva bhṛguḥ pūrvam aṅgārebhyo 'ṅgirābhavat // [MB.h 13.85.15cd]

[19.1]     tat pratīkṣya sa parṇena saṃjuhāva vibhāv asau /
[19.2]     tato 'rciṣo 'bhūd bhagavān bhṛgur aṅgārato 'ṅgirāḥ //
[19.3]     atraivānveṣaṇād atriḥ khananād vikhanā muniḥ /
[19.4]     khananaṃ tattvamīmāṃsety bis hier teluguāhuḥ kecana sūrayaḥ //
[19.5]     apare nigamārthānāṃ khananād iti naśśrutam /
[19.6]     tatas tadvaṃśajā viprā vedavedāṅgavedinaḥ //" iti.
[19.7-10]     "ye vālāḥ te vālakhilyāḥ" ity atra bakārasthāne vakāra. jñānātiśayavaibhavāt kāmādidoṣarāhityena ca bālā ucyante. śrūyate hi: "tasmād brāhmaṇaḥ pāṇḍityaṃ nirvidya bālyena tiṣṭhāset bālyañ ca pāṇdityañ ca nirvidyātha muniḥ" iti.
[19.11-13]     atra kecid evam ūcuḥ: brahmaṇaḥ vidhūtāc charīrāt yanmāṃsaṃ vikīrṇam abhavat tato ketavo vātaraśanā ṛṣaya udatiṣṭhann iti. tad asat. evam arthasvīkāre sṛṣṭikāraṇabhūtasya brahmaśarīrasya śaithilyam uktaṃ syād iti.
[19.14-20]     kiñ ca "tasyāntarmanasi kāmas samavartata" ityādinā "kāmas tadagre samavartatādhi" ity antena sopapattikaṃ vartamānaṃ saṅkalparūpaṃ mananavyāpāram uktvā "manaso retaḥ prathamaṃ yad āsīd" ity atra tatra vidyamānasya vyāpārasya prajāpateḥ sṛṣṭikāraṇatvaṃ retaś śabdebis hier telugunoktvā "sato bandhum asati niravindann" ity ārabhya "ya evaṃ veda" ity antena brahmaṇas tatkālavidyamānamānasaśaktimāab hier telugutreṇa vyaṣṭisṛṣṭer aniṣpannatvam uktvā manaso vyaṣṭikāraṇalābhāya "sa tapo 'tapyata" iti bhagavadupāsanam akarod" ity uktam. ayam evārthaḥ "oṃ ity ekākṣaraṃ brahme"tyādinā brahmāṇḍe 'py uktam.

     [bhrgvādīnāṃ bhagavanmānasaputratvam]

[19.21]     bhagavanmānasaputrā bhṛgvādaya iti bhagavataivoktam:
[19.22]     "maharṣayas sapta pūrve catvāro manavas tathā /
[19.23]     madbhāvā mānasā jātā yeṣāṃ loka imāḥ prajāḥ //" [MBh 6.32.6]

     [bhṛgvādīnāṃ vaikhānasavaṃśakartṛtvam]

[19.24]     bhṛgvādaya eva vaikhānasānāṃ vaṃśakartāraḥ iti bhārate 'py uktam.




[20.1]     yathā śāntiparvaṇi:
[20.2]     "bhṛgvaṅgiromarīcyatri pulastyapulahāḥ kratuḥ / [MBh 13, App. 7.49]
[20.3]     tathā vasiṣṭho dakṣaś ca nava svāyambhuvā dvijāḥ //
[20.4]     ete vaikhānasānān tu ṛṣīṇāṃ bhāvitātmanāṃ /
[20.5]     vaṃśakartāra ucyante sāttvikāhārabhojinām //" iti [MBh ]
[20.6-8]     tasmād bhagavatā nārāyaṇena brahmaṇā ca sṛṣṭānāṃ bhṛgvādīnām ṛṣīṇāṃ tadvaṃśajānāṃ ca niṣekādikriyāvatām advārakabhagavadyajanādhikāravatām eva loke vaikhānasā iti prasiddhiḥ.

     [caturmukhasṛṣṭānāṃ sarveṣāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ vaikhānasatvaṃ samānam ity ākṣepasya parihāraḥ]

[20.9]     nanu brahmaṇā sṛṣṭānāṃ sarveṣām api manuṣyānāṃ vaikhānasatvaṃ samānam.
[20.10-11]     katham eteṣv eva vyavahriyate iti cet satyam. nāmarūbis hier telugupakṛtyavibhāgādikaṃ vedaśabdebhya eva brahmaṇā kṛtam iti śrūyate. "vedena nāmarūpe vyākarot satāsatī prajāpatir" iti.
[20.12]     tathā bhārate: "anādinidhanā hy eṣā vāgudsṛṣṭā svayambhuvā // [MBh 12.224.55cd]
[20.13]     ādau vedamayī divyā yatas sarvāḥ prasūtayaḥ //" iti [MBh 12.671.1]
[20.14]     śrīviṣṇupurāṇe: "nāma rupañ ca bhūtānāṃ kṛtyānāñ ca praab hier telugupañcanam /
[20.15]     vedaśabdebhya evādau devādīnāṃ cakāra saḥ //" iti. [ViṣṇuP 1.5.63]
[20.16]     manu: "sarveṣāñ ca sa nāmāni karmāṇi ca pṛthak pṛthak /
[20.17]     vedaśabdebhya evādau pṛthak saṃsthāś ca nirmame //" [ManuDhŚ 1.21]
[20.18-19]     iti ca nāmarūpavibhāgasya śrutismṛtiṣu pratipāditatvāt brahmaṇā tādṛśaśrutismṛtyanusāreṇa sṛṣṭānām eva vaikhānasatvavyavahāraḥ. Nānyeṣām.
[20.20-23]     kiñca ekasmin paramapuruṣe mukhādiṣu jātānāṃ yathā brāhmaṇādivyavahāraḥ yathā viśvāmitra bhāradvājādi gotreṣūtpannānām ekasūtraniṣṭhatvaṃ vinā anekasūtrānusāritvaṃ, yathā ca kumudakahlārādiṣu "paṅke jāyata" iti vyutpattyā paṅkajatve samāno 'pi yogarūḍhibhyāṃ paṅkajatvaṃ tāmarasa eva vartate tathaiva vaikhānasatvam api. tathoktam:
[20.24]     "kalpe kalpe kṣayotpattyā brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ /
[20.25]     śrutismṛtisadācāra- nirṇetāras tu sarvadā //




[21.1]     na kāścid vedakartā 'sti vedavaktā caturmukhaḥ /
[21.2]     tathaiva dharmaṃ smarati manuḥ kalpāntarāntare //"

     [tṛtīyāśramaniṣṭhānāṃ na naisargikaṃ vaikhānasatvam]

[21.2-6] nanu: "brahmacārī gṛhasthaś ca bhikṣur vaikhānasas tathā" iti tatra tatra tṛtīyāśramaniṣṭhānām eva vaikhānasatvāvagamāt ta eva vaikhānasaśabdavācyāḥ kiṃ na syur iti cet na. śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣu uktaprakāreṇa brahmaṇā sṛṣṭānām eva vaikhānasatvāvagamāt teṣām eva tatra tatrotkṛṣṭatvapratipādanāc ca.

     [vaikhānasānāṃ brahmasabhāpraveśaḥ]

[21.7-8]     tathā hi: śrutāv eva vaikhānasānām utpattiḥ śrūyate. "ye nakhāḥ te vaikhānasāḥ" iti. chandogyabrāhmaṇe: "vaikhānasā vā ṛṣaya indrasya priyā āsan"
[21.9-11]     "pauruhan mahaṃ bhavati. puruhānnādo vā etena vaikhānaso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat" iti. atra indraśabdena paramātmā nārāyaṇa ucyate. "sa brahmā sa śivassendrasso 'kṣaraḥ paramas svarāṭ" ityādi śrutibhyaḥ.
[21.12]     "āśvatthaḥ kapilā gāvas tulasī vikhanās tathā /
[21.13]     catvāro matpriyā rājaṃs teṣāṃ vaikhānaso varaḥ //" [ĀS 19.10]
[21.14]     ity upabrahmaṇāt. brahmasūtre indraprāṇādhikaraṇe tathā nirṇayāc ca.
[21.15]     ānuśāsanike: "tathāgnes tasya bhasmabhyo brahmarṣigaṇasamimtāḥ /
[21.16]     vaikhānasās samutpannās tapaśśrutaguṇepsavaḥ//" [MBh 13.85.18]
[21.17]     iti vaikhānasanāmnaivotpattipratipādanāt.
[21.18]     tathā kiṣkindhākāṇḍe:
[21.19]     "śṛṅgaṃ saumanasaṃ nāma jātarūpamayaṃ dhruvam // [Rā.m 4.39.51cd]
[21.20]     tatra pūrvaṃ padaṃ kṛtvā purā viṣṇus trivikrame /
[21.21]     dvitīyaṃ śikhare raudraṃ cakāra puruṣottamaḥ // [Rā.m 4.39.52]
[21.22]     taduttare pratikramya jambūdvīpaṃ divākaraḥ /
[21.23]     dṛśyo bhavati bhūyiṣṭhaṃ śikharaṃ tan mahocchrayam // [Rā.m 4.39.53]
[21.24]     tatra vaikhānasā nāma vālakhilyā maharṣayaḥ /
[21.25]     prakāśamānā dṛśyante sūryavarṇās tapasvinaḥ //" iti [Rām 4.39.54]





[22.1]     tatraiva catvāriṃśe 'dhyāye:
[22.2]     mainākaś ca vicetavyas sasānuprasthakandaraḥ /
[22.3]     strīṇām aśvamukhīnāñ ca niketās tatra tatra tu // [Rā.m 4.42.30]
[22.4]     taṃ deśaṃ samatikramya āśramaṃ siddhasevitam /
[22.5]     siddhā vaikhānasās tatra vālakhilyāś ca tāpasāḥ // [Rā.m 4.42.31]
[22.6]     vandyās te tu tapassiddhās tapasā vītakalmaṣāḥ /
[22.7]     praṣṭavyā cāpi sītāyāḥ pravṛttir vināyānvitaḥ // [Rā.m 4.42.32]
[22.8]     hemapuṣkarasañchannaṃ tatra vaikhānasaṃ saraḥ /" [Rām 4.42.33ab]
[22.9]     iti ca vānaprasthaparatvaṃ vinā "vaikhānasā vālakhilyā" iti vālakhilyasamānatayā pṛthag vaṃśatvena kīrtanāt.
[22.11]     tathā śrīviṣṇupurāṇe - dvitīṃyāṃśe navame 'dhyāye:
[22.12]     "tataḥ prayāti bhagavān brāhmaṇair abhirakṣitaḥ /
[22.13]     vālakhilyādibhiś caiva prabhur vaikhānasair api // [ViṣṇuP 2.8.58]
[22.14]     mahātmābhir mahātmā vai jagatāṃ pālanodyataḥ //" iti [ViṣṇuP ]
[22.15]     tathā sabhāparvaṇi:
[22.16]     pitāmahasya bhavanaṃ jagmuś ca kṛpayānvitāḥ // [MBh 1.203.2cd]
[22.17]     tato dadṛśur ātmānaṃ saha devaiḥ pitāmaham /
[22.18]     siddhair maharṣibhiś caiva samantāt parivāritam // [MBh 1.203.3]
[22.19]     tatra viṣṇur mahādevas tatrāgnir vāyunā saha /
[22.20]     candrādityau ca dharmaś ca parameṣṭhī tathā budhāḥ // [MBh 1.203.4]
[22.21]     vaikhānasā vālakhilyās somapāś ca marīcipāḥ /
[22.22]     ajāś caivājamīḍhāś ca tejogarbhās tapasvinaḥ /
[22.23]     ṛṣayas sarva eveti pitāmaham upāsate //" [MBh 1.203.5]
[22.24-25]     iti ca vaikhānasānāṃ brahmasabhāpraveśavarṇanāt. tasya ca tṛtīyāśramaniṣṭheṣv asambhavāt.





     [vānaprasthānāṃ śrautakarmaniṣedhaḥ]

[23.1]     ānuśāsanike
[23.2]     "śṛṇu rājan vasiṣṭhasya mukhyaṃ karma yaśasvinaḥ / [MBh 13.140.15cd]
[23.3]     vaikhānasavidhānena gaṅgātīraṃ samāśritāḥ // [MBh 13.140.647*.1]
[23.4]     ādityās satramīhanti saro vaikhānasaṃ prati //" iti [MBh 13.140.16]
[23.5-7]     atra vānaprasthavidhau satrayāgakramavidhānābhāvāt vānaprasthāśramapraviṣṭhānāṃ tena śārīreṇa punar api devatvayogyatā 'sambhavāc ca vaikhānasavidhāneneti vaikhānasapadena vānaprasthānāṃ gṛhītum aśakyatvāt.
[23.8]     kiñca śrībhāgavate ekādaśaskandhe:
[23.9]     "vanyaiś carupuroḍāśair nirvapet kālacoditām /
[23.10]     na tu śrautena vidhinā māṃ yajeta vanāśramī //" [BhāgavataP 11.18.7]
[23.11]     iti vānaprasthānāṃ śarutavidhiniṣedhapratipādanāt.

     [bhagavadarcanakramaḥ]

[23.12]     tathā vṛddhamanau: "vedāntavedibhir viprais tadvaikhānasasūtribhiḥ /
[23.13]     yājayed yajñapuruṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ rājā jagaddhitaḥ //" iti

     [vaikhānasapāñcarātrikayoḥ caturmūrtiṣu saṃjñāyāṃ vaiṣamyam]

[23.14]     tathā āśvamedhike:
[23.15]     yudhiṣṭhirah: "kathaṃ tvaṃ arcanīyo 'si mūrtayaḥ kīdṛśāś ca te / [MBh 14, App. 4.1652]
[23.16]     vaikhānasāḥ kathaṃ brūyuḥ kathaṃ vā pāñcarātrikāḥ // [MB.h 14, App. 4.1653]
[23.17]     śrībhagavān: "śṛṇu pāṇḍava tatsarvam arcanākramam ātmanaḥ / [MBh 14, App. 4.1654]
[23.18]     sthaṇḍile padmakaṃ kṛtvā sāṣṭapatraṃ sakarṇikam // [MB.h 14, App. 4.1655]
[23.19]     aṣṭākṣaravidhānena athavā dvādaśākṣaraiḥ / [MBh 14, App. 4.1656]
[23.20]     vaidikair athavā mantrair mama sūktena vā punaḥ // [MB.h 14, App. 4.1657]
[23.21]     sthitaṃ māṃ mantratas tasmin arcayet susamahitaḥ / [MBh 14, App. 4.1658]
[23.22]     viṣṇuñ ca puruṣaṃ satyam acyutañ ca yudhiṣṭhira // [MB.h 14, App. 4.1659]
[23.23]     aniruddhañ ca māṃ prāhur vaikhānasavido janāḥ / [MBh 14, App. 4.1660]
[23.24]     anye tv evaṃ vijānānti māṃ rājan pāñcarātrikāḥ // [MB.h 14, App. 4.1661]






[24.1]     vāsudevañ ca rājendra saṅkarṣaṇam athāpi vā / [MBh 14, App. 4.1662]
[24.2]     pradyumnañ cāniruddhañ ca caturmūrtiṃ pracakṣate // [MBh 14, App. 4.1663]
[24.3]     etāś cānyāś ca rājendra saṃjñābhedena mūrtayaḥ / [MBh 14, App. 4.1664]
[24.4]     viddhy anarthāntarā eva mām evañ cārcayed budhaḥ //" iti [MBh 14, App. 4.1665]
[24.5]     tathā pāñcarātre pauṣkarasaṃhitāyām:
[24.6]     "viprā vaikhānasākhyā ye te bhaktās tattvam ucyate // [PauṣkaraS 36.260cd]
[24.7]     ekantinas susattvasthā dehāntaṃ nānyayājinaḥ /
[24.8]     kartavyam iti deveśaṃ saṃyajante phalaṃ vinā //" iti [PauṣkaraS 36.261]

     [śuddha, vaidika, tāntrikabhedena pūjātraividhyam]

[24.9]     tathā tatraiva tantrabhedanirṇaye:
[24.10]     "śuddhañ ca vaidikañ ceti tāntrikañ ca tridhā bhavet /
[24.11]     pāñcarātreṇa pūjā tu śuddhaṃ viṣṇor iti smṛtam // [PauṣkaraS ]

     [vaikhānasapūjāyāḥ vaidikatvaṃ]

[24.12]     vaikhānasena sūtreṇa pūjayed viṣṇum avyayam /
[24.13]     vaidikaṃ tad iti proktaṃ dvijātīnāṃ praśasyate //" iti [PauṣkaraS ]
[24.14]     tathā viṣṇusmṛtau:
[24.15]     "pauruṣaṃ sūktam āsthāya ye yajanti dvijottamāḥ /
[24.16]     saṃhitājapamāsthāya te māṃ prāpsyanti vai dvijāḥ //
[24.17]     alābhe vedamantrāṇāṃ pāñcarātroditena vā //" iti
[24.18]     tathā saṅkarṣaṇasaṃhitāyām:
[24.19]     "pūjayet pañcarātrais tu mantrair mokṣaphalapradaiḥ /
[24.20]     vaikhānasoktair divyair vā mantrais sarvārthasiddhaye //" iti [Saṅkarṣaṇasaṃhitā]
[24.21]     tathā śilpe hariharādīnāṃ sthānanirṇaye:
[24.22]     "sahasraviprāvāseṣu śataviprādhikeṣu ca /
[24.23]     pañcamūrtividhānena madhye viṣṇuṃ samarcayet //
[24.24]     tadvāstvaṅgālaye viṣṇuṃ tāntrikeṇa na cārcayet /
[24.25]     arcayed vaidikoktena vaikhānasavidhānataḥ //" iti





     [vaiṣṇavasamayasya traividhyam]

[25.1]     tathā jyautiṣe hayagrīvasaṃhitāyām:
[25.2]     "śrīśāstreṇaiva kartavyaṃ grāmamadhyālayārcanam /
[25.3]     pāñcarātravidhānena nācared iti śāsanam //" iti [Hayagrīvasaṃhitā]
[25.4]     tathā śaive ca suprabhede:
[25.5]     "sahasrabhūsurād ūrdhve grāme brahmāṅkaṇe 'pi ca /
[25.6]     vaikhānasena sūtreṇa niṣekādisusaṃskṛtaiḥ // [SuprabhedĀ ]
[25.7]     bhārgavādimahātantramantrabhedavicakṣaṇaiḥ /
[25.8]     anuddhṛtair mantragaṇair vedavedāntasambhavaiḥ // [SuprabhedĀ ]
[25.9]     kramādhyayanasampannais sāṅgopāṅgaiś ca saṃskṛtaiḥ /
[25.10]     pañcamūrtiprakāreṇa pratiṣṭhāpyārcayed dharim // [Suprabhed.Ā ]
[25.11]     vaidikaṃ tad iti proktaṃ rājarāṣṭravivardhanam //" iti. [SuprabedhĀ ]
[25.12]     tathā kāraṇe grāmavinyāsavidhau:
[25.13]     "brahmāṃśaṃ tu caturbhāgaṃ kṛtvā vāyavyabhāgataḥ /
[25.14]     pañcamūrtikrameṇaiva viṣṇuṃ saṃsthāpya pūjayet //" iti [SuprabhedĀ ]
[25.15]     tathā bhīmasaṃhitāyām samayabhedopanyāsāvasare:
[25.16]     "śaivam evaṃ samākhyātaṃ vaiṣṇavan tv adhunocyate /
[25.17]     vaiṣṇavañ ca tridhā proktaṃ tathā samayabhedavat // [Bhīmasaṃhitā]
[25.18]     pāñcarātraṃ bhāgavataṃ tathā vaikhānasaṃ matam /
[25.19]     śuddhaṃ miśraṃ tathā saumyaṃ yathā saṃkhyakrameṇa tu // [Bhīmasaṃhitā]
[25.20]     vaidikācārabāhyaṃ yat tadraudram iti kīrtitam /
[25.21]     vaidikācārasambandhāt saumyaṃ śreṣṭham udāhṛtam // [Bhīmasaṃhitā]
[25.22]     grāmādīnāṃ samīpe tu miśroktaṃ sthāpayed budhaḥ /
[25.23]     abdhinadyāditīreṣu śuddhoktaṃ sthāpayet tathā // [Bhīmasaṃhitā]
[25.24]     viprāvāseṣu sarveṣu saumyoktenaiva kārayet //" iti [Bhīmasaṃhitā]





[26.1]     tathā gāruḍe: "adhvaryubhir vipravarair mate vikhanasas sthitaiḥ /
[26.2]     tatrārādhanam īhasva viṣṇor amitatejasaḥ //" iti [GaruḍaP ]

     [śrīraṅge vaikhānasārcanam]

[26.3]     tathā tatraiva śrīraṅgamāhātmye:
[26.4]     "brahmā 'pi divyahaṃsena sitameghopamena ca /
[26.5]     pṛṣṭhato 'nuyayau viṣṇuṃ vastreṇācchādya cānanam // [Garuḍa.P ]
[26.6]     tatrārcako mahābhāgo bhagavān vikhanās tathā /
[26.7]     dadau prasādaṃ devānāṃ raṅganāthābhyanujñayā //" iti [GaruḍaP ]
[26.8]     tathā uparicaravasucarite:
[26.9]     "vaikhānasānāṃ vacanair japahomārcanādibhiḥ /
[26.10]     yajed dhariṃ surapatiṃ bhūmer vivarago 'pi san //" iti [GaruḍaP ]

     [vṛṣagirau vaikhānasārcanam]

[26.11]     tathā vṛṣagirimāhātmye:
[26.12]     "antaḥpraviśya munayas saha vaikhānasair dvijair /
[26.13]     praṇamanty anvahaṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇam anāmayam //" iti [GaruḍaP ]
[26.14]     tathā āgneyapurāṇe phullāraṇyamāhātmye:
[26.15]     "phullaśiṣyās tu yakṣās te pūjayanti yuge yuge /
[26.16]     vaikhānasena vidhinā yathā phullamukhāc cyutam // [AgniP ]
[26.17]     mānuṣāḥ pūjayantīha vaikhānasamate sthitāḥ //" iti [AgniP ]
[26.18]     tathā brahmakaivarte puṣkaratīrthavaibhavavarṇane:
[26.19]     "nimnagānāṃ yathā gaṅgā devānāṃ bhagavān hariḥ /
[26.20]     varṇānāṃ brāhmaṇāś śreṣṭhā āśramāṇāṃ yatir yathā // [BrahmakaivartaP ]
[26.21]     śrutīnām ādibhūtānām ādir ekāyanī yathā /
[26.22]     vyūhānām ādibhūtas tu vāsudevo yathā varaḥ /
[26.23]     trimūrtīnāṃ yathā viṣṇuś śivānān tu sadāśivaḥ // [BrahmakaivartaP ]

     [vipreṣu vaikhānasānāṃ, sūtreṣu vaikhānasasūtrasya ca śreṣṭhyam]

[26.24]     dharmāṇāṃ vaiṣṇavo dharmaḥ smṛtīnāṃ mānavī smṛtiḥ /
[26.25]     viprāṇāṃ vedaviduṣāṃ yathā vaikhānaso varaḥ // [BrahmakaivartaP ]




[27.1]     sūtrāṇāṃ tatpraṇītan tu yathā śreṣṭhatamaṃ smṛtam /
[27.2]     tathaiva puṣkaro rājaṃs tīrthānām uttamottamaḥ //" [BrahmakaivartaP ]
[27.3-6]     iti ca pratipādanāt īdṛśānāṃ vaikhānasānām eva śrutismṛtītihāsapurāṇādiṣu caturmukhāt sāmānyatvena vinā sarvotkṛṣṭatvenotpattiśravaṇāt brahmasabhāpraveśasūryapathādyāśrayaṇādipratipādanāc ca vaikhānasā na tṛtīyāśramaniṣṭhāḥ, na vā brahmaṇā sāmānyataḥ sṛṣṭā bhavitum arhanti.

     [jambudvīpe bhāratavarśasya śreṣṭhyam]

[27.7]     śrīviṣṇupurāṇe: "atrāpi bhārataṃ śreṣṭhaṃ jambūdvīpe mahāmune /
[27.8]     yato hi karmabhūr eṣā hy ato 'nyā bhogabhūmayaḥ // [Viṣṇu.P 2.2.22]
[27.9]     kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparañ ca kaliścānyatra na kvacit /
[27.10]     tapas tapyanti yatayo juhvate cātra yajvanaḥ // [ViṣṇuP ]
[27.11]     dānāni cātra dīyante paralokārtham ādarāt /
[27.12]     puruṣair yajñapuruṣo jambūdvīpe sadejyate // [Viṣṇu.P ]
[27.13]     yajñair yajñamayo viṣṇur anyadvīpeṣu cānyathā // [ViṣṇuP ]
[27.14]     atra janmasahasrāṇāṃ sahasrair api sattama /
[27.15]     kadācillabhate jantur mānuṣyaṃ puṇyasañcayāt //" [ViṣṇuP 2.2.23]
[27.16-19]     iti bhāratakhaṇḍavyatiriktasthaleṣu brahmacaryādyāśramādivyavasthāvyavahārādyabhavāt pāñcarātraśilpajyautiṣādiṣu eṣām advārakabhagavadyajanādhikāritvaparamavaidikaparamaikāntitvādeḥ pratipādanāṅ ca eṣv eva vaikhānasatvaṃ naisargikam. vānaprastheṣu vaikhānasatvaṃ na naisargikam.
[27.20-22]     kintu teṣāṃ sūtrāntareṣv anuktānāṃ vānaprasthāśramasvīkāraprayogaśrāmaṇakāgnikuṇḍavidhānādīnāṃ vikhanas sūtre pratipāditānāṃ tatsūtroktaprakāreṇa vānaprasthāśramasvīkārādinaiva vaikhānasatvasiddhir iti.
[27.23]     idam evāha baudhāyanaḥ:

     [vānaprasthānāṃ mukhyavṛttyā vaikhānasaśabdavācyatvābhāvaḥ]

[27.24-28.2]      "vānaprastho vaikhānasaśāstrasamudācāro vane mūlaphalāśī tapaśśīlas savaneṣūdakam upaspṛśan śrāmaṇakenāgnim ādhāyāgrāmyabhojī devapitṛmanuṣyabhūtarṣipūjakaḥ sarvātithiḥ pratiṣiddhavarjaṃ bhaikṣam apy upayuñjīta. na phālakṛṣṭam adhitiṣṭhet grāmaṃ vā na praviśet" iti.





[28.3]     manuḥ: "ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi dharmaṃ vaikhānasāśrayam //" ity ārabhya
[28.4]     "puṣpamūlaphalair vāpi kevalair vartayet sadā /
[28.5]     kālapakvais svayaṃ śīrṇair vaikhānasamate sthitaḥ //" iti [ManuDhŚ 6.21]
[28.6-8]     hārīta: "vānaprastho grāmyā oṣadhīḥ parivarjayet. tretāgnīnāṃ sthāne śrāmaṇakaṃ vāgnim ādhāya valkalaśāṇacarmakuśamuñjādivalkalaṃ vā vasāno vaikhānasaproktena vidhinā vānaprastho bhavati. anujñāyiko 'nuprasthāyika" iti.
[28.9]     yama: "śrāmaṇakena vidhānena sāyaṃ prātar upaspṛśed" iti.
[28.10-11]     śaṅkhalikhitau: "śrāmaṇakenāgnim ādhāya kāle kuruvindaveṇuśyāmākanīvārādibhir vartayed" iti.
[28.12]     vasiṣṭho 'pi: "śrāmaṇakenāgnim ādhāyāhitāgnir vṛkṣamūlika" iti.
[28.13]     asya yajñasvāmivyākhyāne:
[28.14]     "śrāmaṇakaṃ nāma vaikhānasaśāstram. taduktena vidhināgnim ādhāya" iti.
[28.15]     śukānuśāsane vyāso 'pi:
[28.16]     "mūlair eke phalair eke puṣpair eke dṛḍhavratāḥ / [MBh 12.236.13cd]
[28.17]     vartayanti yathānyāyaṃ vaikhānasamate sthitāḥ //" iti [MBh 12.236.14ab]
[28.18]     smṛtyantaram api: "yasminn eva tu samproktaṃ sūtre vikhanasā param /
[28.19]     vanasthānān tu sarveṣāṃ vidhiśrāmaṇakābhidhaḥ //
[28.20]     vānaprasthās tatas sarve ye dvijās tv anyasūtriṇaḥ /
[28.21]     tatsūtravidhyanuṣṭhānāt smṛtā vaikhānasās tu te //" iti ca varṇayanti. [ĀS 11.4]
[28.22]     ataś ca vānaprasthā mukhyatvena vaikhānasaśabdavācyā na bhavanti.
[28.23]     ānuśāsanike ca:
[28.24]     "taṃ patantam abhiprekṣya prekṣya ca rṣigaṇānatha / [MBh 13, App. 1A.313]
[28.25]     āsīnāna vasubhis sārdhaṃ satreṇa jagatīpateḥ // [MBh 13, App. 1A.314]





[29.1]     vaikhānasānām eteṣāṃ vālakhilyagaṇān api / [MBh 13, App. 1A.315]
[29.2]     tasya bhīrāviśattatra patagendrasya bhārata // [MB.h 13, App. 1A.316]
[29.3]     tuṇḍena gṛhya tāṃ śākhām utpapāta khageśvaraḥ //" iti [MBh 13, App. 1A.318]
[29.4]     tatraivomāmaheśvarasaṃvāde:
[29.5]     "vaikhānasānāṃ vai dharmaṃ śrotum icchāmi dharmataḥ // ity ārabhya
[29.6]     teṣu vaikhānasā nāma vānaprasthāś śubhekṣaṇe / [MBh 13, App. 15.702]
[29.7]     tīvreṇa tapasā yuktā dīptimantas sutejasaḥ //" iti [MBh 13, App. 15.703]
[29.8]     harivaṃśe ca akrūrāgamanasamaye:
[29.9]     "śakapotrāvyayā? mode pradoṣe 'bhyāśatas kare / [HariV 68.4]
[29.10]     kiñcid abhyudite some śātiteṣu tamas su ca // [Hariv 68.9]
[29.11]     vanyair vaikhānasair mantraiḥ hūyamāne hutāśane //" iti. [HariV 68.5cd]
[29.12]     pādme ca: "brāhmaṇaṃ vṛddhahārītaṃ vaikhānasamate sthitam //" iti ca varṇanāt [PadmaP ]
[29.13-15]     vānaprasthasya śrautaviṣaye pṛthaktvena mantrapratipādanābhāvāc ca bodhāyanādibhir uktaprakāreṇa vānaprasthasya vaikhānasatvaṃ vaikhānasasūtroktavānaprasthāśramasvīkārād evety avagantavyam. etāvatā vikhanaś śabdārtho nirṇītaḥ.
[29.16]     (ādyahetunirūpaṇaprakāraḥ)

     [vaikhānasasūtraśāstrayor vikhanasā praṇītatvam]

[29.17-18]     atha vaikhānasasūtraśāstrayoḥ akhilajagatkāraṇabhūtena vikhanasā praṇītatvam upapādyate.
[29.19]     viṣṇudharme: "kathayāmi yathāpūrvaṃ matpitrā kathitaṃ mama /
[29.20]     tasyāpi kila tatpitrā tasmai cāha kilośanāḥ // [ViṣṇuDh 1.38]





[30.1]     tenāpi bhṛgum ārādhya prāptam ārādhanaṃ hareḥ /
[30.2]     sakāśād brahmaṇaḥ prāptaṃ bhṛguṇāpi mahātmanā // [ViṣṇuD.h 1.39]
[30.3]     prāptaṃ sakāśād devasya brahmaṇo 'vyaktajanmanaḥ //" iti. [ViṣṇuDh 1.40ab]

     [vaikhānasamārgasya upadeśaparamaṃparā]

[30.4]     hārītasmṛtau: "pūrvaṃ vikhanaso viṣṇuḥ proktavān svayam acyutaḥ /
[30.5]     bhṛgoḥ proktaṃ vikhanasā bhṛguṇā ca mameritam //" iti

     [pāñcarātrāgamotpattyādiprakāraḥ]

[30.6]     gāruḍe: "purā caturmukhādeśāc catvāro munayo 'malāḥ /
[30.7]     praṇīya vaiṣṇavaṃ śāstraṃ bhūmāv abhyarcayan nṛpa // [GaruḍaP ]
[30.8]     marīcir mandare viṣṇuṃ arcayamāsa keśavam /
[30.9]     ādeśād brahmaṇo viṣṇuṃ śrīnivāse 'trir arcayet // [GaruḍaP ]
[30.10]     kaśyapo viṣṇvadhiṣṭhāne śubhakṣetre bhṛgur muniḥ /
[30.11]     gaṅgāyā dakṣiṇe tīre sīmni tasyāntike 'pi ca // [GaruḍaP ]
[30.12]     tatsandhau śuciṣaṇṇāmā bhṛguṇā sthāpito hariḥ //" iti coktam [GaruḍaP ]
[30.13]     pāñcarātre: "ādye kaliyuge prāpte somakena hṛtā trayī /
[30.14]     avaidikeṣu lokeṣu daivateṣu muniṣv api //
[30.15]     bhagavantaṃ samāsādya nārāyaṇam anāmayam /
[30.16]     ananto garuḍaś caiva viṣvakseṇaḥ pitāmahaḥ //
[30.17]     śaṅkaraś caiva pañcaite papracchuḥ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ /
[30.18]     kṣaṇam apy acyutasyārcāṃ tyaktum eva na śaknumaḥ //
[30.19]     avaidikeṣu lokeṣu kiṃ kurmaś calamānasāḥ /
[30.20]     tasmād upāyaṃ lakṣmīśa vadāsmākaṃ cirantana //
[30.21]     ity uktas sa haris tebhyaḥ pañcarātravidhiṃ kramāt /
[30.22]     ekaikarātram ekasmai tantraṃ samupadiṣṭavān //
[30.23]     pañcalakṣapramāṇena pañcarātraṃ prapañcitam //" ity upakramya
[30.24]     "prathamaṃ brahmarātran tu dvitīyaṃ rudrarātrakam /
[30.25]     tṛtīyam indrarātraṃ yac caturthaṃ graharātrakam //




[31.1]     pañcamaṃ munirātran tu pañcarātraṃ vidhīyate /
[31.2]     rātribhiḥ pañcabhiḥ proktaṃ śrutaṃ śiṣyaiś ca pañcabhiḥ //
[31.3]     tasmāt tat pañcarātrākhyāṃ labdhvā tiṣṭhati bhūtale //"
[31.4-5]     ity antena pāñcarātrasyotpattyādikaṃ nirūpya paramavaidikasya śrīvaikhānasasyotpattyādikaṃ pratipādyate.

     [vaikhānasaśāstrotpattyādiprakāraḥ]

[31.6]     atha matsyākṛtiḥ śrīśaḥ praviśyāmbudhimadhyamam /
[31.7]     nirmathya somakaṃ vedān adāt paṅkajayonaye //
[31.8]     tādṛśaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ stotrais santoṣya padmabhūḥ /
[31.9]     uvāca vacanaṃ premṇā daṇḍavat praṇipatya ca //
[31.10]     tāntrikeṇa tvayā proktaṃ mārgeṇa bhavad arcanam /
[31.11]     na prasīdati tenāsman manaḥ kamalalocana //
[31.12]     vaidikena tvad arcāṃ me yathāpūrvaṃ vadācyuta /
[31.13]     ity ukto bhagavān devaḥ śāstraṃ śrutipathāgatam //
[31.14]     sahasrakoṭibhiḥ ślokais saṅkhyātaṃ bahuvistaram /
[31.15]     sūtramūlam anādyantaṃ kalpe kalpe samāśritam //
[31.16]     uvāca jagatāṃ prītyai yajñānāṃ pūraṇāya ca /
[31.17]     mūlaṃ sarvāgamānāñ ca purāṇānāṃ tathaiva ca //
[31.18]     smṛtīnāṃ sarvasūtrāṇāṃ pratyaṅgopāṅgaśobhinām /
[31.19]     vedāś ca vikhanaśśāstraṃ pramāṇam iti cerayan //
[31.20]     yathā vaikhānasaṃ pūrve 'han sāmabhavatīti ca /
[31.21]     ye nakhā bhuvi sañjātās te vai vaikhānasā iti //
[31.22]     śrutyuktaṃ tad idaṃ śāstraṃ vaikhānasamahārṇavam /
[31.23]     ity uktvā bhagavān ādyas tatraivāntaradhīyata //
[31.24]     tataḥ paraṃ caturvaktro jaṭākāṣāyadaṇḍabhṛt /
[31.25]     naimiśāraṇyam āsādya dvijasaṅghaniṣevitam //





[32.1]     tapas taptvā ciraṃ kālaṃ dhyāyaṃs tejas tu vaiṣṇavam /
[32.2]     paścād apaśyad viṣṇūktam āgamaṃ vistarāt tadā //
[32.3]     saśrautañ ca sagṛhyañ ca vedamantrair abhiṣṭutam /
[32.4]     saṃkṣipya sāram ādāya śāṇollikhitaratnavat //
[32.5]     dhātā vikhanaso nāma marīcyādisutān munīn /
[32.6]     abodhayad idaṃ śāstraṃ sārdhakoṭipramāṇataḥ //
[32.7]     kalpe kalpe purā viṣṇur udbhūtaḥ pūrvavat sadā /
[32.8]     tasmād vaidikam ācāraṃ yaḥ kartuṃ bhuvi vāñchati //
[32.9]     tasyedaṃ śāstram ity uktaṃ netareṣābhitīritam //"

     [vaikhānasasūtrasya tatsūtriṇāṃ ca māhātmyam]

[32.10]     purātantre saptacatvāriṃśe 'dhyāye:
[32.11]     ṛṣaya ūcuḥ: "vaikhānasasya sūtrasya kiṃ māhātmyaṃ mahāmune /
[32.12]     vihāya sarvasūtrāṇi yat tvayā cānuvartitam // [Purātantra.]
[32.13]     tatsūtriṇāñ ca māhātmyaṃ śrotum icchāmahe vayam /
[32.14]     samūrtasyāsya yajñasya ye yogyāḥ iti kīrtitāḥ // [Purātantra.]
[32.15]     bhṛguḥ: yuṣmābhiḥ paripṛṣṭaṃ yat samyag vakṣyāmi suvratāḥ /
[32.16]     śruṇvantu munayas sarve sūtramāhātmyam uttamam // [Purātantra]
[32.17]     suptotthitaś ciraṃ brahmā sraṣṭukāmaḥ purābhavat /
[32.18]     sasmāra vedān akhilān na sṛṣṭis sampravartate // [Purātantra.]
[32.19]     ciraṃ suptasya vai dhātus tamasākrāntacetasaḥ /
[32.20]     vismṛtā nikhilā vedā hṛdaye tasya saṃsthitāḥ // [Purātantra.]
[32.21]     cintāturas tadā brahmā nālaṅkartuṃ kim apy abhūt /
[32.22]     tataś cintān tu tāṃ tyaktvā svasthacittaḥ prajāpatiḥ // [Purātantra.]
[32.23]     hṛdpadmamadhye puruṣaṃ parameṇa samādhinā /
[32.24]     arcayāmāsa vai viṣṇum ṛgyajussāmarūpiṇam // [Purātantra.]






     [dakṣādinavabrahmasṛṣṭiḥ]

[33.1]     tuṣṭāva ca tadā brahmā haripravaṇamānāsaḥ /
[33.2]     nanāma ca tadā viṣṇuṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam // [Purātantra.]
[33.3]     bruvato bhagavaddhyānāt vinaṣṭatamaso vidheḥ /
[33.4]     sattvodriktasya tasyāśu nairmalyaṃ hṛdaye 'bhavat // [Purātantra]
[33.5]     tatas tu bhagavān brahmā chandomūlam avāptavān /
[33.6]     tasya dakṣiṇato vaktrāt tuṣṭāva jagataḥ patim // [Purātantra]
[33.7]     sasmāra vividhān vedān sāṅgān upaniṣadgaṇān /
[33.8]     purāṇanyāyamīmāṃsā dharmaśāstrāṇi sarvaśaḥ // [Purātantra.]
[33.9]     antarhitānāṃ khananād vedānān tu viśeṣataḥ /
[33.10]     sa vibhuḥ procyate sarvair vikhanā brahmavādibhiḥ // [Purātantra.]
[33.11]     vaikhānasaś ca bhagavān procyate sa pitāmahaḥ /
[33.12]     tatas sasarja bhagavān viśvayoniḥ pitāmahaḥ // [Purātantra]
[33.13]     jagat sarvam aśeṣeṇa vedadṛṣṭena vartmanā /
[33.14]     prāṇāc ca cakṣuṣas tadvad abhimānāc ca karmaṇaḥ // [Purātantra]
[33.15]     hṛdayāc chirasaś śrotrād udānād vyānatas tataḥ /
[33.16]     samānāc ca tathāpānād ṛṣṭiśreṣṭhānimān daśa // [Purātantra]
[33.17]     dakṣaṃ marīcinaṃ nīlalohitaṃ bhṛgum eva ca /
[33.18]     tathāṅgirasam atriñ ca pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ tathā // [Purātantra]
[33.19]     vasiṣṭhañ ca kratuñ caiva kramād asṛjad abjabhūḥ /
[33.20]     nava brahmāṇa evaite vinā syur nīlalohitam // [Purātantra]
[33.21]     vedānāṃ vyasanād arvāk prāgrūpaṃ militan tu yat /
[33.22]     tān tu vaikhānasīṃ śākhāṃ ādāvadhyāpayan munīn // [Purātantra]
[33.23]     (nāmnā vikhanasaṃ prāhur yañ ca vaikhānasaṃ tathā // [Purātantra]
[33.24]     bhṛgvaṅgiromarīcyatripulastyapulahāḥ kratuḥ /






[34.1]     tathā vasiṣṭho dakṣaś ca nava brahmāṇa īritāḥ // [Purātantra]
[34.2]     nava brahmāṇa evaite vinā syur nīlalohitam // [Purātantra]

     [dakṣādīnāṃ navānāṃ vikhanaś śiśyatvam]

[34.3]     ete vikhanasaś śiṣyāḥ śrutismṛtividhānataḥ /
[34.4]     tacchiṣyās tu mahātmano munayas tattvadarśinaḥ // [Purātantra.]
[34.5]     vedānugāni śāstrāṇi cakrur lokahitaiṣiṇaḥ /
[34.6]     kecit sūtraṇi vai cakruḥ gṛhyaśrautātmikāni tu // [Purātantra]
[34.7]     dharmaśāstrāṇi kecit tu purāṇāni ca kecana /
[34.8]     itihāsāṃs tathā kalpān procuranye mahārṣayaḥ // [Purātantra.]

     [vaikānasaśākhāniṣpattiprakāraḥ]

[34.9]     tān tu vaikhānasīṃ śākhāṃ svasūtre viniyuktavān /
[34.10]     padmabhūḥ paramo dhātā tasminn ārādhanatrayam // [Purātantra.]
[34.11]     tān tu vaikhānasīṃ śākhāṃ vyāsas tu bhagavān muniḥ /
[34.12]     cakre ṛgādibhedais tu vyasitvā tu pṛthak pṛthak // [Purātantra]
[34.13]     audgātraṃ sāmabhir yāge brāhmam ātharvaṇena ca /
[34.14]     hautram ṛgbhir yajur mantrair ādhvaryavam akārayat // [Purātantra.]
[34.15]     āmnāyasya vidhir brāhmaḥ pañcakāṇḍātmikā tu sā /
[34.16]     sā ca vaikhānasī śākhā taittirīyā ca kīrtitā // [Purātantra]
[34.17]     ādikāle tu bhagavān brahmā tu vikhānā muniḥ /
[34.18]     yajuś śākhānusāreṇa cakre sūtraṃ mahattaram // [Purātantra]
[34.19]     varṇāśramācārayutaṃ śrautasmārtasamanvitam /
[34.20]     yasminn eva tu samproktaṃ sūtre vikhanasā param // [Purātantra]
[34.21]     vanasthānān tu sarveṣāṃ vidhiś śrāmaṇakābhidhaḥ /
[34.22]     vānaprasthās tatas sarve ye dvijāś cānyasūtriṇaḥ /
[34.23]     tatsūtravidhyanuṣṭhānāt smṛtā vaikhānasās tu te // [Purātantra]
[34.24]     yatsūtrādyantamadhyeṣu bhagavān viṣṇur avyayaḥ /





[35.1]     yaṣṭavyo gīyate yasmāt sarvasūtrottaman tu tat // [Purātantra]
[35.2]     vede vaikhānase sūtre yo dharmaḥ parikīrtitaḥ /
[35.3]     sarvais sa dharmo 'nuṣṭheyo nātra kāryā vicāraṇā // [Purātantra]

     [vaikhānasasūtrasya sūtrāntarānapekṣatvam]

[35.4]     svasūtrasya parityāgād anyasūtrasya saṃśrayāt /
[35.5]     sadyaḥ patati vai vipro na vedasya samāśraye // [Purātantra]
[35.6]     etad vaikhānasaṃ sūtram anyaśāstrānapekṣitam // [Purātantra]
[35.7]     etad vaikhānasaṃ sūtraṃ sarvavedārthasaṅgraham /
[35.8]     vaiṣṇavaṃ sarvaviprāṇāṃ sāmānyam abhidhīyate // [Purātantra]
[35.9]     vaikhānasasya sūtrasya cāgneḥ śrāmaṇakasya ca /
[35.10]     nārāyaṇasya devasya māhātmyaṃ nāvabuddhyate // [Purātantra]
[35.11]     yathā vedeṣu sarveṣu sāmavedaḥ praśasyate /
[35.12]     tathā sūtreṣu sarveṣu sūtram etad praśasyate // [Purātantra]
[35.13]     agnir vaikhānasaṃ śāstraṃ viṣṇur vedāś ca śāśvatāḥ /
[35.14]     gāyatrī vaiṣṇavā viprās saptaite 'tipavitrakāḥ // [Purātantra]
[35.15]     yadadhīteṣu vedeṣu sāṅgeṣu labhate phalam /
[35.16]     tatphalaṃ labhate sadyaḥ sūtram etat paṭhan dvijaḥ // [Purātantra]
[35.17]     agnīṣomādayo devā ye yajñāṃśahavir bhujaḥ /
[35.18]     ......
[35.19]     śārīrāṇy anyasūtrāṇi tathā svargaphalāni ca /
[35.20]     vaiṣṇavaṃ sūtram ettu sarvasiddhikaraṃ param // [Purātantra]
[35.21]     ādyatvāt sarvasūtrāṇāṃ vaiṣṇavatvāc ca tat tu vai /
[35.22]     mayānuvartitaṃ tadvatkaśyapātrimarīcibhiḥ // [Purātantra]
[35.23]     gṛhe puruṣapūjāyā vidhānam ṛṣisattamāḥ /




[36.1]     uktaṃ saṅkepataḥ sūtrenoktam ālayapūjanam // [Purātantra]

[36.3]     teṣān tu havir ādatte viṣṇus sākṣāt sanātanaḥ // [Purātantra]
[36.4]     śatakratūnāṃ yajato yatphalaṃ parikīrtitam /

     [ālaye pañcamūrtyarcanasya śraiṣṭhyam]

[36.5]     ālaye pañcamūrtīnām arcanan tv adhikaṃ bhavet // [Purātantra]
[36.6]     ālāyārcā gṛhārceti cobhayaṃ śruticoditam /

[36.11]     asmābhir api tatsūtra- matagāmibhir eva tu // [Purātantra]
[36.12]     pañcamūrtividhānena śāstram etad udāhṛtam /
[36.13]     tasmād atra mayoktasya homasyāgnyālayasya ca // [Purātantra]
[36.14]     puṇyāhavāstusāmānya- homādīnāñ ca karmaṇām /
[36.15]     ye 'nye ca mantrās te grāhyās sūtre vikhanasā smṛtāḥ // [Purātantra.]
[36.16]     ālayārcavidhis so 'yaṃ vaidikas sarvasiddhidaḥ /
[36.17]     sarvalokahitārthāya prokto 'smābhir viśeṣataḥ // [Purātantra.]

     [vaikhānasānam garbhavaiṣṇavatvam]

[36.18]     ālayārcaṇakarmedaṃ vaidikaṃ bhagavatpriyaṃ /
[36.19]     anuṣṭheyaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhaiḥ tadvaikhānasasūtribhiḥ // [Purātantra.]
[36.20]     ye vaikhānasasūtreṇa saṃskṛtās tu dvijātayaḥ /
[36.21]     te viṣṇusadṛśā jñeyāḥ sarveṣām uttamottamāḥ // [Purātantra.]
[36.22]     vaikhānasānāṃ sarveṣāṃ garbhavaiṣṇavajanmanām /
[36.23]     nārāyaṇaḥ svayaṃ garbhe mudrāṃ dhārayate nijām // [Purātantra]

     [vaikhānasapūjāyaḥ bhagavatprītikaratvam]

[36.24]     viprā vaikhānasākhyā ye te smṛtā bhagavatpriyāḥ /





[37.1]     ekāntinas susattvasthā dehāntaṃ nānyayājinaḥ // [Purātantra]
[37.2]     viṣṇoḥ priyatamā loke catvāraḥ parikīrtitāḥ /
[37.3]     aśvatthaḥ kapilā gāvas tulasī vikhanās tathā // [Purātantra.]
[37.4]     dvijeṣu brāhmaṇāḥ śreṣṭhāḥ brāhmaṇeṣu ca vaiṣṇavāḥ /
[37.5]     vaiṣṇaveṣu dvijāḥ śreṣṭhā ye vaikhānasasūtriṇaḥ // [Purātantra.]
[37.6]     vaiṣṇavīṃ pratimāṃ loke vipraṃ vaikhānasaṃ tathā /
[37.7]     gaṅgāṃ viṣṇupadīṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate // [Purātantra]
[37.8]     tasmād vaikhānasā viprā vaiṣṇavā munisattamāḥ /
[37.9]     ālayārcanayogyāś ca yogyā nānye dvijātayaḥ /
[37.10]     purā tu pṛṣṭavān brahmā devadevaṃ janārdanam // [Purātantra]
[37.11]     "kathaṃ kena prakāreṇa pūjanīyo 'si kair api /"
[37.12]     ity evaṃ bhagavān pṛṣṭaḥ prāha vai caturānanam // [Purātantra]
[37.13]     "ālaye ty arcanaṃ syāt tu parivārānvitasya me /
[37.14]     vaikhānasavidhānena vaidikena viśeṣataḥ // [Purātantra]
[37.15]     vaikhānasais tu viprendrair arcanaṃbis hier noch Telugu vergleichen mama tuṣṭidam /
[37.16]     amūrtañ ca samūrtañ ca dvidhā vaidikam ucyate // [Purātantra]
[37.17]     amūrtaṃ gārhapatyādyaṃ samūrtaṃ berapūjanam /
[37.18]     yathā karmaṇa ekasya kalpitāḥ pañca vahnayaḥ // [Purātantra]
[37.19]     tathā caikavimānasya pañcaberāṇi kalpayet /
[37.20]     grāmādāv ālaye tasmād devadevo janārdanaḥ // [Purātantra]
[37.21]     anena vidhinā pūjyo viprair vaikhānasais tathā /
[37.22]     pūjā vaikhānasair viprair ālaye syād viśeṣataḥ // [Purātantra]
[37.23]     sarvasampatkarañ caiva sarvāśubhavināśanam /
[37.24]     tadgrāmavāsināṃ tadvad aihikāmuṣmikapradam // [Purātantra]





     [avaikhānasapūjane doṣaḥ, tatprāyaścittañ ca]

[38.1]     varṣadaṃ puṣṭidaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ rājarāṣṭrābhivṛddhidam /
[38.2]     karṣaṇādipratiṣṭhārcāprāyaścittāvasānakam /
[38.3]     anuṣṭheyo vidhis so 'yaṃ viprair vaikhānasais tataḥ // [Purātantra]
[38.4]     avaikhānasasūtrais tu viprair ārādhanaṃ hareḥ /
[38.5]     vālaye sarvalokānāṃ vināśāya bhaviṣyati // [Purātantra]

[38.8]     yady avaikhānaso vipra ālayārcanam ācaret /

[38.14]     ālāpaṃ darśanañ caiva sparśanañ ca viśeṣataḥ /

[38.16]     avaikhānasasūtreṇa spṛṣṭe bimbe pramādataḥ /

[38.18]     evam eva tathā kuryād viprair anyaiḥ prapūjite /

[38.20]     tryahan tu pūjite tadvad vāstuhomaṃ samāpya ca /

[38.22]     arcane tu mahāviṣṇos saptāhan tu viśeṣataḥ /
[38.23]     mahāśāntiṃ yajitvā tu śuddhiṃ pūrvavad ācaret // [Purātantra]
[38.24]     dvādaśāhaṃ samārabhya māsāntan tu viśeṣataḥ /





[39.1]     avaikhānasapūjāyāṃ tantrasaṅkara eva ca // [Purātantra]

     [avaikhānasapūjane bhagavatsānnidhyavirahaḥ]

[39.2]     māsatrayaṃ ca ṣaṇmāsam anyaviprais tu pūjane /
[39.3]     na tatra bimbe sānnidhyaṃ devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ // [Purātantra]
[39.4]     tasmāt tad doṣaśāntyarthaṃ mahāśānter anantaram /
[39.5]     adhivāsatrayaṃ kṛtvā pratiṣṭhāṃ punar ācaret // [Purātantra]
[39.6]     saṃvatsare tu devasya viprair vaikhānasetaraiḥ /
[39.7]     pūjābhicārikī proktā tatra sarvaṃ vinaśyati // [Purātantra]
[39.8]     tasmāt tatkarṣaṇādyañ ca niṣkṛtyantālayārcanam /

     [tāntrikārcāyām api tantradīkṣitānām evādhikāraḥ]

[39.9]     kārayed vidhivadvidvān tadvaikhānasasūtribhiḥ /
[39.10]     tāntrikārcāvidhau cāpi tāntrikair eva dīkṣitaiḥ // [Purātantra.]
[39.11]     pūjanīyo hariḥ samyak vipraiḥ nānyaiḥ kadācana /
[39.12]     anyena vidhinā mantrair anyair anyārcakena vā // [Purātantra]
[39.13]     ālaye tvarcanaṃ syāc cen mahādoṣo bhaved dhruvam /

[39.15]     pratiṣṭhādiṣu saṅgrāhyāḥ proktā vaikhānasā dvijāḥ /
[39.16]     brahmāpi bhagavān devo harir nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ // [Purātantra]
[39.17]     nāviṣṇur jāyate viṣṇur nāviṣṇur viṣṇum arcayet /
[39.18]     suprītenārcakenaiva yad uktaṃ devasannidhau // [Purātantra.]
[39.19]     taddevenaiva samproktaṃ tathaiva ca bhaviṣyati /

[40.1]     padmabhūḥ paramo dhātā tasminn ārādhanatrayam // [SkandaP ]
[40.2]     uktavān nigamārthānām ācāraṃ pravibhāgaśaḥ //" iti [SkandaP ]

     [ekasya yajurvedasya vyāsakatṛkaṃ vibhajanam]

[40.3]     brahmakaivartavacanāni pūrvam evoktāni.
[40.4-5]     nanu ṛgyajussāmātharvāṇa iti vedānāṃ loke prasiddheḥ sarvaśākhāmūlabhūto yajurveda iti pūrvoktaṃ katham upapadyate iti ced ucyate.
[40.6]     śrīviṣṇupurāṇe
[40.7]     "vedadrumasya maitreya śākhābhedās sahasraśaḥ /
[40.8]     na śakyā vistarād vaktuṃ saṅkṣepeṇa śṛṇuṣva tam // [Viṣṇu.P 3.3.4]
[40.9]     dvāpare dvāpare viṣṇur vyāsarūpī mahāmune // [Viṣṇu.P ]

[40.11]     vīryaṃ tejo balañ cālpaṃ manuṣyāṇām avekṣya ca /
[40.12]     hitāya sarvabhūtānāṃ vedabhedaṃ karoti saḥ // [Viṣṇu.P 3.3.6]
[40.13]     ity ārabhya
[40.14]     "eka āsīd yajurvedas taṃ caturdhā hy akalpayat /
[40.15]     cāturhotram abhūd yasmiṃs tena yajñam athākarot // [Viṣṇu.P 3.4.11]
[40.16]     ārdhvaryavaṃ yajurbhis tu ṛgbhir hautraṃ tathā muniḥ /

[40.20]     rājñāntvatharvavedena sarvakarmāṇi sa prabhuḥ /
[40.21]     kārayāmāsa maitreya brahmatvañ ca yathāsthiti /// [ViṣṇuP 3.4.14]
[40.22]     so 'yam eko mahān vedatarus tena pṛthakkṛtaḥ /

     [yajurvedasya vaikhānasaśākhātvaprasiddhiḥ]

[41.1-3]     sa ca yajurvedaḥ: "bahuśṛṅgaś catus sānuḥ pṛthulo vedaparvataḥ" ity ārabhyoktarītyā vedavyāsarupiṇā bhagavatā yadā vyastaḥ, tataḥ pūrvam ekarūpeṇāvasthitasya tasya vedaparvatasya vaikhānasaśākhātvaprasiddhir āsīd iti pūrvam eva pratipāditam.
[41.4]     vaikhānasānāṃ śraiṣṭhyam

     [vaikhānasānāṃ śreṣṭhyaṃ pañcakālaparāyaṇatvañ ca]

[41.5-6]     prasaṅgāt vaikhānasaśākhāmūlakatvena praṇītasūtrānuṣṭhātṝṇāṃ śreṣṭhatvam acchidrapañcakālaparāyaṇatvādikañ ca pratipādyate.

     [vaikhānasadarśanaphalam]

[41.14]     taṃ brāhmaṇan tu dṛṣṭvaiva sarvaṃ pāpaṃ vyapohati // [Vṛddhayājñavalkya.]
[41.15]     vaiṣṇavīṃ pratimāṃ loke vipraṃ vaikhānasaṃ tathā /
[41.16]     gaṅgāṃ viṣṇupadīṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate //" iti [Vṛddhayājñavalkya]

[41.20]     nityayājisahasrebhyas somayājī viśiṣyate /
