     [vaikhānasānām ekāntitvam]

[42.1]     brahmakaivarte: "nimnagānāṃ yathā gaṅgā devānāṃ bhagavān hariḥ /
[42.2]     varṇānāṃ brāhmaṇaṃ śreṣṭhaḥ āśramāṇāṃ yatir yathā // [Brahmakaivarta.P ]
[42.3]     śrutīnām ādibhūtānāṃ śrutir ekāyanī yathā /
[42.4]     tasyāṃ niṣadyātha yasyāṃ niṣaṇṇo bhagavān hariḥ // [BrahmakaivartaP ]
[42.5]     vyūhānām ādibhūtas tu vāsudevo yathā paraḥ /
[42.6]     trimūrtīnāṃ yathā viṣṇuḥ śivānān tu sadāśivaḥ // [Brahmakaivarta.P ]
[42.7]     dharmāṇāṃ vaiṣṇavo dharmaḥ smṛtīnāṃ mānavī smṛtiḥ /
[42.8]     viprāṇāṃ vedaviduṣāṃ yathā vaikhānaso varaḥ // [Brahmakaivarta.P ]
[42.9]     yathā munīnāṃ vikhanā ādibhūta udāhṛtaḥ /
[42.10]     sūtrāṇāṃ tatpraṇītan tu yathā śreṣṭhatamaṃ smṛtam // [Brahmakaivarta.P ]
[42.11]     tathaiva puṣkaro rājaṃs tīrthānām uttamottamaḥ //" [BrahmakaivartaP ]
[42.12] kaurme:
[42.13]     "maccittā madgataprāṇā mayi saṅgatamānasāḥ /
[42.14]     ananyaśaraṇā rājaṃs tasmād vaikhānasā varāḥ //" [KūrmaP ]

     [vaikhānasādhiṣṭhatadeśe viṣṇusānnidhyam]

[42.15]     purāṇāntare:
[42.16]     "yatra vaikhānasā viprā yatra santi gavāṃ gaṇāḥ /
[42.17]     yatra bilvāḥ palāśāś ca tatra sannihito hariḥ //"
[42.18]     bṛhannāradīye:
[42.19]     "jagatpavitrās te nityaṃ viṣṇum abhyarcayanti ye /
[42.20]     durvṛttā vā suvṛttā vā pūjanīyā viśeṣataḥ //" [BṛhannāradaP]
[42.21]     hārīte:
[42.22]     tasmāt te śuddhasattvasthāś śuddhā vaikhānasāḥ smṛtāḥ /
[42.23]     yān lokān prāpnuvanty ete tān śṛṇuṣva samāhitaḥ //"
[42.24]     pāñcarātre pauṣkare:
[42.25]     "viprā vaikhānasākhyā ye te bhaktās tattvam ucyate // [PauṣkaraS 36.260cd]
[42.26]     ekāntinas susattvasthā dehāntaṃ nānyayājinaḥ /





[43.1]     kartavyam iti deveśaṃ saṃyajante phalaṃ vinā // [PauṣkaraS 36.261]
[43.2]     prāpnuvanti ca dehānte vāsudevatvam abjaja //" iti [PauṣkaraS 36.262ab]
[43.3]     gautamīye:
[43.4]     "vaikhānasavidhānajñas tattvātmārthavyavasthitaḥ /
[43.5]     sūkṣmāt sūkṣmam avāpnoti paraṃ brahmāṇam avyayam //" iti

     [puṣkare vaikhānasāśramaḥ]

[43.6]     āraṇyaparvaṇi: rameśaḥ:
[43.7]     "dhyātañ ca saindhavāraṇyaṃ munibṛndaniṣevitam / [MBh 3.87.12cd]
[43.8]     pitāmahasaraḥ puṇyaṃ puṣkaraṃ nāma bhārata // [MBh 3.87.12ef]
[43.9]     vaikhānasānāṃ siddhānām ṛṣīṇām āśramaṃ priyam //" iti [MBh 3.87.13]
[43.10]     anyatra:
[43.11]     "saindhavāraṇyam āsādya kulyāṃ tāṃ lokadarśanām /
[43.12]     puṣkareṣu mahārāja sarveṣu ca jalaṃ spṛśan //" ity ārabhya [MBh 3.125.12]
[43.13]     "etac candrasaro nityam arpayanty ṛṣayas tathā /
[43.14]     vaikhānasaprabhṛtayo vālakhilyās tathaiva ca //" iti [MBh 3.125.14]

     [vaikhānasānām pūjanīyatvam]

[43.15]     anyatra: gālavaḥ:
[43.16]     "sarvān lokān prapaśyāmi prasādāt tava suvrata /
[43.17]     vaikhānasānāṃ japatām eṣa śabdo mahātmanām //" iti [MBh 3.114.15]
[43.18]     gāruḍe:
[43.19]     "kauṣītakīnāṃ hotṝṇāṃ grāmatrayam akalpayat /
[43.20]     akalpayac ca trīn grāmān vaikhānasamahātmanām //" iti [GaruḍaP ]
[43.21]     parameśvare trayodaśādhyāye pavitraviniyogāvasare:
[43.22]     "pūjayed āptapūrvāṃś ca yatipūrvāṃs tapasvinaḥ // [PārameśvaraS 12.437cd]
[43.23]     pañcavaikhānasāṃś caiva viprādīṃś caturas tathā /
[43.24]     pañcayogaratādyāṃs tu tathānyān vaiṣṇavān dvijān // [PārameśvaraS 12.438]
[43.25]     ekāyanīyaśākhoktiśrotṝṇāṃ prathamaṃ tataḥ //" iti [PārameśvaraS 12.439ab]





[44.1]     nāradīye: "sāttvike tu sadādhikyaṃ pūjanaṃ mama nārada /
[44.2]     viddhi vaikhānase dattaṃ dānaṃ brahmavidas tathā //" [NāradaP]

     [vaikhānasānām śrīrāmakṛtā pūjā]

[44.3]     vāsiṣṭharāmāyaṇe: "kṛtābhiṣekas santuṣṭas sāmātyas sasuhṛjjanaḥ /
[44.5]     pūjayāmāsa dharmātmā rāmo vaikhānasān munīn //" iti [Vāsiṣṭharāmāyaṇa]
[44.6]     vaikhānasānām pañcakālaparāyaṇatvam

     [pañcakālaparāyaṇasya lakṣaṇam]

[44.7]     śāṇḍilyasmṛtau: "ye pāvayanti dharaṇīṃ caraṇaiḥ pāñcakālikāḥ /
[44.8]     darśanāt sparśanāt teṣāṃ kṛtārthās sarvajantavaḥ // [Śāṇḍilyasmṛti.]
[44.9]     ijyāmadhye tathā home yoge ca japakarmaṇi /
[44.10]     āgataṃ pañcakālajñaṃ sampūjyair vācayet param // [Śāṇḍilyasmṛti.]
[44.11]     ye toṣayanty avirataṃ pañcakālaparāyaṇān /
[44.12]     sakāmās tatphalaṃ yānti niṣkāmāḥ paramaṃ padam // [Śāṇḍilyasmṛti]
[44.13]     sadāhitāgnayo ye ca śāntāś śūdrānnavarjitaḥ /
[44.14]     mām arcayanti madbhaktās tebhyo dattam ihākṣayam // [Śāṇḍilyasmṛti.]
[44.15]     dvādaśākṣaratattvajñaś caturvyūhavibhāgavit /
[44.16]     acchidrapañcakālajñas sa vipras tārayiṣyati //" [Śāṇḍilyasmṛti]

     [vaikhānasānām dvādaśākṣaratattvajñatvam]

[44.17]     yathā:
[44.18]     dvādaśākṣaratattvajña iti. dvādaśākṣaratattvāni.
[44.19]     "cijjīvaḥ prakṛtir buddhir manas sattvādayo guṇāḥ /
[44.20]     vyomāgnimarutaś cāpo varṇānāṃ tattvam īritam //" ity uktāni. [PādmaS caryāpāda 24.19]

     [vaikhānasānām caturvyūhavibhāgajñatvam]

[44.21]     caturvyūhavibhāgavit iti

     [vaikhānasapāñcarātrayoḥ vyūhacatuṣṭaye saṃjñāvaiṣamyam]

[44.22]     "puruṣañ ca tatas satyam acyutañ ca yudhiṣṭhira / [MBh 14, App. 4.1659]
[44.23]     aniruddhañ ca māṃ prāhur vaikhānasavido janāḥ // [MBh 14, App. 4.1660]
[44.24]     anye tv evaṃ vijānanti māṃ rājan pāñcarātrikāḥ / [MBh 14, App. 4.1661]
[44.25]     vāsudevañ ca rājendra saṅkarṣaṇam athāpi vā // [MBh 14, App. 4.1662]




[45.1]     pradyumnañ cāniruddhañ ca caturmūrtiṃ pracakṣate / [MBh 14, App. 4.1663]
[45.2]     etāś cānyāś ca rājendra saṃjñābhedena mūrtayaḥ // [MBh 14, App. 4.1664]
[45.3]     viddhi me 'rcāntarāṇy eva mām evañ cārcayed budhaḥ //" [MBh 14, App. 4.1665]
[45.4]     ityādy uktānāṃ caturṇāṃ vyūhānāṃ vibhāgāvit.

     [vāsudevasya daivikamānuṣabhedena dvaividhyam]

[45.5]     evaṃ vaikhānase daivikamānuṣabhedena vāsudevo dvividhaḥ pratipādyate. yathā -
[45.6-8]     khile: "athordhvaṃ vāsudevasya mānuṣasya vidhiṃ paraṃ". ity ārabhya "mānuṣyavapuṣaṃ devaṃ dvibhujaṃ śaṅkhacakriṇam" ityādinā rukmiṇīpradyumnāniruddhasāmbabrahmagaruḍādiyutaṃ mānuṣavāsudevaṃ nirvarṇya punaḥ:
[45.9]     "daivikaṃ vāsudevaṃ taṃ pravakṣyāmy ānupūrvyaśaḥ /
[45.10]     somacchandavimānaṃ vā bṛhadvṛttam athāpi vā //
[45.11]     caturbhujadharaṃ devaṃ śaṅkhacakradharaṃ param /
[45.12]     abhayaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ vāmaṃ kaṭyavalambitam //
[45.13]     kirīṭādisamastaiś ca bhūṣaṇair api bhūṣitam /
[45.14]     raktāmbaradharaṃ devaṃ daśātālena mānataḥ //
[45.15]     ubhe devyāv ubhe pārśve pūrvavat kārayed budhaḥ /
[45.16]     balabhadrādipūrvoktaṃ sāyudhaṃ vā nirāyudham //
[45.17]     tattad devībis hier tnoch telugu vergleichensamāyuktaṃ vinā vā samyag ācaret /
[45.18]     revatī rohiṇī caiva ramācendukarīti ca //
[45.19]     raktaṃ nīlaṃ tathā śyāmaṃ pītavarṇaṃ samācaret /
[45.20]     kirīṭamakuṭādyuktās sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ //
[45.21]     evaṃ puṣpadharaṃ kuryād ekañ caiva prasāritam /
[45.22]     devyā yuktaṃ vinā vāpi dvimārgaṃ samyag ācaret //"
[45.23-24]     ity ārabhya "evaṃ daivikamārgan tu sthāpanārambham ācared" ityādinā daivikaḥ vāsudevaḥ pradarśitaḥ.





     [vaikhānasetarasūtriṇāṃ pañcakālaparāyaṇatvābhavāḥ]

[46.1-5]     itthaṃ vāsudevādīnāṃ daivikamānuṣabhedena dvaividhyasya, "puruṣaṃ paramapuruṣaṃ paramātmānaṃ paraṃ brahmāṇam" ityādinā pratipāditānāṃ caturṇāṃ puruṣādīnāṃ mūrtivibhāgasya ca śrīvaikhānasaśāstre pratipādanāt, etas sarvavibhāgajña eva caturvyūhavibhāgavid ity anenocyate. ācchidrapañcakālajña iti:
[46.6]     "prātaḥkāle 'bhigamanam upādānaṃ tataḥ param /
[46.7]     madhyāhna ijyāṃ kurvīta svādhyāyañ cāparāhṇake /
[46.8]     yogaṃ sāyāhnakāle tu pañcakālā udāhṛtāḥ //" [VA ]
[46.9]     iti vāsādhikāre pratipāditapañcakālaparāyaṇam adhikṛtya prakṛttāni -
[46.10-14]     "ye pāvayanti dharaṇīṃ" "ijyāmadhye tathāhome" "ye toṣayanty avirataṃ" iti vacanāni, sāmanyena pañcakālaparāyaṇasya darśanasparśanādibhis sarveṣāṃ pāvanatāṃ kṛtārthatāṃ, ijyāyogādisamayeṣu cāgatasya tasya pūjanāntaraṃ śeṣakarmācaraṇañ ca pratipādayanti, etādṛśaḥ pañcakālaparāyaṇaḥ kīdṛśā ity ākaṅkṣāyāṃ "dvādaśākṣaratattvajña" ityādinā "acchidrapañcakālajña" ity antena tallakṣaṇam ucyate.
[46.15-17]     īdṛśācchidrapañcakālaparāyaṇā vaikhānasā eva. vaikhānasaśāstra eva pañcakālavibhāgasya pratipāditatvāt. svasvasūtre 'nuktatvād āpastambīyādayas tu na. pañcakālapratipādanarahitasūtrāntaraniṣṭhānāṃ:
[46.18]     "brāhme muhūrte buddhyeta dharmārthāv anucintayan /" ity ārabhya
[46.19]     "dvitīye ca tathā bhāge vedābhyāso vidhīyate //
[46.20]     tṛtīye ca tathā bhāge poṣyavargārthacintanam /
[46.21]     bhāge caturthe kurvīta snānam ambhasy akṛtrime //
[46.22]     pañcame tu tathā bhāge saṃvibhāgo yathārhataḥ /
[46.23]     itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ ṣaṣṭaṃ saptamam abhyaset /
[46.24]     aṣṭame lokayātrāñ ca vicārya ca gṛhī tataḥ //"





[47.1-2]     ity antena dakṣādismṛtyantareṣu brāhmaṇajāteḥ sāmānyena tattatkāleṣu kartavyatvena pratipāditakarmācaraṇa eva yathāyogyaṃ yogyatāsambhavāt.
[47.3]     anyathā
[47.4]     "vidharmaḥ paradharmaś ca ābhāsa upa vā cchalaḥ /
[47.5]     adharmaśākhāḥ pañcemā dharmajño 'dharmavattyajet //
[47.6]     dharmabādho vidharmas syāt paradharmo 'nyacoditaḥ /
[47.7]     upadharmas tu pāṣaṇḍo dambhovāṃśasurbhiśchalaḥ (?) /
[47.8]     yas tv icchayā kṛtaṃ pumbhir ābhāso hy āśramād bahiḥ //".
[47.9]     iti bhāgavatavacanoktaparadharmāśrayaṇadoṣaprasaṅgaḥ.
[47.10]     "śreyān svadharmo viguṇaḥ paradharmāt svanuṣṭhitāt /
[47.11]     svadharme nidhanaṃ śreyaḥ paradharmo bhayāvahaḥ //" [MBh 6.25.35]
[47.12]     iti bhagavadvacanavirodhaś ca.

     [sūtrāntaranuṣṭhānāṃ pāñcarātrānuyāyināñ ca devalakatvam]

[47.13-19]     kiñca tatsūtreṣu dvādaśākṣaratattvādipratipādanam api nāsti. evaṃ "sati kuḍye citrakarme"ti nyāyena yajñopavītadhāraṇasandhyopāsanabhagavadārādhanādividhipratipādanarahitasūtrāntaraniṣṭhānāṃ, tathā śrīmannārāyaṇasya samānatvena rudrādidevatāntarārādhanavidhipratipādakasūtraniṣṭhānāñ ca caturvyūhavibhāgajñānāsambhavāt bhagavadārādhanasvarūpajñānābhāvena pañcakālaparāyaṇatvādigandhaleśo 'pi na sambhavati. sūtrāntaroktamārgeṇa vā pañcarātroktamārgeṇa vā bhagavadārādhanaṃ kurvato 'nadhikāriṇo devalakatvaṃ pratipādyate.

     [pāñcarātre durgādidevatāntarārcanapratipādanam]

[47.20]     tathā hi - pañcarātre viṣvaksenasaṃhitāyāṃ nāradaṃ prati viṣvaksenoktiḥ:
[47.21]     "idan tu tava vakṣyāmi guhyād guhyatamaṃ mune /
[47.22]     yo 'sau nārayaṇas sākṣāt sa hi vighneśa ucyate // [ViṣvaksenaS 10.114]
[47.23]     yo vai vighneśa ity uktas sa vai nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ // [Viṣvaksena.S 10.115ab]
[47.24]     naiva bhedaṃ vijānanti munayas tattvadarśinaḥ //" ity ārabhya [ViṣvaksenaS 10.116ab]




[48.1]     "kuryāt pāśāṅkuśau vāpi śaṅkhacakrāv athāpi vā /
[48.2]     ākhuṃ vāpi khagendraṃ vā tasya vāhanam ācaret // [ViṣvaksenaS ]
[48.3]     nārāyaṇāśakatvāc cāvyāvṛttatvān mahāmune /
[48.4]     vīśas tadvāhanaṃ proktaṃ ākhuṃ vāpi samācaret // [Viṣvaksena.S ]
[48.5]     tasmāc chriyañ ca durgāñ ca vāṇīṃ vighneśam eva ca /
[48.6]     svatantreṇārcayed dhīmān sarvakāryārthasiddhaye //" ityādi ca dṛśyate. [ViṣvaksenaS ]
[48.7-10]     devatāntarāṇāṃ aṅgabhāvenārcanaṃ na niṣiddhyate. "svatantrabuddhyā kurvan vai brāhmaṇo narakaṃ vrajet" ityādi vacanaiḥ aṅgatvena vinā svātantryeṇāṅgivyatiriktadevatāntarārādhanaṃ niṣiddhyate. tathāvidhaniṣiddhadevatāntarārcanapratipādakaśāstraniṣṭhasya pañcakālaparāyaṇatvaṃ na sambhavati.

     [paramaikāntinām eva pañcakālaparāyaṇatvam]

[48.11]     "yair iṣṭaḥ pañcakālajñair harir ekāntibhir naraiḥ /
[48.12]     nūnaṃ tatra mato devo yathā tair vāgudīritaḥ //" ity uktarītyā

     [vaikhānasavyatiriktānāṃ paramaikāntitvābhāvaḥ]

[48.13-15]     paramaikāntitvāsambhave tad(pañcakālaparāyaṇatvā)sambhavāt. paramaikāntitvañ ca bhagavadekaparatvam eva. tac ca svātantryeṇānyadevatāyājināṃ vaikhānasavyatiriktānāṃ hi na sambhavati.
[48.16-17]     atra "yair iṣṭaḥ pañcakālajñair" ity anena pañcakālavyatiriktakālāntarapratipādakaśāstraniṣṭhānāṃ vyavṛttiḥ. "ekāntibhir narair" ity anena
[48.18]     "viprā vaikhānasākhyā ye te bhaktās tattvam ucyate // [PauṣkaraS 36.260cd]
[48.19]     ekāntinas susattvasthā dehāntaṃ nānyayājinaḥ // [PauṣkaraS 36.261ab]
[48.20-23]     ityādi pauṣkarasaṃhitāvacanānusāreṇa svātantryeṇa durgādidevatāntarārcanapratipādakapāñcarātraśāstraniṣṭhānāṃ vyāvṛttiḥ. "nūnam atra mato deva" ity anena - "yatra vaikhānasā viprā yatra santi gavāṃ gaṇāḥ /
[48.24]     yatra bilvāḥ palāśāś ca tatra sannihito hariḥ //"
[48.25-26]     ity asyārtho jñāpyate iti "yair iṣṭa" iti kṛtsnam api vacanaṃ vaikhānasaparam ity evāvagamyate.



     [pāñcarātriṇām api pañcakālaparāyaṇatvam ity ākṣepaḥ parihāraś ca]

[49.1]     nanu:
[49.2]     brahmā: "pañcakālavidhijñānaprāśastyaṃ bhagavann iha /
[49.3]     kathitaṃ pañca ke kālā vidhayaś cāpi pañca ke // [PādmaS caryāpāda 13.1]
[49.4]     mahyaṃ jijñāsamānāya kathayasva yathātatham /
[49.5]     na ced rahasyam atyantaṃ yad ahaṃ pṛṣṭavān iha // [PādmaS caryāpāda 13.2]
[49.6]     śrībhagavān:

     [pāñcarātroktam abhigamanam]

[49.7]     ādyaṃ karmābhigamanam upādānaṃ tataḥ param /
[49.8]     ijyā tapaś ca svādhyāyas tathā yogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ // [PādmaS caryāpāda 13.3]
[49.9]     pañcaite vidhayas teṣāṃ kālāḥ pañcaiva te kramāt /
[49.10]     kalyāṇācaraṇāntaṃ yat karmajātaṃ caturmukha // [Pādma.S caryāpāda 13.4]
[49.11]     utthānādikramād etad abhiyānam udīritam /
[49.12]     brāhme muhūrte buddhyeta dhyāyan nārāyaṇaṃ param // [Pādma.S caryāpāda 13.5]
[49.13]     utthāyāsīta śayane kīrtayan nāma vaiṣṇavam /
[49.14]     krameṇa sṛṣṭvā tattvāni deham utpādya tattvavit // [Pādma.S caryāpāda 13.6]
[49.15]     svasya dehe ṣaḍaṅgāni mantram uccārya mānasam //" [PādmaS caryāpāda 13.7]
[49.16]     ityādinā abhigamanam upakramya
[49.17]     "añjanālepanais sragbhiḥ vāsobhir bhūṣaṇais tathā // [Pādma.S caryāpāda 13.29ab]
[49.18]     alaktakarasādyaiś ca tāmbūlair mukhaśodhanaiḥ /
[49.19]     upeto maṅgalair anyair nayed abhigamakriyām //" [PādmaS caryāpāda 13.30]
[49.20]     ity abhigamanam uktā

     [pāñcarātroktam upādānam]

[49.21]     "upādadyāt tataḥ pūjā- sādhanāni yathātatham /
[49.22]     puṣpāṇi phalamūlāni vividhāny oṣadhīr api // [Pādma.S caryāpāda 13.31]
[49.23]     dadhyādi ca haviryogyaṃ taṇḍulādi guḍādi ca /
[49.24]     snānīyāni ca vastrāṇi svādūni salilāni ca // [Pādma.S caryāpāda 13.32]





[50.1]     darbhān parṇāni samidho yathāśakti yathāvasu /
[50.2]     āhṛtya yājñiyān daivān pūjāsthāne niveśayet // [PādmaS caryāpāda 13.33]
[50.3]     nītvopādānasamayam itthaṃ tad anupūjayet /"
[50.4]     ity upādānam uktam.

     [pāñcarātroktā ijyā]

[50.5]     "prāpte madhyāhnasamaye snānaṃ kuryād yathāvidhi //" [PādmaS caryāpāda 13.34]
[50.6]     ity ārabhya
[50.7]     "uttīrya karma nikhilaṃ madhyāhnasamayocitam / [PādmaS caryāpāda 13.41cd]
[50.8]     kṛtvā yajeta deveśaṃ homāntaṃ kamalāsana // [Pādma.S caryāpāda 13.42ab]
[50.9]     ijyāyās samayas tasyāḥ kathitaḥ kamalāsana //" [PādmaS caryāpāda 13.66ab]
[50.10]     iti bhagavadyajanam uktvā

     [pāñcarātroktaḥ svādhyāyaḥ]

[50.11]     "mandire vā harer nadyās tīre vāmarabhūmiṣu // [Pādma.S caryāpāda 13.66cd]
[50.12]     vivikte vipine vāpi parvate vā gṛhe 'pi vā /
[50.13]     ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni vidyamānāny anekadhā // [PādmaS caryāpāda 13.67]
[50.14]     śākhābhedair mūlaśākhām ekāyanasamāhvayām /
[50.15]     trayīmayīm adhīyīta sukhāsīnas samāhitaḥ //" [PādmaS caryāpāda 13.68]
[50.16]     svādhyāyam uktvā

     [pāñcarātroktaḥ yogaḥ]

[50.17]     "tataḥ paścimasandhyāyāṃ prāptāyāṃ tatra coditam // [PādmaS caryāpāda 13.72cd]
[50.18]     japahomādikaṃ sarvaṃ kṛtvā paramapūruṣam /
[50.19]     arcayitvā yathānyāyyaṃ yathāpūrvam aśeṣataḥ // [PādmaS caryāpāda 13.73]
[50.20]     bhuktvānnaṃ viśya śayane samutthāya mahāniśi /
[50.21]     ācamya prayato bhūtvā dhyātvā paramapūruṣam // [PādmaS caryāpāda 13.74]
[50.22]     yogāsane samāsīno yuñjītātmānam ātmanā /
[50.23]     yathoktena prakāreṇa yathāśakti caturmukha // [Pādma.S caryāpāda 13.75]
[50.24]     sahārakramam āśritya tattvāny ātmani saṃharet /
[50.25]     ātmānañ cāpi hṛtpadme paramātmani niṣṭhite // [Pādma.S caryāpāda 13.76]





[51.1]     saṃhared itthato yogāt svāpaṃ kleśāpahaṃ vrajet /
[51.2]     ity eṣa kathito brahman yogaḥ kālaś ca pañcamaḥ // [Pādma.S caryāpāda 13.77]
[51.3]     pañcaite samayāḥ pañcavidhayas teṣu darśitāḥ /
[51.4]     ittham eteṣu kāleṣu darśitaiḥ karmabhir naraḥ // [PādmaS caryāpāda 13.78]
[51.5]     ārādhanaṃ bhagavataḥ kurvan naivāvasīdati /
[51.6]     varṣeṣu dvādaśasu evam anutiṣṭhan samāhitaḥ // [Pādma.S caryāpāda 13.79]
[51.7]     kriyākalāpam akhilaṃ yāti sāyujyasampadam /
[51.8]     ṣaṭsu varṣeṣu sārūpyaṃ sāmīpyaṃ triṣu niścitam // [PādmaS caryāpāda 13.80]
[51.9]     sālokyaṃ phalam ekasmin vatsare nātra saṃśayaḥ //" [PādmaS caryāpāda 13.81ab]
[51.10-11]     iti pādme caryāpāde trayodaśe 'dhyāye avicchinnatayā pañcakālānāṃ pratipāditatvāt teṣām apy acchidrapañcakālaparāyaṇatvaṃ sambhavatīti cet - tad asat.

     [pāñcarātriṇām aniyataparimitacchidradrapañcakālaparāyaṇatvam]

[51.12]     tatraiva:
[51.13]     "pūtyūṣam ardharātrañ ca prātar madhyaṃdināni ca /
[51.14]     pañcakālā ime proktās tataḥ kālacatuṣṭaye //
[51.15]     eteṣu hīnāḥ pratyūṣaṃ (?) vijñeyāś caturānana //"
[51.16-20]     ity abhigamanādīnām ekarūpeṇa vinā nyūnātiriktakālatvenoktatvāt "kālaṃ madhyandinacchidrapañcakālaparāyaṇair" ity āgamasiddhānte "sāntarālam anuṣṭhānaṃ pañcakāloditaṃ tathā" iti tantrasiddhānte ca chidrapañcakālaparatvasyoktatvāt, kālacatuṣṭayapratipādanena niyatapañcakālaparāyaṇatvābhāvāt, dvādaśavarṣam ārabhya ekavarṣaparyantaṃ parimitapañcakālaparatvasyoktatvāt dvādaśavarṣād ūrdhvaṃ pañcakālaparatvābhāvāc ca.
[51.21]     tathā, mārkaṇḍeye
[51.22]     "mahāniśā tu vijñeyā rātrer madhyaṃ dvitīyayoḥ /
[51.23]     tasyāṃ snānaṃ na kurvīta samyag ācamanaṃ tathā //" [MarkaṇḍeyaP]





[52.1]     ity ācamanasya mahāniśāyāṃ niṣedhāt.
[52.2]     "yāmadvayaṃ śayānas tu brahmabhūyāya kalpate //"
[52.3-4]     iti dharmaśāstroktanidrākāle yogasyāyuktatvāc ca. yogakālasyārdharātrikatve svādhyāyakālād vyavahitatvena chidrapāñcakālikatvāpātāc ca.
[52.5-6]     kālacatuṣtvāsyaivoktatvena abhigamanādiṣv ekasya lopasambhavena aniyatapañcakālaparasya pañcakālaparāyaṇaśabdābhilāpāsambhavāc ca.
[52.7]     tathā:
[52.8]     "kliśyantīha suṣuptānām indriyāṇi dravanti ca /
[52.9]     aṅgāni samatāṃ yānti uttamāny adhamais saha //"
[52.10]     iti dharmaśāstreṣu prātar ārabhya sāyaṅkālaparyantam eva karmācaraṇakālatvena pratipādanāt.
[52.11]     tathā:
[52.12]     "atyantamalinaḥ kāyo navacchidrasamanvitaḥ /
[52.13]     sravaty eva divārātraṃ prātas snānaṃ viśodhanam //
[52.14]     asnātvā nācaret karma japahomādi kiñcana /
[52.15]     snātvādhikārī bhavati daive pitrye ca karmaṇi //"
[52.16-20]     iti smṛteḥ snānāt pūrvaṃ tattvasṛṣṭer ayuktatvāc ca. pretaprāyasya saṃhṛtatattvasya svāpayogyatāsambhavāc ca. tasmāt "abbhakṣo vāyubhakṣa" ityādiśabdavadavadhāraṇagarbhasya pāñcakālikaśabdasya aniyataparimitapāñcakālikeṣu pāñcarātrikeṣu prayogāsaṃbhavād aniyataparimitachidrapāñcakālikāḥ pāñcarātriṇo na niyatāchidrapañcakālaparāyaṇavaikhānasatulyā bhavitum ahantīti siddham.

     [devatāpūjakasāmānasya devalakatvam ity ākṣepaparihāraḥ]

[52.21]     nanu:
[52.22]     "yo devaṃ pūjayed vipro vittārthī vatsaratrayam /
[52.23]     sa vai devalako nāma havyakavyabahiṣkṛtaḥ //"
[52.24-53.2]      iti devatāpūjakasya devalakatvaṃ sambhavatīti cet - tad asat. sāmānyataḥ devatārādhanaṃ ye kurvanti te devalakā iti vā? uta śrutismṛtītihāsapurāṇādiṣu mukhyādhikāritvena pratipāditā apīti vā?. sāmānyataḥ devatārādhanaṃ ye kurvanti te iti cet - tarhi gṛhadevatāpūjakānām api devalakatvaprasaṅgaḥ. kiñca:


     [vaikhānasānām devalakatvābhāvaḥ]

[53.3]     "brahmacārī gṛhasthaś ca vipro vaikhānasas tathā /
[53.4]     kurvanti nijakarmāṇi viṣṇum eva yajanti te //"
[53.5-11]     iti sandhyopāsanādīnāṃ bhagavadārādhanarūpatvoktyā teṣāñ ca tyāgas sambhavati. atas sāmānyataḥ iti vaktum ayuktam. śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣu mukhyādhikāritvena pratipāditā devalakāḥ iti cet - tad asat. "'agnir vai devānām avamo viṣṇuḥ paramas tadantareṇa sarvā anyā devatā'; iti brāhmaṇam. tasmād gṛhe paramaṃ viṣṇuṃ pratiṣṭhāpya sāyaṃ prātar homānte 'rcayati" iti vaikhānasasūtre, "pravaḥ pāntam andhaso dhiyāyate maheśūrāya viṣṇave cārcata" iti ṛgbrāhmaṇam anusṛtya viṣṇupradhānatayā "sa vā eṣa puruṣaḥ pañcadhā pañcātmā" ityādiśrutyuktaviṣṇvādipañcamūrtīnām ārādhanasya pratipāditatvāt.
[53.12-13]     āśvamedhike "kathaṃ tvam arcanīyo 'sī"tyādeḥ, vṛddhamanau "vedāntavedibhir" ityādeś coktatvāt.
[53.14-15]     evam eva pāñcarātraśaivaśilpajyautiṣādiṣu utkṛṣṭamukhyādhikāripratipādakānāṃ vacanānāṃ vaiyarthyaprasaṅgāt tanmūlabhūtaśrutismṛtipurāṇādīnām aprāmāṇyaprasaṅgo duṣpariharaḥ.

     [vaikhānasānām bhagavaddravyopabhogādau doṣābhāvaḥ]

[53.16-17]     evaṃ ca pramāṇabhūteṣu śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣu pratipāditānām ācārādīnāṃ tyāgaḥ prasajyet, niṣphalatvāt. nanu paradravyoṇālayārcanaṃ kurvatāṃ devalakatvam iti cet na.
[53.18-19]     śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣu tattacchāstreṣu ca ālayārcakānāṃ mukhyādhikāritvena taddravyopabhogārhatvena ca pratipādanāt.
[53.20]     yathā - marīciproktāyām ānandasaṃhitāyāṃ vikhanasotpattyādikaṃ pratipādya:
[53.21]     "tathā tvadanujīvitve tvaddravyānubhave sati /
[53.22]     yad bhaved doṣa utpanna iti cintākulo 'smy aham //" [ĀS 4.77]
[53.23]     iti bhagavaddravyopajīvanadoṣabhīroḥ vikhanasaḥ bhagavantaṃ prati praśne -
[53.24]     "athovāca hṛṣīkeśo bhīruṃ taṃ munisattamaṃ / [ĀS 4.78ab]
[53.25]     vaikhānasānāṃ tad doṣo nāsti matkṛtakarmaṇām // [ĀS 4.83ab]





[54.1]     maddravyaṃ havyakavyārthe dānābhyāgatapūjane / [ĀS 4.84cd]
[54.2]     mukhyam evāstu bhavatāṃ sadā matkarma kurvatām // [Ā.S 4.85ab]

     [vaikhānasānām bhagavadvigrahavikraye 'pi doṣābhāvaḥ]

[54.3]     kim ebhir bahubhir vākyair anyat te kathayāmy aham // [ĀS 4.85cd]
[54.4]     maddravyakṣetrabimbānām ālayānāṃ tathāpadi /
[54.5]     vikrīṇanādikāryeṣu nāsti doṣo madājñayā // [ĀS 4.87]
[54.6]     tasmād bhavān abhimatas sarvaṃ karma sadā kuru // [ĀS ]
[54.7]     madīyadhanabhogena matkriyālopatas tava /
[54.8]     maccharīratayā satyam apacāro na vidyate //" [ĀS 4.86]
[54.9]     iti bhagavadvacanodāharaṇena bhagavaddravyopabhogādiṣu doṣābhāvaḥ pratipāditaḥ.
[54.10-14]     atra "ahaṃ bhaktaparādhīno hy asvatantra iva dvija" ityādivacanānusāreṇārcakaparādhīnatāṃ darśayituṃ, bhagavatprītiviṣayīkṛtānāṃ vaikhānasānāṃ taddravyopabhogādiṣu doṣagandho nāstīti pratipādanāvasare "maddravyaṃ kṣetrabimbādī"tyādinā kaimutikanyāyam abhipretya bhagavadvigrahavikraye kṛte 'pi doṣo nāstīty ucyate. tāvatā na tad abhipretam.
[54.15-16]     nanv evam api devadravyopabhogadoṣas sāmānyataḥ mukhyāmukhyādhikāriṣu sarveṣv āpadyate eva iti cet na.

     [māṃsabhakṣane narakapatanam]

[54.17]     "ye bhakṣayanti māṃsāni sattvānāṃ jīvitaiṣiṇām /
[54.18]     bhakṣyante te 'pi tais sarvair iti brahmābravīt svayam // [MBh 13.117.33]
[54.19]     māṃ sa bhakṣayitām utra yasya māṃsam ihādmy aham /
[54.20]     etan māṃsasya māṃsatvaṃ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ // [MBh 13.117.34]
[54.21]     na hi māṃsaṃ tṛṇāt kaṣṭhād upalād vāpi jayate /
[54.22]     hatvā jantuṃ bhaven māṃsaṃ tasmāt tat parivarjayet // [MBh 13.116.26]
[54.23]     hantā caivānumantā ca viśas tā krayavikrayī /
[54.24]     saṃskartā copakartā ca khādakaś cāṣṭa ghātukāḥ // [MBh 13.116.47]





[55.1]     dhanena krāyako hanti khādakaś copabhogataḥ /
[55.2]     ghātuko vadhabandhābhyām ity eṣa trividho vadhaḥ // [MBh 13.116.38]
[55.3]     svamāṃsaṃ paramāṃsena yo vardhayitum icchati /
[55.4]     nāradaḥ prāha dharmātmā narake sa vipacyate //" [MBh 13.117.10]

     [kutracid dharmasyāpy adharmaṃ, adharmasyāpi dharmatvañ ca]

[55.5-6]     ityādi vacanaiḥ māṃsabhakṣaṇena narakapatanasmaraṇāt bhagavatprītyarthaṃ kriyamāṇeṣu yajñeṣv api māṃsabhakṣaṇasattvāt yājñikānām api narakapatanaṃ sambhavatīti yāgasyāpi tyāgaprasaṅgāt.
[55.7]     "tasmāc chāstraṃ pramāṇaṃ te kāryākāryavyavasthitau /
[55.8]     jñātvā śāstravidhānoktaṃ karma kartum ihārhasi //" [MBh 6.38.24]
[55.9-12]     iti bhagavadvacanāt śāstroktānāṃ karmaṇāṃ doṣo nāstīti cet. "maddravyopabhogādau doṣo nāstī"ti bhagavatā pratipāditvāt prakṛte 'pi doṣo nāsty eva. "vacanāt pravṛttir vacanān nivṛttir" iti khalu śiṣṭoktiḥ. evaṃ kutracid dharmo 'dharmaḥ adharmaś ca dharmo bhavati.
[55.13]     yathā
[55.14]     "ukte 'nṛte bhavet kiñcit prāṇināṃ prāṇarakṣaṇam /
[55.15]     anṛtaṃ tatra satyaṃ syāt satyam atrānṛtaṃ bhavet //
[55.16]     kāminīṣu vivāheṣu gavāṃ pīḍāsu bādhane /
[55.17]     brāhmaṇābhyavapattau ca śapathe nāsti pātakam //"
[55.18-19]     "yadbrāhmaṇaś cābrāhmaṇaś ca praśnam eyātāṃ brāhmaṇāyādhibrūyāt yadbrāhmaṇāyādhyātmane 'dhyāha yad brāhmaṇaṃ parāhātmānaṃ parāha tasmād brāhmaṇo na parocyaḥ" ity śrutiś ca.
[55.20-21]     śrautasūtre ca: "sarva evam abhivādayanti nābhivādayati na juhoty anyatra somāṅgebhyaḥ" ityādi pratipādyate.
[55.22]     "sarvasvaharaṇe bhāryāveśyayoḥ (?) prāṇasaṃśaye /
[55.23]     godvijārthe vivāde ca śapathe nāsti pātakam //"
[55.24]     ityādi smṛtiś ca.
[55.25]     evaṃ ca śāstroktaprakāreṇa bhagavadarcanaṃ kurvatāṃ taddravyopabhoge na doṣaḥ.





     [devalakatvalakṣaṇavicāraḥ]

[56.1-2]     kiñca - kiṃ devalakatvaṃ jātiparam, uta karmaparam? jātiparam iti vaktuṃ na śakyate. tathānuktatvāt. icchayā kalpitum aśakyatvāc ca.

     [avihitakarmakartṛtvam eva devalakatvam]

[56.3-4]     atha karmaparam iti cet. vihitakarmaparam, uta avihitakarmaparam? vihitakarmaparam iti vaktum aśakyam - śrutismṛtītihāsasūtrapurāṇādīnām apramāṇyaprasaṅgāt.
[56.5]     vihitadharmaparatvenānuktatvāt.
[56.6]     "śrutismṛtī mamaivājñā yas tām ullaṅghya vartate /
[56.7]     ājñāc chedī mama drohī madbhakto 'pi na vaiṣṇavaḥ //"

     [paradravyakṛtasyāpy ārādhanasya nirdoṣatvam]

[56.8]     iti bhagavadājñābhaṅgadoṣāc ca. evaṃ ca avihitakarmaparam iti hi pariśiṣyate.
[56.9-10]     nanu - paradravyeṇa kṛtaṃ bhagavadārādhanaṃ kratuvat parārtham eva bhavatīti cet maivam.
[56.11]     "anyadharmaparo vipro bhraṣṭo gacchaty adhogatim /
[56.12]     matkarmanirato vipro nādhaḥ patati kutracit //"
[56.13]     iti bhagavadvacanāt.
[56.14]     purāṇāntare: "svasminn arpitamātreṇa yena kenāpi karmaṇā /
[56.15]     tuṣṭo dadāti svapadam aho vatsalatā hareḥ //" iti.
[56.16]     kiñca:

     [dakṣiṇāpratigrahe doṣābhavaḥ]

[56.17]     "ekaviṃśatiniṣkantu dadyād ācāryadakṣiṇām /
[56.18]     ṛtvijān tu tadardhaṃ syāt tadardham itarasya ca //"
[56.19]     iti dakṣiṇādānaṃ pratipādyate.
[56.20]     nanu - "pratigraheṇa viprasya brāhmaṃ tejo vinaśyati //" iti manuvacanāt [ManuDhŚ 4.186cd]
[56.21-25]     "pratigraheṇa tejo hi viprāṇāṃ śāmyate" ity ānuśāsanikavacanāc ca pratigraheṇa brahmatejonāśanaṃ smaryate. śrūyate pratigrahe prāyaścittam api. "yo yājayati prati vā gṛhṇāti yājayitvā pratigṛhya vānaśnaṃs tris svādhyāyam adhīyīta trirātraṃ sāvitrīṃ gāyatrīm anvatirecayati varo dakṣiṇā vareṇaiva varaṃ spṛṇoty ātmā hi varaḥ" iti.
[56.25]     ataḥ pratigrahe doṣo 'stīti cet - na.




     [harismaraṇasya mokṣapradatvam]

[57.1]     "trāyante khalu nātyantam anyadharmās svanuṣṭitāḥ /
[57.2]     api matkarma viguṇaṃ trāyate mahato bhayāt //
[57.3]     merumandaramātro 'pi rāśiḥ pāpasya karmaṇaḥ /
[57.4]     keśavaṃ vaidyam āsādya ab hier noch Telugu vergleichendurvyādhir iva naśyati //
[57.5]     nidhisthānaṃ khanan dveṣāt mṛdarthaṃ vāpnuyān nidhim /
[57.6]     ajñaḥ kāmāc ca doṣāc ca smṛtvaivaṃ mokṣabhāktathā //
[57.7]     dveṣiṇā vāprayatnena kṣipto 'gniḥ kakṣamādahet /
[57.8]     katham abhyarcito viṣṇuḥ na dahet sarvakilbiṣam //
[57.9]     yathājño vajrakāyas syāt spardhann api sudhāṃ piban /
[57.10]     evaṃ viruddhabhāvo 'pi mucyaty eva hariṃ smaran //" iti
[57.11]     nāradīye: "kṛtāpi dambhahāsyādyair yat sevā tārayej janān /
[57.12]     viphalā nānyakarmeva kṛpāluḥ ko 'nvataḥ param // [NāradaP.]
[57.13]     hāsyānādaramāyābhir api bhaktiḥ kṛtā tvayi /
[57.14]     nṛṇāṃ dadātīndrapadaṃ sāttvikānāṃ kim ucyate // [NāradaP]
[57.15]     vastusvabhāva evaiṣa yanmokṣāya harismṛtiḥ /
[57.16]     pūṣeva dhyāntanāśāya śśītaśāntyai yathānalaḥ // [NāradaP.]
[57.17]     saiṣā harismṛtiṛ daityaṃ krodhād api kṛtā satī /
[57.18]     ānayet sadgatiṃ vipraṃ sānugaṃ kimu varṇyate // [NāradaP.]
[57.19]     yathāmṛtārthaṃ yatatāṃ surāṇām abdhimanthane /
[57.20]     pārijātādikāny āsan phalāny aprārthitāny api // [NāradaP.]
[57.21]     evaṃ mokṣaikacittānāṃ yatatām īśasaṃsmṛtau /
[57.22]     bhavanti siddhayo divyāḥ puṇya puṇyānubandhi yat //" ityādi [NāradaP]
[57.23]     tatraiva: "surātithyarcanakṛte gurubhṛtyartham eva ca /
[57.24]     sarvataḥ pratigṛhṇīyāt na tu duṣyet svayaṃ tataḥ //" [NāradaP]





[58.1-2]     iti ca smaraṇāt. ataḥ śāstroktamārgeṇa bhagavadyajanavidhau pravṛttānāṃ tattatkarmasu dakṣiṇāpratigrahe kṛte 'pi na doṣaḥ.

     [ālayārcanāyāḥ mahābhāratādisaṃmatatvam]

[58.3]     gṛhārcanāvyatirekeṇālayārcanā bhāratādiṣu pratipāditā dṛśyate. yathā -
[58.4]     mahābhārate āśvamedhike "kathaṃ tvam arcanīyo 'sī"ty ādi. [MBh 14 App. 4.1652pr]
[58.5]     viṣṇudharmottare ṣaṣṭhe 'dhyāye:
[58.6]     "yas tu devagṛhasyārthaṃ prākāraṃ parikalpayet /
[58.7]     sa tu svargaṃ samāsadya vimānādhipatir bhavet // [Viṣṇudharmottara.P ]
[58.8]     yas tu devālayasyāgre śilādārubhir eva vā /
[58.9]     karoti toraṇaṃ ramyaṃ sa tu svargādhipo bhavet // [Viṣṇudharmottara.P ]
[58.10]     yas tu devālayaṃ viṣṇor dāruśailamṛdā tathā /
[58.11]     iṣṭakākalpitaṃ vāpi kuryāt tasya phalaṃ bahu // [Viṣṇudharmottara.P ]
[58.12]     ahanyahany aśvamedha- sahasrāṇi karoti yaḥ /
[58.13]     prāpnoti maṇḍapaṃ viṣṇoḥ yaḥ kārayati mānavaḥ // [Viṣṇudharmottara.P ]
[58.14]     keśavasya sa tallokam akṣayyaṃ pratipadyate /
[58.15]     pratimārthaṃ mahāviṣṇos sādhayed uttamāṃ śilām // [ViṣṇudharmottaraP ]
[58.16]     ṣaṣṭirvarṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate //" iti. [ViṣṇudharmottaraP ]
[58.17-19]     eteṣāṃ ca prākāratoraṇamaṇḍapavigrahaśilādīṇāṃ gṛhadevatāsvasaṃbhavaḥ śrīvaikhānasasaṃhitāsu pratipāditaḥ. prasaṅgād arcakamahimādīha kathyate.

     [arcakamāhātmyam]

[58.20]     bṛhannāradīye: "sa kadācin mahāpāpo jantūnāmantakopamaḥ //" [BṛhannāradaP]
[58.21]     ity ārabhya
[58.22]     "tasyopavanamadhyasthaṃ ramyaṃ keśavamandiram /
[58.23]     chāditaṃ hemakavacaiḥ dṛṣṭvā vyādho mudā yayau // [BṛhannāradaP]
[58.24]     harāmy atra suvarṇāni bahūnīti sa niścitaḥ /
[58.25]     jagāma viṣṇubhavanaṃ kīnāśaś cauryalolupaḥ // [BṛhannāradaP]

[59.1]     tatrāpaśyad dvijavaraṃ śāntaṃ tattvārthakovidam /
[59.2]     paricaryāparaṃ viṣṇor udaṅkaṃ tapasāṃ nidhim // [BṛhannāradaP]
[59.3]     ekāntinaṃ dayāluñ ca nisspṛhaṃ dhyānalolupam /
[59.4]     dṛṣṭvā taṃ lubdhako mene svakāryasyāntarāyinam // [BṛhannāradaP]
[59.5]     devasya dravyajātan tu samādātumanā niśi //" [BṛhannāradaP]
[59.6-7]     ityādināpṛthagālayārcakasadbhāvādikaṃ uktvā svakāryāntarāya bhūtārcakahiṃsāyāṃ pravṛttasya tasya maraṇam api pratipādya.

     [viṣṇupādodakamāhātmyam]

[59.8]     "udaṅkaḥ patitaṃ prekṣya lubdhakantu dayāparaḥ /
[59.9]     viṣṇupādodakenainam abhyaṣiñ canmahāmuniḥ //
[59.10]     haripādodakas parśāl lubdhako vītakalmaṣaḥ /
[59.11]     divyaṃ vimānamāruhya munim enam athābravīt //"
[59.12] iti bhagavatpādodakamāhātmyaṃ ca pratipāditam.
[59.13] tatraiva - yajñadhvajavītihotrasaṃvāde:

     [ālaye dīpasthāpanādeḥ phalam]

[59.14]     "sa kadācit tu kāmāndho rantukāmaḥ parastriyam /
[59.15]     śūnyaṃ pūjādibhir viṣṇor mandiraṃ prāptavān niśi //
[59.16]     tatra kāmopabhogārthaṃ śayituṃ tena kāminā /
[59.17]     svavastraprāntato brahman kṛtaṃ taddeśamārjanam //
[59.18]     yāvantaḥ pāṃsukaṇikāḥ tena sammārjitās tadā /
[59.19]     tāvaj janmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tadaiva kṣayam āgatam //
[59.20]     pradīpaḥ sthāpitas tatra suratārthaṃ dvijottama /
[59.21]     tenāpi tasya duṣkarma niśśeṣaṃ kṣayam āgatam //
[59.22]     avaśenāpi yatkarma kṛtvemāṃ siddhim āgataḥ /
[59.23]     bhaktimadbhiḥ praśāntaiś ca kiṃ punas samyagarcanāt //



     [ālayapradakṣiṇaphalam]

[60.1]     tasmāc chruṇuta viprendrāḥ devo nārāyaṇo 'vyayaḥ /
[60.2]     jñānato 'jñānato vāpi pūjakānāṃ vimuktidaḥ //"
[60.3]     tathā tatraiva - indrasudharmasaṃvāde:
[60.4]     "ahamāsaṃ purā śakra gṛdhraḥ pāpāvaśeṣataḥ /
[60.5]     sthitaś ca bhūmibhāge vai amedhyāmiṣabhojanaḥ //
[60.6]     ekadāhaṃ viṣṇugṛhe prākāre saṃsthitaḥ prabhoḥ /
[60.7]     patito vyādhaśastreṇa sāyaṃ viṣṇugṛhaṃ gate //
[60.8]     mayi kaṇṭhagataprāṇe kaścit śvā māṃsalolupaḥ /
[60.9]     jagraha māṃ svavaktreṇa śvabhir anyair abhidrutaḥ //
[60.10]     gataḥ pradakṣiṇākāraṃ viṣṇos tanmandiraṃ prabhoḥ /
[60.11]     tenaiva tuṣṭim āpannaḥ antarātmā jaganmayaḥ //
[60.12]     mama cāpi śunaś cāpi dattavān paramaṃ padam /
[60.13]     pradakṣiṇākāratabis hier noch Telugu vergleichenyā gatasya sadṛśaṃ phalam //
[60.14]     samprāptaṃ tu mayā śakra kiṃ punas samyag arcanāt /
[60.15]     ye 'rcayanti sadā bhaktyā nārāyaṇam anāmayam /
[60.16]     tān arcayanti vibudhā brahmādyā devatāgaṇāḥ //" iti

     [amedhyāni pañca]

[60.17]     evam āśvamedhike: "loke trīṇy apavitrāṇi pañcāmedhyāni bhārata / [MBh 13, App. 4.3249]
[60.18]     śvā ca śūdraś śvapākaś ca tryapavitrāṇi pāṇḍava / [MBh 13, App. 4.3250]
[60.19]     devalaḥ kukkuṭo yūpaḥ udakyā vṛṣalīpatiḥ //" [MBh 13, App. 4.3251]
[60.20]     pañcamedhyāni iti.

     [bhagavatpūjādyanadhikāriṇaḥ]

[60.21]     śrīvaikhānase: "sūtādipratilomāś ca pāṣaṇḍāḥ patitās tathā /
[60.22]     nāstikā bhinnamaryādās tathā vedavidūṣakāḥ //
[60.23]     pāparogayutāś caiva tathaiva gurunindakā /
[60.24]     arcanaṃ devadevasya havirdānañ ca vīkṣitum /





[61.1]     nārhanti tasmāt kurvīta dvāraṃ yavanikāvṛtam //"
[61.2-3]     iti pratipādanāt bhagavadarcanadarśanādiṣu yogyatārahitānāṃ nikṛṣṭānāṃ (devalakānāṃ) autkṛṣṭyaṃ na sambhavati.

     [advārakabhagavadyājinām utkṛṣṭatvam]

[61.4-6]     śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣūktaprakāreṇa kalpasūtre yeṣām advārakabhagavadyajanādhikāro vidhīyate te utkṛṣṭā jñeyāḥ. yathā śrutiḥ: "yathā kratur asmin loke bhavati tathetaḥ pretya bhavati" iti.
[61.7]     smṛtiś ca: "vedoktenaiva bhārgeṇa sarvabhūtahṛdi sthitam /
[61.8]     mām arcayanti ye bhaktās sāyujyaṃ yānti te mama //
[61.9]     tasmād yāvaj jano jīvet tāvat sampūjayed dharim /
[61.10]     pāpair na lipyate martyo harimandiram āpnuyāt //
[61.11]     jagat pavitrās te nityaṃ viṣṇum abhyarcayanti ye /
[61.12]     durvṛttā vā suvṛttā vā pūjanīyā viśeṣataḥ //"

     [vaikhānasānāṃ bhagavatprītipātratvam]

[61.13-16]     vyāsenapi ānuśāsanike (90. adhyāye) pātrakathanāvasare devalakānām apātratāṃ satkarmaniṣṭhānāṃ pātratāñ ca pratipādya svavacanadṛḍhīkaraṇārthaṃ "vaikhānasā vā ṛṣaya indrasya priyā āsan" iti bhagavatprītiviṣayāṇāṃ vaikhānasānāṃ vacanam api śrūyate iti pratipāditam. yathā:
[61.17]     "ṛṣīṇāṃ samayaṃ nityaṃ ye rakṣanti yudhiṣṭhira /
[61.18]     niścitāḥ sarvadharmajñās tān devā brāhmaṇān viduḥ // [MB.h 13.9.42]
[61.19]     svādhyāyaniṣṭhā ṛṣayo jñānaniṣṭhās tathaiva ca /
[61.20]     taponiṣṭhāś ca boddhavyāḥ karmaniṣṭhāś ca bhārata // [MBh 13.9.43]
[61.21]     kavyāni jñānaniṣṭhebhyaḥ pratiṣṭhāpyāni bhārata /
[61.22]     tatra ye brāhmaṇān ke cin na ca nindanti te varāḥ // [MBh 13.9.44]
[61.23]     ye tu nindanti jalpeṣu na tāñ śrāddheṣu bhojayet /
[61.24]     brāhmaṇā ninditā rājan hanyus tripuruṣaṃ kulam // [MBh 13.9.45]





[62.1]     vaikhānasānāṃ vacanam ṛṣīṇāṃ śrūyate nṛpa /
[62.2]     dūrād eva parīkṣeta brāhmaṇān vedapāragān /
[62.3]     priyo vā yadi vā dveṣyaḥ teṣu tac chrāddham āvapet // [MBh 13.9.46]
[62.4]     yaḥ sahasraṃ sahasrāṇāṃ bhojayed anṛcāṃ naraḥ /
[62.5]     ekas tān mantravit pūtaḥ sarvān arhati bhārata //" [MBh 13.9.47]

     [aṣṭākṣarādimantrajapaniṣṭhānāṃ mahimā]

[62.6-7]     evaṃ aṣṭākṣara dvādaśākṣara puruṣasūktādimantrajapaniṣṭhānāṃ darśanena brahmahā 'pi śuddhyatīti purāṇoktam. yathā:
[62.8]     padmapurāṇe: "sāṅgaṃ samantraṃ sanyāsaṃ sarṣicchandodhidaivatam /
[62.9]     sadīkṣāvidhi sadhyānaṃ sayantraṃ dvādaśākṣaram // [Padma.P ]
[62.10]     sāṣṭākṣarañ ca mantreśaṃ ye japanti narottamāḥ /
[62.11]     tān dṛṣṭvā brahmahā śuddhyet kiṃ punar vaiṣṇavas svayam //" iti [PadmaP ]
[62.12-14]     śruyate 'pi. "yo ha vai nārāyaṇasyāṣṭākṣaraṃ padam adhyeti anupabravas sarvam āyur eti vindate prājāpatyaṃ rāyaspoṣaṃ gaupatyaṃ tato 'mṛtatvam aśnute tato 'mṛtatvam aśnuta iti".
[62.15]     śrīpāñcarātre kapiñjalasaṃhitāyām:
[62.16]     "yājanādhyāpanayutaḥ śiṣyānugrahakārakaḥ /
[62.17]     ācārya iti vijñeyo mantratantraparāyaṇaḥ // [KapiñjalaS]
[62.18]     āśrame vā vane vā 'pi sa vaikhānasa ucyate /
[62.19]     grāmyadharmāṇi sarvāṇi varjayed vanavāsakaḥ //" iti. [KapiñjalaS]
[62.20]     yamasmṛtau: "yo 'nucānaṃ dvijaṃ martyo hatavān arthalobhataḥ /
[62.21]     sa vadet pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ jalasthaś cintayed dharim //"
[62.22-24]     iti kevalāṣṭākṣaramantrajapaniṣṭhānām apy evaṃ vidhāḥ prabhāvāḥ śrūyanta iti cet śrutismṛtivihitais tair eva mantraiḥ advārakabhagavadarcane mukhyādikāriṇāṃ vaikhānasānāṃ kaimutikanyāyasiddham autkṛṣṭyaṃ kenāpodituṃ śakyam.





     [devalakanirūpaṇam]
[63.1-3]     kiñca - yathā vaikhānasānām utpattyādikaṃ śrutismṛtipurāṇādiṣu viśeṣeṇa pratipāditaṃ tathā itareṣāṃ viśeṣeṇa pratipāditañ cet tadā vaikhānasasāmyam itareṣāṃ syāt. tathā na dṛśyate hi.
[63.4]     atha vastuto devalakā nirūpyante.
[63.5]     vaikhānase: "avaikhānasavipro yaḥ pūjayed ālaye harim /
[63.6]     sa vai devalako nāma havyakavyabahiṣkṛtaḥ //
[63.7]     vaikhānasakule jātaḥ pāñcarātreṇa dīkṣitaḥ /
[63.8]     na dīkṣito na sañjāto (?) lobhān mohān madarcanam /
[63.9]     kuryāc cet tu viśeṣeṇa bhaved devalakas to saḥ //"

     [devalakatraividyam]

[63.10]     pāñcarātre saṃkarṣaṇasaṃhitāyām: "karmadevalakāḥ kecit kalpadevalakāḥ pare /
[63.11]     śuddhadevalakāś cānye tridhā devalakāḥ smṛtāḥ // [Saṅkarṣaṇasaṃhitā.]

     [karmadevalakalakṣaṇam]

[63.12]     arthārthī kālanirdeśī yo devaṃ pūjayet sa hi /
[63.13]     karmadevalako nāma sarvakarmabahiṣkṛtaḥ // [Saṅkarṣaṇasaṃhitā.]
[63.14]     pāñcarātravidhānajño dīkṣāvirahito 'rcakaḥ /
[63.15]     caturvedādhikāro 'pi kalpadevalakaḥ smṛtaḥ // [Saṅkarṣaṇasaṃhitā.]
[63.16]     āgamoktavidhānajño bhadrakālyupajīvakaḥ /
[63.17]     śuddhadevalakaḥ proktaḥ sarvakarmabahiṣkṛtaḥ // [Saṅkarṣaṇasaṃhitā.]
[63.18]     ārṣoktena vidhānena devalatvaṃ na vidyate /
[63.19]     tasmāt sarvaprayatnena vaidikenaiva pūjayet //" iti [Saṅkarṣaṇasaṃhitā]
[63.20]     śivaśekharatantre - rudraḥ:
[63.21]     "atha devalakān vakṣye śṛṇu devi samāhitā /
[63.22]     karmadevalakāḥ kecit kalpadevalakāḥ pare // [Śivaśekharatantra]
[63.23]     śuddhadevalakās tv anye tridhā devalakāsmṛtāḥ /
[63.24]     anyasūtroktamārgeṇa yas saṃvatsarapūjakaḥ //





     [Śivaśekharatantra]

     [kalpadevalakalakṣaṇam]

[64.1]     adīkṣitaḥ svayaṃ tantre karmadevalakas tu saḥ /
[64.2]     anenaiva prakāreṇa vatsaratryapūjakaḥ /
[64.3]     kalpadevalakaḥ proktaḥ sa vai śailasute dhruvam // [Śivaśekharatantra]

     [śuddhadevalakalakṣaṇam]

[64.4]     ananujñātam ācāryāt āgamaṃ śuśruve ca yaḥ /
[64.5]     śīlataḥ tasya śiṣyaś ca śuddhadevalakāv ubhau // [Śivaśekharatantra]

     [trividhasyāpi devalakatvasya rudrādiviṣayakatā]

[64.6]     tridhā devalakatvaṃ tu na viṣṇuviṣaye kvacit /
[64.7]     rudrakālyādiviṣayam etad āgamasaṃmatam //" iti [Śivaśekharatantra]
[64.8]     smṛtyantare: "śarvaṃ sūryaṃ tathā candraṃ durgādī rudradevatāḥ /
[64.9]     yo 'rcayet paṇapūrvaṃ saḥ sadyaḥ patati mānavaḥ //
[64.10]     durgā ca bhadrakālī ca buddhaś ca kṣetrapālakaḥ /
[64.11]     pañcapūjā ca ity ete pañcadevalakāḥ smṛtāḥ //
[64.12]     ādityam ambikāṃ viṣṇuṃ gaṇanāthaṃ maheśvaram /
[64.13]     gṛhe pūjā ca ity ete pañcadevalakāḥ smṛtāḥ (?) //" iti
[64.14]     viṣṇudharmottare: "caṇḍikāyāś ca durgāyā jyeṣṭāyā bhairavasya ca /
[64.15]     rudrasya pūjakā ye vai te vai devalakāḥ smṛtāḥ //" iti [ViṣṇudharmottaraP ]
[64.16]     viṣṇu: "devārcanaparo yo 'pi parārthaṃ vittakāṅkṣayā /
[64.17]     caturvedadharo vipraḥ sa caṇḍālasamo bhaved //" iti [ViṣṇuP ]
[64.18-19]     evam ebhir vacanaiḥ śāstrānanumatamārgeṇa pūjakānāṃ devatāntarapūjakānām eva ca devalakatvaṃ siddhyatīti sphuṭam avagamyate.
[64.20]     kiñca: "vṛṣo dharmas samākhyataḥ tasya yaḥ kurute layam /
[64.21]     vṛṣalaṃ taṃ vidur devā nikṛṣṭaṃ śvapacād api //"





     [devalakaśabdanirvacanam]

[64.22-65.2]      iti vṛṣalaśabdo yathā vedaśāstroktamārgalayakārake vyutpāditaḥ, tathā devalakśabdo 'pi "div krīḍāvijigīṣāvyavahāradyutistutimodamadasvapnakāntigatiṣv" iti dhātvarthānusāreṇa gatyaparaparyāyamārgārthakadivdhātughaṭitassan vedoktamārgalayaprāpake vyutpādayituṃ śakyate iti tatpratīpeṣu vedamārgapratiṣṭhāpakeṣu vaikhānaseṣu na sarvātmanā pravartate. tathā ca:
[65.3]     hārītaḥ: "vaikhānasās tu ye viprā haripūjanatatparāḥ /
[65.4]     na te devalakāḥ proktā viṣṇupādābjasaṃśrayāt //" iti [Vṛddhahārīta 8.78]

     [vaikhānasānaṃ devalakaśabdavācyatvābhāvaḥ]

[65.5]     smṛtyarthasāre: atri: "vaidikenaiva vidhinā dambhalobhavivarjitaḥ /
[65.6]     pūjayed bhaktito viṣṇuṃ sa hi devalako na vai //" iti
[65.7-8]     anyathā śrutyuktamārgeṇālayārcakānām api devalakatve tādṛśālayārcanapratipādakānāṃ śrutismṛtipurāṇādivacanānāṃ vyarthatā syāt.
[65.9-10]     nanu - ajñānataḥ kṛtam api bhagavadārādhanam apavargapradañ cet. vinā śāstraṃ anadhikāriṇāpi kṛtaṃ tatapavargapradaṃ kiṃ na syād iti cet. na. bhagavadājñābhaṅgāpatteḥ.
[65.11]     yathoktaṃ bhagavatā: "yaś śāstravidhim utsṛjya vartate kāmakārataḥ /
[65.12]     na sa siddhim avāpnoti na sukhaṃ na parāṃ gatim //" iti [MBh 6.38.23]
[65.13]     "śrutismṛtī mamaivājñā yas tām ullaṅghya vartate /
[65.14]     ājñācchedī mama drohī madbhakto 'pi na vaiṣṇavaḥ //" iti
[65.15]     "mama cāpi priyaṃ viṣṇor devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ /
[65.16]     mānuṣo vaidikācāraṃ manasā 'pi na laṅghayet //" iti
[65.17-18]     ataḥ anadhikāriṇā kṛtaṃ śāstrāsammatam iti tantroktaprakāreṇa kṛtam api tat nāpavargapradam.
[65.19]     nanu: "brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ vaiśyaiḥ śūdraiś ca kṛtalakṣaṇaiḥ /
[65.20]     arcanīyaś ca sevyaś ca pūjanīyaś ca mādhavaḥ /
[65.21]     sāttvataṃ vidhim āsthāya gītaḥ saṅgarṣaṇena yaḥ //"

     [tantrānusāripūjāyāḥ apavargapradatvābhāvaḥ]

[65.22-24]     iti śūdrādīnām api pāñcarātroktamārgeṇārcane adhikāre siddhe kathaṃ tāntrikoktaprakāreṇārcanaṃ kurvataḥ brāhmaṇādeḥ (anadhikāriṇaḥ) tat apavargapradaṃ na bhavatīty ucyata iti ced ucyate.




     [caturvidhatantreṣu ekatra dīkṣitasya tantrāntare 'nadhikāraḥ]

[66.1]     "prathamaṃ mantrasiddhāntaṃ dvitīyañ cāgamāhvayam / [PādmaS caryāpāda 19.112cd]
[66.2]     tṛtīyaṃ tantrasiddhāntaṃ tantrāntaramataḥ param //" [PādmaS caryāpāda 19.113ab]
[66.3]     iti caturvidheṣu siddhānteṣu
[66.4]     "ekatra dīkṣitas tantre siddhānte vā dvijottama /
[66.5]     kriyāṃ na kuryād anyatra karṣaṇādi caturmukha // [Pādma.S caryāpāda 19.131]
[66.6]     ācāryakam athārtvijyaṃ pūjāñ ca madhuvidviṣaḥ /
[66.7]     mantre deve ca siddhānte tad evāsya hi yujyate //" [PādmaS caryāpāda 19.132]
[66.8]     iti caturvidhatantreṣu ekatra dīkṣitasya tantrāntare praveśayogyatābhāvasya pratipādanāt.
[66.9]     "ekagotrasamutpannaṃ pañcagotraṃ pṛthak pṛthak / ity ārabhya
[66.10]     sūtraṃ kātyāyanaṃ śākhāṃ yājuṣaṃ śuklam eva ca //
[66.11]     aupagāyanaśāṇḍilyau bhāradvājo 'tha gautamaḥ /
[66.12]     mauñjāyanis tu pañcaite pāñcarātrādhikāriṇaḥ //"
[66.13]     ity adhikāribhedasya vidhīyamānatvāt.

     [āpastambādisūtrasaṃskṛtasya pāñcarātroktasaṃskārayogyatābhāvaḥ]

[66.14]     "caturṇām api varṇānām itareṣāñ ca tadbhuvām /
[66.15]     dīkṣā samaiva sarveṣām ācāras tantravartmanā //" [PādmaS caryāpāda 21.55]

     [tantroktaprakāreṇa dīkṣitānām eva tantroktārcanāyām adhikāraḥ]

[66.16-18]     ityāpastambādisūtraiḥ saṃskṛtasya pāñcarātroktamārgeṇa niṣekādisaṃskārayogyatābhavakathanāt. tāntrikoktaprakāreṇa dīkṣitānām eva tantroktārcanāyām adhikāritva sambhavāt.

     [paradharmānuṣṭhātuḥ patitatvādi]

[66.19]     "svasūtre vartamāne tu parasūtreṇa vartate /
[66.20]     apramāṇam ṛṣiṃ kṛtvā so 'ndhe tamasi majjati //"
[66.21]     "svakīyadharmam utsṛjya paradharmaṃ ya āśrayet /
[66.22]     patitas sa bhaved āśu sadya eva na saṃśayaḥ //"
[66.23]     "svasūtrasya parityāgāt parasūtrasamāśrayāt /
[66.24]     sadyaḥ patati vai vipro na vedasya samāśraye //"






[67.1]     "śākhāṃ śikhāṃ tathā puṇḍraṃ samayācāram eva ca /
[67.2]     pūrvair ācaritaṃ kuryād anyathā patito bhavet //"
[67.3]     "yas svaśākhāṃ parityajya paraśākhāsu vartate /
[67.4]     śākhāraṇḍas sa vijñeyas sarvakarmabahiṣkṛtaḥ //" [ĀS 4.59]
[67.5]     "yas svadharmaṃ parityajya paradharmaṃ niṣevate /
[67.6]     pāṣaṇḍinaṃ tam āhur vai nikṛṣṭaṃ śvapacād api //" iti.
[67.7]     bhagavān: "śreyān svadharmo viguṇaḥ paradharmāt svanuṣṭhitāt /
[67.8]     svadharme nidhanaṃ śreyaḥ paradharmo bhayāvahaḥ //" iti. [MBh 6.25.35]
[67.9]     vyāsa: "svadharmaṃ yas samutsṛjya paradharmaṃ samāśrayet /
[67.10]     anāpadi sa vidvadbhiḥ patitaḥ parikīrtitaḥ //"
[67.11-12]     ityādibhiś ca vacanaiḥ paradharmānuṣṭhātuḥ patitatvādismaraṇāc ca anyasūtroktaprakāreṇa tāntrikoktena mārgeṇa vā bāhmaṇādibhir api anadhikāribhiḥ bhagavadārādhanaṃ kartuṃ na śakyate.

     [śūdrasya pūjāyām anadhikāraḥ]

[67.13]     tarhi "brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyair vaiśyaiḥ" ityādi bhāratavacanasya kā gatir iti cet - ucyate.
[67.14]     mādhavāḥ: mukhyatvena advārakabhagavadyajanādhikāritvena nirūpitaiḥ brāhmaṇaiḥ pūjanīyaḥ.
[67.15-16]     itaraiḥ kṣatriyair vaiśyaiś cārcanīyaḥ. śūdraiḥ strībhiś ca yathārham ijyas sevyaś ca iti tasya vacanasyārthaḥ.
[67.17]     "... śūdraiḥ strībhis tathetaraiḥ /
[67.18]     yathārham ijyas sevyaś ca nityaṃ sarveśvaro hariḥ //"
[67.19-22]     iti bhāradvājavacanāt "arghyāntam arcanaṃ proktaṃ havirantañ ca pūjanam //" ity arcanapūjanayoḥ bhinnārthakatvapratipādanāt, sarvair ekarītyā pūjane 'bhimate ekapadasyaiva paryāptatvāt itarayoḥ padayor vaiyarthyāpātāc ca. anyathā śūdrasyāpi pūjārcanādiṣv adhikārāṅgīkāre śrutismṛtisūtrapurāṇādivirodho bhavet.
[67.23-25]     śūdrasyānadhikārapratipādakāni vacanāni caitāni. śruti "tasmāc chūdro yajñe 'navakḷptaḥ. sa hi devatā anvasṛjata tasmāc chūdro bahupaśur ayajñīyo daiva" iti.





[68.1]     smṛti: "japas tapas tīrthasevā pravrajyā mantrasādhanam /
[68.2]     devatārādhanañ caiva strīśūdrapatitāni ṣaṭ //" iti

     [śūdrasyadvijaśuśrūṣaiva dharmaḥ]

[68.3]     śrībhāgavate: "śuśrūṣaṇaṃ dvijagavāṃ devānāñ cāpy amāyayā /
[68.4]     tatra labdhena santoṣaḥ śūdraprakṛtayas tv imāḥ //" iti [BhāgavataP 11.17.19]
[68.5]     manau: "brāhmaṇasya tapo jñānaṃ tapaḥ kṣatrasya rakṣaṇam /
[68.6]     vaiśyasya tu tapo vārtā tapaś śūdrasya sevanam //" iti [ManuDhŚ 11.235]
[68.7]     anyatra: "yadi śūdras tapaḥ kuryād vedadṛṣṭena vartmanā /
[68.8]     iha cāsya parikleśaḥ pretya cāsyāśubhā gatiḥ //" iti.
[68.9-11]     kimarthaṃ śūdrasya dvijaśuśrūṣā sarvadā abhihiteti cet - ucyate. janmāntarīyakarmavaśāt jananakāle 'pi tamoguṇair abhibhūtasya tasya śūdrasya tamonirasanārthaṃ dvijaśuśrūṣaṇaṃ brahmaṇā prayuktam.
[68.12]     āśvamedhike: "udite savitar yasya kriyāyuktasya dhīmataḥ / [MBh 14, App. 4.1690]
[68.13]     caturvedadharasyāpi dehe ṣaḍvṛṣalāḥ sthitāḥ // [MBh 14, App. 4.1691]
[68.14]     kṣatriye sapta vijñeyā vaiśye tv aṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ / [MBh 14, App. 4.1692]
[68.15]     niyatāḥ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha śūdre 'ṣṭāviṃśatiḥ khalu //" ity ārabhya [MBh 14, App. 4.1693]
[68.16]     "rāgadveṣau ca mohaś ca pāruṣyañ ca nṛśaṃsatā / [MBh 14, App. 4.3340]
[68.17]     śāṭhyañ ca dīrghavairañ ca atimānamanārjavam // [MBh 14, App. 4.3341]
[68.18]     anṛtañ cāpavādaś ca paiśunyam atilobhatā / [MBh 14, App. 4.3342]
[68.19]     hiṃsā steyaṃ mṛṣāvādo vañcanā roṣalobhate // [MBh 14, App. 4.3343]
[68.20]     abuddhatā ca nāstikyaṃ bhayam ālasyam eva ca / [MBh 14, App. 4.3344]
[68.21]     aśaucañ cākṛtajñatvaṃ dambhatā stambha eva ca // [MBh 14, App. 4.3345]
[68.22]     niṣkṛteś cāpy avijñānaṃ janane śūdram āviśan / [MBh 14, App. 4.3346]
[68.23]     dṛṣṭvā pitāmahaḥ śūdram abhibhūtan tu tāmasaiḥ // [MBh 14, App. 4.3347]
[68.24]     dvijaśuśrūṣaṇaṃ dharmaṃ śūdrāṇān tu prayuktavān / [MBh 14, App. 4.3348]
[68.25]     naśyanti tāmasā bhāvāḥ śūdrasya dvijabhaktitaḥ //" iti. [MBh 14, App. 4.3349]






     [vaikhānasetarasūtriṇāṃ bhagavadārādhanaprakāraḥ]

[69.1]     ataḥ tamoguṇābhibhūtasya śūdrasya bhagavadyajanādhikāro nāsty eva.
[69.2-7]     nanv eṣāṃ śaunakādyuktaprakāreṇa bhagavadārādhane 'dhikāro bhaved iti cet - tad asat. tatra adhikāriviśeṣapratipādanābhavāt; sāmānyenoktatve 'pi śrutismṛtisūtrapurāṇamahābhāratavaikhānasapāñcarātraśaivaśilpajyautiṣādiṣu adhikāriṇāṃ viśiṣya pratipāditatvāt sarvaśākhāpratyayanyāyena sāmānyaviśeṣanyāyena "matprakaraṇādhītaṃ sarvaṃ madartham" iti nyāyena prakaraṇasāmyena, upāsya devataikyāt guṇopasaṃhāranyāyena ca śaunakādibhir uktārcanāvidher api atraiva paryavasānaṃ yuktam.
[69.8-9]      itarasūtriṇām katham iti cet - svāśramadharmācaraṇenaiva bhagavadārādhanaphalam siddhyati. yathocyate:
[69.10]     smṛtiṣu: "bahvalpaṃ vā svagṛhyoktaṃ yasya karma pracoditam /
[69.11]     tasya tāvati śāstrārthe kṛte sarvaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavet //" iti
[69.12]     śrīviṣṇupurāṇe: "varṇāśramācāravatā puruṣeṇa paraḥ pumān /
[69.13]     viṣṇur ārādhyate panthā nānyas tattoṣakārakaḥ //" [ViṣṇuP 2.8.9]
[69.14]     tathānyatra: "varṇāśrameṣu ye dharmāḥ śāstroktā munisattama /
[69.15]     teṣu tiṣṭhan naro viṣṇum ārādhayati nānyathā // [ViṣṇuP 3.8.19.1-2?]
[69.16]     ye yajanti pitṝn devān brāhmaṇāṃś ca hutāśanam /
[69.17]     sarvabhūtāntarātmānaṃ viṣṇum eva yajanti te //" iti
[69.18]     purāṇāntare: "agnikāryaṃ japaṃ snānaṃ tapas svādhyāyam eva ca /
[69.19]     tam evoddiśya deveśaṃ kuru nityam atandritaḥ //
[69.20]     prātar utthāya vidhivat snātvā nityaṃ samāhitaḥ /
[69.21]     yajet karmabhis tais taiḥ viṣṇuṃ devādisaṃjñitam //"





[70.1]     śāṇḍilya:"prakṛttaiś ca nivṛttaiś ca svargadair mokṣadair api /
[70.2]     ārādhyo bhagavān eva vedadharmais sanātanaiḥ // [Śāṇḍilyasmṛti.]
[70.3]     sa eva sarvathopāsyo nānyas saṃsāratārakaḥ /
[70.4]     ubhābhyāṃ jñānakarmabhyām ārādhyo bhagavān hariḥ //" iti [Śāṇḍilyasmṛti]
[70.5]     śāntiparvaṇi: "svayambhūvihito dharmo yo yasya hi nareśvara / [MBh 14, App. 4.222]
[70.6]     sa tena kṣapayet pāpaṃ samyag ācaritena hi //" iti [MBh 14, App. 4.223]
[70.7]     pādme: "dharmān nijāṃś ca śāstroktān varṇadharmān aśeṣataḥ /
[70.8]     pālayantīha ye vaiśyā na te yānti yamālayam //" iti [PadmaP ]
[70.9]     smṛtyantare: "śrutismṛtisadācāravihitaṃ karma yas sadā /
[70.10]     svasvadharmaṃ prayatnena śreyo 'rthīha samāśrayet //"
[70.11-12]     "nānyaḥ panthā vidyate 'yanāye" 'ti "brāhmaṇā vividaśanti yajñena dānena tapasānāśakena" iti ca śrutir imam arthaṃ draḍhayanti.
[70.13-15]     ataḥ advārakabhagavadyajanādhikāribhiḥ śrīmadvaikhānasasūtribhis sāmyaṃ keṣāñcid api nopapadyate iti kṛtaṃ pallavitena. etāvatā "akhilajagatkāraṇabhūtena vikhanasā praṇītatvāt" iti prathamo hetuḥ nirūpitaḥ.
[70.16]     iti prathamahetunirūpaṇam





[71.1]     atha dvitīyahetunirūpaṇam
[71.2]     athāsya vaikhānasasūtrasya sarvasūtrāṇām āditvaṃ nirūpyate. tathā hi:

     [vaikhānasasūtrasya sarvasūtrāpekṣayā āditvam]

[71.3]     brahmakaivarte: " yathā munīnāṃ vikhanā ādibhūta udāhṛtaḥ /
[71.4]     sūtrāṇāṃ tatpraṇītan tu tathā śreṣṭatamaṃ smṛtam //" iti [BrahmakaivartaP ]
[71.5]     purātantre bhṛgu: "vedānāṃ vyāsanād arvāk prāgrūpaṃ militan tu yat /
[71.6]     tān tu vaikhānasīṃ śākhām iti vedavido viduḥ //" ity ārabhya [Purātantra]
[71.7]     "vaiṣṇavaṃ sūtram etad dhi sarvasiddhikaraṃ param /
[71.8]     ādyatvāt sarvasūtrāṇāṃ vaiṣṇavatvāc ca tat tu vai // [Purātantra]
[71.9]     mayānuvartitaṃ tadvat kāśyapātrimarīcibhiḥ //" iti [Purātantra]
[71.10]     skānde ca: "vaikhānasīṃ mahāśākhāṃ svasūtre viniyuktavān /
[71.11]     padmabhūḥ paramo dhātā tasminn ārādhanatrayam //
[71.12]     uktavān nigamārthānām ācāraṃ pravibhāgaśaḥ //" iti [SkandaP ]

     [ādau caturaśrasya ravimaṇḍalasya kālāntare vartulatvam]

[71.13-14]     sūtrārthaparyālocanayāpi sarvasūtrāditvam asyāvagamyate. yathā -"mukhyād indraś cāgniś ce" ti bhagavanmukhād agnisṛṣṭiḥ śrūyate. tathā:
[71.15]     āśvamedhike - bhagavadvacanam:
[71.16]     "prathamaṃ manmukhāt sṛṣṭo lokārthe pacanaḥ prabhuḥ / [MBh 14, App. 4.2572]
[71.17]     sṛṣṭamātro jagatsarvam attum aicchat purā khalu // [MBh 14, App. 4.2573]
[71.18]     tataḥ praśamitas so 'yam upāsīno mayā purā / [MBh 14, App. 4.2574]
[71.19]     satatopāsanāt so 'yam aupāsana iti smṛtaḥ //" iti [MBh 14, App. 4.2575]
[71.20-21]     evaṃ paramapuruṣamukhāj jātasyaupāsanāgneḥ kuṇḍavidhānādikam atraiva sūtre pratipāditam.
[71.22-24]     kiñ ca navagrahamakhe savitṛmaṇḍalasya caturaśratvam ucyate "caturaśraṃ vṛttam ityādinā (sūtre). ādau caturaśrasya sato ravimaṇḍalasya kālāntare vṛttatvakalpanaṃ pramāṇair avagamyate. yathā:





[72.1]     viṣṇupurāṇe: "tejasaś śamanañ cāsya viśvakarmā cakāra ha /
[72.2]     bhramimāropya sūryan tu tasya tejo 'vaśātanam // [Viṣṇu.P ]
[72.3]     kṛtavān aṣṭamaṃ bhāgaṃ sa vyaśātayad avyayam /
[72.4]     yatsūryād vaiṣṇavaṃ tejaś śātitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā // [Viṣṇu.P ]
[72.5]     jājjvalyamānam apatat tadbhūmau munisattama //"iti [ViṣṇuP ]
[72.6]     evaṃ ca sūryasāvarṇikamanvantaramārabhya ravimaṇḍalasya vṛttākārapratītiḥ.
[72.7-8]     tad anusāreṇa bodhāyanādibhiḥ vṛttākāratvaṃ ravimamaṇḍalasyoktam. tataḥ pūrvaṃ caturaśratvam va. tad evāsmin sūtre pratipāditam.
[72.9-10]     evaṃ "vānaprastho vaikhānaśāstrasamudācāro vaikhānasa" iti vaikhānasasūtram anusmṛtya tṛtīyāśramadharmān bodhāyanaḥ pratipādayati. [BaudhDhS 2.6.11.14]
[72.11-17]     tathā āgnivaiśyasūtre "athātas sūtragaṇanāṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ. bodhāyanam āpastambaṃ satyāṣāṭhaṃ drāhyāyaṇam āgastyaṃ śākalyam āśvalāyanaṃ śāmbhavīyaṃ kātyāyanam iti navāni pūrvasūtrāṇi. vaikhānasaṃ śaunakīyaṃ bhāradvājam āgnivaiśyaṃ jaiminīyaṃ vādhūlaṃ mādhyandinaṃ hiraṇyakeśīyaṃ kauṣītakam iti navāny aparasūtrāṇi. evam aṣṭādaśasūtrāṇy aṣṭādaśasūtrakārāś ca. etāni caturvedamūlāni. pūrvasūtrāṇi śārīrāṇi sāmānyāni bhavanti. uttarasūtrāṇi vaikhānasādīni viṣṇusaṃbandhīni daivikānī" ti vaikhānasasūtrasyāditvaṃ vaiṣṇavatvañ cocyate.
[72.18-19]     asya sūtrasyādhikyaṃ ca "ye vaikhānasasūtreṇa saṃskṛtās dvijātaya" ityādinā pūrvam eva pratipāditam.
[72.20-21]     ataḥ sarvasūtrāṇām ādir idaṃ sūtram iti siddham. tataḥ sarvasūtrottamatvañ cāsyopapadyate iti nirūpito dvitīyo hetuḥ.
[72.22]     iti dvitīyahetunitūpaṇam.





     [tṛtīyahetunirūpaṇam]

     [vaikhānasasūtrasya śrutimārgānusāritvam]

[73.1-3]     athāsya śrīvaikhānasasūtrasya sūtrāntarāpekṣayā vailakṣaṇyāpādakaṃ pratyakṣaśrutimūlakatvam astīti jñāpayituṃ "sarvakarmasu śrutimārgānusāritvād" iti tṛtīyo hetur nirūpyate. tathā hi:

     [śuddhācamanavidheḥ śrautatvam]

[73.4-9]     śuddhācamanavidhau "yattrir ācāmati tena ṛcaḥ prīṇāti" ityādi śrutyanusāreṇa sūtre "ṛgvedaḥ prīṇātv" ityādinā śuddhācamanam uktam. nanu bodhāyanenāpi śuddhācamanavidhir ukta iti cet satyam. "ācamanavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ" ity ārabhya "gokarṇabaddhahastena trir ācamet, prathamaṃ yat pibati tena ṛgvedaṃ prīṇāti yad dvitīyaṃ tena yajurvedaṃ yat tṛtīyaṃ tena sāmavedaṃ prīṇātī"ty ācamanena ṛgvedādīnāṃ prītir bhavatīty uktam. na tu mantraḥ.
[73.10-11]     śrutismṛtisūtravihitasya sandhyopāsanasya pradhānabhūtam arghyapradānādikam atraiva pratipāditam. "prātas sūryaś cetyādinācamya āpo hiṣṭhādibhis tisṛbhiḥ prokṣya
[73.12]     gāyatryā 'po 'bhimantrya ādityābhimukhaṃ vikṣipya pradakṣiṇaṃ karoti" ityādi.
[73.13-17]     bodhāyanenāpi sandhyāvandanavidhir uktaḥ iti cet naivam. "athātas sandhyopāsanavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ. tīraṃ gatvāprayato 'bhiṣiktaḥ prayato vā nābhiṣiktaḥ prakṣālipādapāṇir apa ācamya surabhimatyā abliṅgābhir vāruṇībhiḥ hiraṇyavarṇābhiḥ pāvamānībhiḥ vyāhṛtibhir anyaiś ca pavitrair ātmānaṃ prokṣya prayato bhavati. athāpy udāharanti." [BaudhDhS 2.4.7.1-3]
[73.18]     "āpo 'vagāhanaṃ snānaṃ vihitaṃ sārvavarṇikam /
[73.19]     mantravatprokṣaṇañ caiva dvijānām avaśiṣyate //" iti [BaudhDhS 2.4.7.3-2]
[73.20-74.3]      sarvakarmaṇāñ caivārambheṣu prāksandhyopāsanākālāc caitenaiva pavitrasamūhenātmānaṃ prokṣya prayato bhavati. athāpy udāharanti. "darbheṣv āsīno darbhān dhārayamāṇaḥ sodakapāṇinā pratyaṅmukhaḥ sāvitrīṃ sahasrakṛtvaḥ āvartayet. prāṇāyāmaśo vā śatakṛtvaḥ. tribhiś ca prāṇāyāmaiḥ tato (tānto) brahmahṛdayena. vāruṇībhyāṃ rātrim upatiṣṭhate." ityādinā mārjanādikam uktam. pradhānabhūtam arghyapradānādikam anuktam. [BaudhDhS 2.4.7.4-9]





     [śrutyukto brahmayajñaprakāraḥ]

     [brahmavaraṇapūrvakasomavaraṇam]

[74.4-9]     brahmayajñaḥ. talavakāropaniṣadi "tasyā vā eṣa prathamaḥ pādaḥ oṃ bhūs tatsavitur vareṇyaṃ oṃ bhuvaḥ bhargo devasya dhīmahi oṃ suvaḥ dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayāt iti pacchaḥ, oṃ bhūr bhuvas tatsavitur vareṇyaṃ bhargo devasya dhīmahi oṃ suvaḥ dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayāt ity ardhacaśaḥ, oṃ bhūrbhuvassuvas tatsavitur vareṇyaṃ bhargo devasya dhīmahi dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayāt iti samastāñ ca sāvitrīṃ japtveti yathodiṣṭaḥ, tathātra sūtre 'pi ukto 'sti.
[74.10-11]     āghārādiṣu sarvam api śrautavat. atra brahmavaraṇānantaraṃ somavaraṇam apy uktam asti. "somo 'smākaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ rājā - somarājāno brāhmaṇā" iti.
[74.12-13]     "viṣṇuś ca vai somaś ca brahmav ādyam avadetāṃ 'ahaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ pratiṣṭhe'ti viṣṇur abravīt 'ahaṃ pratiṣṭhe'ti somaḥ. tau prajāpatiṃ praśnam aitāṃ so 'bravīt prajāpatiḥ
[74.14]     'chandāṃsi viṣṇum adhigacchanti, nakṣatrāṇi somaṃ. tāv ubhau brahmaṇyāv'; iti so 'bravīt.
[74.15-17]     pūjitau pūjayantau stutau stunvantau priyau priyavantau brahmaṇyau brahmavittau brāhmaṇānāṃ pratiṣṭhātārau bhavata iti yan māṃ brahmaṇā vakṣyanti yajñeṣu so 'ham iti viṣṇur abravīt. tasmād viṣṇur yajño brāhmaṇānāṃ pratiṣṭhā iti. vijñayate ca.
[74.18-22]     "brāhmaṇo vai chandāṃsī"ty etasmāt brāhmaṇāt yan māṃ brāhmaṇā vakṣyanti nakṣatreṣu tatrāham iti so 'bravīt. tasmāt brāhmaṇānāṃ somo rājeti tasmād vijñāyate ca brāhmaṇe vā aṣṭāviṃśo nakṣatrāṇāṃ tasya vacaḥ puṇyam iti tāv ubhau brahmaṇyau brahmavittau brāhmaṇānāṃ pratiṣṭhātārau brāhmaṇeṣu pratiṣṭhitau ya evaṃ brāhmaṇapuraskṛtāni karmāṇi karoti yajñasya samṛddhyā" iti ca śrutiprasiddhatvāt.
[74.23-25]     evam atra śāntikapauṣṭikādiṣu pradhānakarmatvāt navagrahamakhasya pañcāgnikuṇḍavidhānam uktam. "atha grahaśāntiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ. grahyāyattā lokayātrā tasmād ātmaviruddhe prāpte grahān samyak pūjayatī" ti.



     [grahaśānteḥ prādhānyam]

[75.1-8]     grahaśānteḥ kathaṃ prādhānyam iti ced ucyate. "udyantam astaṃyantam ādityam abhidhyāyan kurvan brāhmaṇo vidvān sakalaṃ bhadram aśnute 'sāv ādityo brahmeti brahmaiva san brahmāpy eti ya evaṃ veda" iti "ya eṣo 'ntarāditye hiraṇmayaḥ puruṣo dṛśyate" iti "yo 'sau tapann udeti" ityādi "viṣṇuśakter avasthānaṃ sadāditye karoti ca" iti "dhyeyas sadā savitṛmaṇḍalamadhyavartī" tyādibhiś ca vacanaiḥ yat pratipāditaṃ savitṛmaṇḍalamadhyavartino bhagavato nārāyaṇasya yajanaṃ tad evedam ity abhiprāyeṇa sūtrakārair asya grahayajñasya prādhānyam uktam. tathānte "anyathā mahattaro doṣo bhavatī"ty apy uktam.
[75.9]     bodhāyanaś ca: "athāto grahātithyabalikarmopahārān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ"

     [savitṛhomaḥ]

[75.10]     aśraddhadhānam aśucim ajapaṃ tyaktamaṅgalam /
[75.11]     grahā nayanti suvyaktaṃ puruṣaṃ yamasādanam //
[75.12]     grahāṇām ugraceṣṭānāṃ nakṣatrapathacāriṇām /
[75.13]     upahārān pravakṣyāmi śāntyarthan tu yathāvidhi //"

     [viṣṇvārādhanasya śrautatvam]

[75.14-16]     māsi māsy ṛtāv ṛtau candragrahe sūryagrahe viṣuve 'yane śubhāśubhe janmanakṣatre tadgrahāṇām ātithyaṃ saṃvatsarād api prayuñjānaḥ sarvān kāmān avāpnoti" iti grahaśāntikālaṃ nirūpya.
[75.17]     "grahā gāvo narendrāś ca brāhmaṇāś ca viśeṣataḥ /
[75.18]     pūjitāḥ pūjayanty enaṃ nirdahanty avamānitāḥ //"
[75.19]     ity akaraṇe pratyavāyam api darśitavān.
[75.20-22]     tasmād eva sūtrakāraiḥ sūryacandrau vinā lokapravṛtty asambhavāt sūryapradhānatvāc ca grahāṇāṃ sarvakarmaṇām ādau grahapuraskāram uktvā tatra pañcāgnikuṇḍavidhānam upadiśya pradhāne sabhye viṣṇurūpasya savituḥ homaḥ "sabhye savitur" iti pratipāditaḥ.
[75.23-24]     evam - "nārāyaṇa paraṃ brahma" - "brahmaiva bhūtānāṃ jyeṣṭhāṃ tena ko 'rhati spardhitum" - "agnir vai devānām avamo viṣṇuḥ paramaḥ tadantareṇa sarvā anyā devatāḥ"



     [śrutimūlakatve prāmāṇyātiśayaḥ]

[76.1]     ityādi śrutyanusāreṇa "tasmād gṛhe paramaṃ viṣṇuṃ pratiṣṭhāpya sāyaṃprātarhomānte 'rcayati"
[76.2-3]     iti nārāyaṇaparatvena sūtrāntareṣv anuktam ārādhanavidhim uktvā tatra "sa vā eṣa puruṣaḥ pañcadhā pañcātmā" ityādi śrutyanusāreṇa pañcamūrtividhānam apy uktam.
[76.4-5]     āghārādiṣu śrautavad eveti pratyakṣasiddham iti pūrvam evoktam. evam anyatrāpi draṣṭavyam.
[76.6-7]     śrutimārgānusāritve ko viśeṣa iti cet - ucyate. śrutimūlatve hi prāmāṇyātiśayasambhavaḥ. yathāha
[76.8]     manu: "vedaḥ smṛtiḥ sadācāraḥ svasya ca priyam ātmanaḥ /
[76.9]     etac catuṣṭayaṃ prāhuḥ sākṣād dharmasya lakṣaṇam // [ManuDhŚ 2.12]
[76.10]     sarvaṃ tu samavekṣyaitad akhilaṃ jñānacakṣuṣā /
[76.11]     śrutiprāmāṇyato vidvān svadharme niviśeta vai //" [ManuDhŚ 2.8]
[76.12]     śrībhārate: "vedapraṇihito dharmo hy adharmas tadviparyayaḥ /
[76.13]     vedo nārāyaṇas sākṣāt svayambhūr iti śuśrumaḥ //" [MBh ]
[76.14]     pracetā: "amīṃāṃsyā bahiśśāstrā ye cānye vedabarjitaḥ /
[76.15]     yattadbrūyur na tatkuryād vedād dharmo vidhīyate //"
[76.16]     smṛtyantare: "dharmaṃ jijñāsamānānāṃ pramāṇaṃ prathamaṃ śrutiḥ / [MBh 14 App. 4.2492]
[76.17]     dvitīyaṃ dharmaśāstrān tu tṛtīyaṃ lokasaṅgrahaḥ //" iti [MBh 14 App. 4.2493]
[76.18-20]     etāvatā sarvakarmasu śrutimārgānusāritva rūpaḥ tṛtīyo hetur nirūpito bhavati. tathā ca śrutimārgānusāritvād asya sūtrasya sarvasūtrottamatvaṃ siddhyati iti nirūpitas tṛtīyo hetuḥ.
[76.21]     iti tṛtīyahetunirūpaṇam.





     [caturthahetunirūpaṇam]
     [vaikhānasasūtrasya samantrakasarvakriyāpratipādakatvam]

[77.1-2]     idānīṃ tāvat vaikhānasasūtroktadharmānuṣṭhānena anantasthiraphalaprāptiḥ satkulīnatvaṃ phalabhūyastvam api bhavatīti jñāpayituṃ "samantrakasarvakriyāpratipādakatvād" iti caturtho hetu nirūpyate. tad yathā:
[77.4-10]     atra sūtra nityānuṣṭhānavidhau "indro 'ham ubhābhyām" ity ārabhya karaprakṣālanādīni samantrakatvenoktāni. brahmayajñe "ṛtañ ca satyañ ce" ty ādi viśeṣaḥ. puṇyāhe samantrakatvaṃ spaṣṭam. sūtrāntareṣv anuktam aupāsanāgnikuṇdavidhānaṃ pratipāditam. āghāravidhau samantrakatvaṃ siddham. antahome tathaiva. nāndīmukhapūrvakopanayanādiṣu śārīreṣu saṃskāreṣu samantrakatvaṃ pratyakṣam. sthālīpākādiṣu "pūrvavad" ity anena pūrvaṃ vistareṇa pratipāditasyāghāravidheḥ prayogasaukaryārthaṃ saṃkṣepeṇa pratipādanam.

     [aparakriyāyām api samantrakatvam]

[77.11-15]     aparakriyāyām apy asti samantrakatvam. tatra kvacit "tūṣṇīm" ity uktvatvāt samantrakatvaṃ nāstīti svayam evāśaṅkya prakārāntareṇa samantrakatvaṃ pratyapādayat. tatra tatra kvacit mantrayogyatābhāve 'pi vihitaviśaye sarvatra samantrakatvam astīty avagamyate. sūtrāntareṣu vihitaviśayeṣv api samantrakatvānukteḥ teṣāṃ samantrakasarvakriyātvaṃ nāsti. tatra aparakriyāyām api sūtrāntarānapekṣā dṛśyate.
[77.16-19]     bodhāyanena agnimukhādiṣu paridhiparistaraṇādikṣepaṇam tūṣṇīm evoktam. samantrakatvena karmaṇām uktau ko viśeṣa iti cet - ucyate. karmaṇāṃ mantravattve hi vīryavattaratvaṃ karmārādhya bhagavatprīṇanadvārā anantasthiraphalaprāptiḥ satkulīnatvañ ca bhavantīti smṛtipurāṇādiṣv avagamyate. yathā

     [karmaṇām samantrakatve vīryavattaratvam]

[77.20-22]     chāndogye: "yad eva vidyayā karoti śraddhayopaniṣadā tad eva vīryavattaraṃ bhavatī"ti. tatraivaṃ vyākhyātam. "mantraprakāśitāni karmāṇi kriyante nāmantra kam asti karme"ti.





     [mantrahīnakarmanindā]

[78.1]     ātharvaṇe: "ṛgyajussāmākhyā (?) mantreṣu karmāṇi kavayo yāny apaśyann iti"
[78.2]     āraṇyaparvaṇi: "vratopanayanābhyāṃ vā upavāsena vā dvijaḥ /
[78.3]     kriyāmantraiś ca saṃyukto brāhmaṇas syān na saṃśayaḥ //" [MBh 3.81.134]
[78.4]     tatraiva: "guṇābhāve phalaṃ nyūnaṃ bhavaty aphalam eva vā /
[78.5]     anārambhe tu na phalaṃ na guṇo dṛśyate hy utaḥ //" iti [MBh 3.33.48]
[78.6]     bṛhannāradīye: "amantrato havir yat tu hūyate jātavedase /
[78.7]     apātre dīyate yac ca tad ghoraṃ bhogasādhanam // [BṛhannāradaP.]
[78.8]     hutaṃ haviś cāśucinā dattaṃ yatkarma yatkṛtam /
[78.9]     tatsarvaṃ tava bhāgārham adhaḥpātaphalaprada //" [BṛhannāradaP]
[78.10]     iti balicakravartinaṃ prati bhagavatā vāmanenoktam.
[78.11]     bodhāyana: "gobhir aśvaiś ca yānaiś ca kṛṣyā rājopasevayā /
[78.12]     kulāny akulatāṃ yānti yāni hīnāni mantrataḥ // [BaudhDhS 1.5.10.28]
[78.13]     mantratas susamṛddhāni kulāny alpadhanāny api /
[78.14]     kulasaṃkhyāṃ ca gacchanti karṣanti ca mahad yaśaḥ //" [BaudhDhS 1.5.10.29]
[78.15]     manur api: "kuvivāhaiḥ kriyālopair vedānadhyayanena ca /
[78.16]     kulāny akulatāṃ yānti brāhmaṇātikrameṇa ca // [ManuDhŚ 3.63]
[78.17]     śilpena vyavahāreṇa śuddhāpatyaiś ca kevalaiḥ /
[78.18]     gobhir aśvaiś ca yānaiś ca kṛṣyā rājopasevayā // [ManuDhŚ 3.64]
[78.19]     ayājyayājanāc caiva nāstikyena ca karmaṇā /
[78.20]     kulāny akulatāṃ yānti yāni hīnāni mantrataḥ // [ManuDhŚ 3.65]
[78.21]     mantratas tu samṛddhāni kulāny alpadhanāni ca /
[78.22]     kulasaṃkhyāṃ ca gacchanti karṣanti ca mahad yaśaḥ //" [ManuDhŚ 3.66]





[79.1]     mantrapūtan tu yac chrāddham" iti somotpattau smaryate.
[79.2]     śrīgītāyāñ ca: "vidhihīnam asṛṣṭānnaṃ mantrahīnam adakṣiṇam /
[79.3]     śraddhāvirahitaṃ yajñaṃ tāmasaṃ paricakṣate //" ity uktam. [BhGī = MBh 6.39.13]
[79.4-5]     yathopāsanaṃ phalam iti ca śrutisiddhaṃ "yathā kratur asmin loke puruṣo bhavati tathetaḥ pretya bhavatī"ti.
[79.6-7]     ataḥ śārīreṣu saṃskāreṣu samantrakasarvakriyāpratipādanāt pūrṇatvaṃ, pūrṇatvād eva sarvasūtrottamatvaṃ cāsya sūtrasya siddham iti nirūpitaḥ caturtho hetuḥ.
[79.8]     iti caturthahetunirūpaṇam.



     [pañcamahetunirūpaṇam; vaikhānasasūtrasya niṣekādisaṃskārapratipādakatvam]

[80.1]     atha pañcamahetunirūpaṇam.
[80.2-5]     athāsya śrīvaikhānasasūtrasya sarvottamatve tatsūtroktadharmānuṣṭhātṝṇām api sarvotkṛṣṭatve ca itarasūtriṣu mukhyatvenānupapannaṃ niṣekādisaṃskārādimattvam asya sūtrasya mukhyata evopapadyata iti jñāpayituṃ niṣekādisaṃskārādimatvād iti pañcamo hetur nirūpyate. yathā:

     [saṃskāreṣu niṣekasya prathamatvam]

[80.6]     "atha niṣekādisaṃskārān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ, ṛtusaṅgamane"ty upakramya
[80.7]     "pāṇigrahaṇānī"ty antena śārīrasaṃskārā niṣekasaṃskārapūrvakatvena pratipāditāḥ.

     [niṣekam antareṇa prajotpattyasaṃbhavaḥ]

[80.8-11]     nanu: jātakopanayanavivāhānāntarabhāvino niṣekasya katham āditvaṃ pratipādyate? tathā "brāhmaṇo 'sya mukham āsīt" "manasā tv eva bhūtāni pūrvaṃ dakṣo 'sṛjat tadā" ityādi śrutismṛtiṣu niṣekena vinā utpattidarśanāc ca niṣekasya kim artham āditvaṃ pratipādyate? jātakasyāditvaṃ śrībhārate cāvagamyate.
[80.12]     "jātakarmādibhir yais tu saṃskāraiḥ saṃskṛtaś śuciḥ /
[80.13]     vedādhyayanasampannaṣ ṣaṭsu karmasv avasthitaḥ // [MB.h 12.182.2]
[80.14]     śaucācāraratas samyak bhikṣārthī ca gurupriyaḥ /
[80.15]     nityavratas satyaparaḥ sa vai brāhmaṇa ucyate //" iti [MBh 12.182.3]
[80.16]     evaṃ harivaṃśe:"kva dārāḥ kva ca saṃsargaḥ kva ca bhāvaviparyayaḥ /
[80.17]     yadiyaṃ brahmaṇā sṛṣṭā manasā mānasī prajā // [HariV 35.42]
[80.18]     yady asti tapaso vīryaṃ yuṣmākaṃ viditātmanāṃ /
[80.19]     sṛjadhvaṃ mānasān putrān prājāpatyena karmaṇā //" [HariV 35.43]
[80.20]     iti niṣekaṃ vināpi utpattiḥ śrūyate iti niṣekasyāditvaṃ na saṃbhavati iti cet -
[80.21-23]     tad asat. "niṣekavirahe 'pi utpattis saṃbhavatī"ty etan nopapadyate. tapobalād yogabalāc ca bhagavato nārāyaṇasya brahmaṇo maharṣīṇāṃ vā mānasaprajāsṛṣṭau śaktis sambhavati. nānyeṣām. yathā:





[81.1]     śrīviṣṇupurāṇe: "saṅkalpād darśanāt sparśāt pūrveṣām abhavan prajāḥ" [ViṣṇuP ]
[81.2]     tapoviṣeśair iddhānāṃ tadātyantatapasvinām //" [ViṣṇuP 1.15.79]
[81.3]     "yuge yuge bhavanty ete dakṣādyā munisattamāḥ /
[81.4]     punaś caiva niruddhyante vidvāṃs tatra na muhyati // [ViṣṇuP 1.15.83]
[81.5]     kāniṣṭhyaṃ śryaiṣṭhyam apy eṣāṃ pūrvaṃ nāsti dvijottama // [ViṣṇuP 1.15.84ab]
[81.6]     tapa eva garīyo 'bhūt prabhāvaś caiva kāraṇam //" iti [ViṣṇuP ]

     [niṣekenaiva rudrasyāpi utpattiḥ]

[81.7]     rudrotpattir api niṣekeneti śrūyate. śatapathe: "abhūd vā idaṃ sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhā"
[81.8-10]     ity ārabhya "bhūtānāñ ca prajāpatis saṃvatsarāyādikṣata bhūtānāṃ grahapatir āsīd uṣā patnī"ty ādikam uktvā "bhūtānāṃ patiḥ saṃvatsara uṣasi reto 'siñcat saṃvatsare kumāro 'jāyata tasya rudrasya nāma karotī"ty ādi.

     [niṣekakriyāprakāraḥ]

[81.11-13]     niṣekakriyāprakāro 'pi śrūyate hi. "nagnaṃ kṛtvorum upapravartayati yadā hi nagna ūrur bhavaty atha mithunībhavato 'tha retas sicyate 'tha prajāḥ prajāyante" iti, "retasa eva siktasya bahuśo rūpāṇi vikaroti sa vai prajāyate śvaḥ śvo bhūyān bhavatī"ti,
[81.14-18]     "reto mūtraṃ vijahāti yoniṃ praviśad indriyaṃ garbho jarāyuṇā vṛtaḥ ulbaṃ jahāti janmanā" iti. muṇḍopaniṣadi - "pumān retas siñcati yoṣitāyāṃ bahvyaḥ prajās sṛjamānās sarūpāḥ" iti. chāndogye - "yoṣā vā va gautamāgnir" ity ārabhya "tasya upastha eva samid. yad antaḥ karoti te 'rciṣā. abhinandā visphuliṅgās. tasminn agnau devā reto juhvati. tasyā āhuter garbhas sambhavatī"ti ca.

     [sṛṣṭikālād ārabhya niṣekād evotpattiḥ]

[81.19]     śrīviṣṇupurāṇe: "prajās sṛjeti vyādiṣṭaḥ pūrvaṃ dakṣas svayambhuvā /
[81.20]     yathā sasarja bhūtāni tathā śruṇu mahāmate // [ViṣṇuP 1.15.86]
[81.21]     manasā tv eva bhūtāni pūrvaṃ dakṣo 'sṛjat tadā /
[81.22]     devān ṛṣīṃs tu gandharvān asurān pannagāṃs tathā // [ViṣṇuP 1.15.87]
[81.23]     yadā 'sya sṛjamānasya na vyavardhanta tāḥ prajāḥ /
[81.24]     tatas sañcintya bahuśaḥ sṛṣṭihetoḥ prajāpatiḥ // [ViṣṇuP 1.15.88]




[82.1]     maithunenaiva dharmeṇa sisṛkṣur vividhāḥ prajāḥ /
[82.2]     tataḥ prabhṛti maitreya prajā maithunasambhavāḥ //" [ViṣṇuP 1.15.79ab?]
[82.3]     bhārate: "na caiṣāṃ maithuno dharmo babhūva bharatarṣabha /
[82.4]     saṅkalpād eva caiteṣāṃ garbhas samupapadyate // [MBh 12.200.35]
[82.5]     tatra tretāyuge kāle saṃsparśāj jāyate prajā /
[82.6]     na hy abhūn maithuno dharmas teṣām api narādhipa // [MB.h 12.200.36]
[82.7]     dvāpare maithuno dharmaḥ prajānām abhavan nṛpa /
[82.8]     tathā kaliyuge kāle dvandvam āpedire janāḥ //" iti [MBh 12.200.37]
[82.9-10]     evaṃ śrutismṛtiṣu sṛṣṭikālād ārabhya niṣekād evotpar iti śravaṇāt niṣekena vinā utpādanasāmarthyābhāvāc ca niṣekādimatvād ity uktam.

     [niṣekaśabdārthanirṇayaḥ]

[82.11-13]     atrāpastambīyā evam āhuḥ. "niṣeko nāma garbhādhānam eva, niṣekagarbhādhānayoḥ paryāyatvāt garbhādhānātirekeṇa niṣekaśabdasyārthāntarāsambhavāc ca. garbhādhānaśabdasyārthe vicāryamāṇe 'garbho 'sminn ādhīyate'; iti vyutpattyā 'indriyaṃ vai garbha'
[82.14-15]     iti śrutyanusāreṇa retassecanam eva garbhādhānam ity avagateḥ niṣekāditvam asmākam apy astī"ti.
[82.16-19]     atra baudhāyanīyaḥ pratyavatiṣṭhante. "yad uktaṃ 'niṣeko nāma garbhādhānam niṣekagarbhādhānayoḥ paryāyatvād'; iti - tadasat. niṣekagarbhādhānayoḥ pṛthaktvena pratipādanāt paryāyatvaṃ na ghaṭate. yathā - 'caturthyāṃ snātāyāṃ niśāyām alaṅkṛtya śayane 'bhimantrayate 'viṣṇur yonim'; ity upakramya 'athainām upaiti'; - 'tvāṃ pūṣann ...'; iti.
[82.20-23]     evaṃ niṣeka uktaḥ. 'atha garbhādhānavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ. pūrvapakṣe puṇye nakṣatre brāhmaṇān annena pariviṣya puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvā atha devayajanaprabhṛtyāgnimukhāt kṛtvā pakvāj juhoti - pravedhase kavaye medhyāye'ti. iti garbhādhānam uktam. evaṃ niṣekagarbhādhānayoḥ pṛthaktvena kīrtanāt     niṣeka eva garbhādhānam iti vaktum ayuktam.
[82.24-25]     kiñca āpastambasūtre niṣekapūrvakatvenānuktatvāt catvāriṃśat saṃskāraparigaṇane agṛhītatvāc ca teṣāṃ niṣekādyās saṃskārā na bhavantīti."





[83.1-6]     atra āpastambīyā ūcuḥ. "yady asmākaṃ niṣekādyāḥ saṃskārā na bhavantīty ucyate tarhi yuṣmākam api tathaiva, bhavat sūtre 'pi >yato etad dhutaḥ prahutaḥ āhutaḥ śūlagavo baliharaṇaṃ pratyavarohaṇam aṣṭakā pārvaṇahoma itīcaturyyāṃ snātāyom< ityādinā pṛthaktvena vidhīyamānasya garbhādhānasya lakṣaṇapratipādanābhāvāt viśiṣya kālanirūpaṇābhāvāc ca.

     [vaikhānasānām eva niṣekādisaṃskāravattvam]

[83.7]     (vaikhānase sūtre eva niṣekāditvena uktatvāc ca vaikhānasānām niṣekāditvam),
[83.8]     āvayoḥ ubhayor api niṣekādyās saṃskārā na bhavanti iti. ayam eva siddhāntaḥ.

     [itareṣāṃ garbhadhānādisaṃskāravattvam]

[83.9]     tathā ca: "niṣekādyāḥ śmaśānāntās teṣāṃ vai mantrataḥ kriyāḥ / [YājñavalkyaDhŚ 1.10cd]
[83.10]     garbhādhānam ṛtau puṃsasavanaṃ spandānāt purā //" [YājñavalkyaDhŚ 1.11ab]
[83.11-14]     iti yājñavalkyoktau teṣām iti śabdena "mukhye sambhavaty amukhyakalpanāyogād" iti nyāyena mukhyatvena śrīvaikhānasasūtre eva niṣekāditvasya vidyamānatvāt vaikhānasā eva parāmṛśyante iti - teṣām eva niṣekāditvam, itareṣāṃ niṣekāditvaṃ na sambhavati. api tu garbhādhānāditvam eva. ayam eva yājñavalkyābhiprāyaḥ.
[83.15-20]     athocyete. garbhādhānalakṣaṇam anuktaṃ viśiṣya kālaś cānukta iti yad uktam tatrocyate - sarveṣāṃ kāraṇabhūtena paramācāryeṇa vikhanasā praṇīte śrīvaikhānasasūtre "atha gṛhītagarbhāliṅgāni śarīrāṭopaḥ sakthisīdanaṃ dveṣo bhartur arucir āhāre lālāprakopaḥ kharatā vācaḥ sphuraṇaṃ yoner iti garbhasya daivānubandhaṃ jñātvā āpūryamāṇapakṣe puṇye punnāmni śubhe nakṣatre" ityādinā garbhādhānalakṣaṇakālayor api vaikhānasasūtre pratipāditvāt:
[83.21]     "vede vaikhānase sūtre yo dharmaḥ parikīrtitaḥ /
[83.22]     sarvaiḥ sa dharmo 'nuṣṭheyo nātra kāryā vicāraṇā //"
[83.23]     iti bhṛguṇoktatvāt "anuktam anyato grāhyam" iti nyāyāt vikhanasaḥ ācāryatvena
[83.24-25]     bhāratādiṣu pratipāditavyāc ca "anuktāṃśeṣu vaikhānasoktaprakāreṇa asmābhir api kartuṃ yuktam" iti. etad eva yuktataram. Tathāhi:



     [niṣekagarbhādhānayor aparyāyatvam]

[84.1-10]     āpastambādīnām ācāryeṇa bodhāyanena svaśiṣyān prati "athātra pākayajñānāṃ prāyaścittir" ity ārabhya "vyāhṛtīnāṃ prayoge ayathākṛtaṃ yathākṛtaṃ bhavatīty ācāryā bruvate. tatrāpy udāharanti" iti, "caturthīprabhṛtyā ṣoḍaśīm uttarām uttarām upaiti. prajāniḥśreyasam ṛtugamanam ity ācāryāḥ. sarvāṇy upagamanāni mantravanti bhavantīti bodhāyanaḥ. yac cādau yac cartāv iti śālīkir" iti - "athāsyātithayo bhavanti guros samānavṛttir vaikhānasaḥ snātako rājā vā dharmayuktaḥ. teṣām abhyutthāyāsanaṃ pādyam arhaṇam arghyaṃ vā prajuñjīta" iti - "ekam agnihotraṃ sāyam upakramaṃ prātar apavargam ācāryā bruvate tatrodāharanti" iti, "vaikhānasānāṃ na druhyet" ityādi sūtreṣu "ācāryā bruvate" iti nirdiṣṭaḥ ācāryaḥ vaikhānasa eveti vaktuṃ yuktam - manvādīnāṃ śārīrasaṃskāravaktṛtvābhāvāt, bodhāyanena pratipāditasya vaikhānasasūtre vidyamānatvāt,
[84.11]     "guroḥ samānavṛttir vaikhānasaḥ" iti bodhāyanenaivoktatvāt, "vikhanasācārye"ti.
[84.12-13]     bhārate pratipāditvāc ca. tathā ca sarveṣāṃ kāraṇabhūtena vikhanasā praṇītatvāt tatsūtroktaprakāreṇa sarvaiḥ kartuṃ yuktam eva. kiñca araṇyādipātralakṣaṇam api tatraiva pratipāditam.
[84.14]     anye 'py āhuḥ. "asmākam api niṣekāditvaṃ samānam" iti. tad apy asat.
[84.15]     garbhādhānaśabdasyārthe vicāryamāṇe "yoniṃ praviśad indriyaṃ garbho jarāyuṇā vṛta" iti
[84.16-20]     pramāṇena garbhagole praviṣṭasya retasa eva garbhaśabdavācyatvam avagamyate. na tv itarasya kevala retasaḥ. tathā - "āsiñcatu prajāpatir dhātā garbhaṃ dadhātu" iti niṣekakriyānantarabhāvitvāt garbhādhānasya, niṣekasya tu pratyārtavaṃ kartuṃ vyogyatāsambhavāt adhṛtaretasaḥ srāvadoṣaprasaṅgāt śrutismṛtivirodhāt pratyakṣavirodhāṅ ca niṣeka eva garbhādhānam iti vaktum ayuktam.

     [niṣekaprathamakasaṃskāravatāṃ śraiṣṭhyam]

[84.21]     atha niṣekāditve ko viśeṣa iti cet - ucyate. niṣekādikriyāvatām eva
[84.22]     śrotriyatvaṃ dharmaśāstrādhikāritvaṃ brahmaśarīritvañ ca bodhāyanādibhir uktam. yathā:
[84.23]     "niṣeke garbhasaṃskāre jātakarmakriyāsu ca /
[84.24]     vidhivat saṃskṛtā mantraiḥ cīrṇā vratasamāpanāt //
[84.25]     śrotriyā iti vijñeyāḥ śākhāpārāś ca ye dvijāḥ /
[84.26]     vidhivat gṛhyate pāṇim ṛtau cīrṇavratās tu te //




[85.1]     mantravatsamprayogena brāhmaṇyāṃ garbham ādadhuḥ /
[85.2]     niṣekādyāḥ śmaśānāntāḥ satkriyā brāhmaṇāśritāḥ //" iti
[85.3]     yājñavalkya: "niṣekādyāḥ śmaśānāntāḥ teṣāṃ vai mantrataḥ kriyāḥ / [YājñavalkyaDhŚ 1.10cd]
[85.4]     garbhādhānam ṛtau puṃsassavanaṃ spandanāt purā //" iti [YājñavalkyaDhŚ 1.11ab]
[85.5]     manu: "niṣekādiśmaśānāntāḥ mantrair yasyoditāḥ kriyāḥ /
[85.6]     tasya śāstre 'dhikāro 'smin jñeyo nānyasya kasyacit //" iti [ManuDhŚ 2.16]
[85.7-8]     atra manuvākye "yasya - tasya - kasyacit" ityādi śabdānāṃ vaiyarthyaprasaṅgāt "sarveṣāṃ niṣekāditvaṃ samānam" iti vaktum ayuktam.
[85.9]     āśvamedhike bhagavān: "vaidikaiḥ karmabhiḥ puṇyaiḥ niṣekādir dvijanmanām /
[85.10]     kāryaḥ śarīrasaṃskāraḥ pāvanaḥ pretya ceha ca // [MB.h 14, App. 4.2513]
[85.11]     gārbhair homair jātakarmanāmacaulopanāyanaiḥ / [MBh 14, App. 4.2514]
[85.12]     svādhyāyaiś ca tapobhiś ca vivāhasnātakavrataiḥ // [MBh 14, App. 4.2515]
[85.13]     mahāyajñaiś ca yajñaiś ca brāhmīyaṃ kriyate tanuḥ /" iti [MBh 14, App. 4.2516]
[85.14]     evam anyatrāpi draṣṭavyam.
[85.15]     bodhāyanena "yato etad dhutam" ityādinā sūtrādau vivāhapūrvakatvenoktam.
[85.16-21]     āpastambena "atha karmāṇy ācārādyāni gṛhyante" ity ārabhya "upanayanaṃ vyākhyāsyāma" iti. bhāradvājasatyāṣāḍhābhyām āśvalāyanena ca "uktāni vaitānikānī"ty ārabhya vaiśvadevapūrvakatvena. drāhyāyaṇena "athāto gṛhyakarmāṇi, udagayanapūrvapakṣa" ity ārabhya ācārāditvena. kātyāyanaś ca "athāto gṛhyasthālīpākānāṃ karme"ty ārabhya pratipāditavān. "atha niṣekādisaṃskārān vyākhyāsyāma" ity ārabhya niṣekapūrvakatvena bhagavatā vikhanasaiva pratipāditam.
[85.22-24]     evaṃ ca niṣekapūrvakatvenoktatvād asya sarvasūtrottamatvaṃ etatsūtroktadharmānuṣṭhānenaiva tatsūtriṇāṃ sarvotkṛṣṭatvañ copapadyate iti śrutismṛtipurāṇādimukhena pratipāditam iti nirūpitaḥ pañcamo hetuḥ.
[85.25]     iti pañcamahetunirūpaṇam




     [ṣaṣṭhahetunirūpaṇam]

     [vaikhānasasūtrasyāṣṭādaśasaṃskārapratipādakatvam]

[86.1]     atha ṣaṣṭhahetunirūpaṇam
[86.2-4]     athedānīṃ śrīvaikhānasasūtroktadharmānuṣṭhātṝṇām eva sarvebhyaḥ śreṣṭhamatvaṃ sūtrāntareṣv anuktaṃ śrutisiddhāṣṭādaśasaṃskāravatvaṃ kriyābāhulyañ ca sambhavatīti jñāpayituṃ "aṣṭādaśasaṃskārapratipādakatvād" iti ṣaṣṭho hetur nirūpyate. tathā hi:
[86.5-8]     "atha niṣekādisaṃskārān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ṛtusaṅgamana-garbādhāna-puṃsavana-sīmanta-viṣṇubali-jātakarmotthāna-nāmakaraṇānnaprāśana-pravāsāgamana-piṇḍavardhana-caulopanayana-pārāyaṇa-vratabandhavisargopākarma-samāvartana-pāṇigrahaṇānīty aṣṭādaśa-saṃskārāś śārīrāḥ" iti aṣṭādaśasaṃskārāḥ sūtre pratipāditāḥ. ete ca

     ["aṣṭādaśoktam avaraṃ yeṣu karme" ti śrutyarthavicāraḥ]

[86.9-10]     śrutisiddhāḥ. yathā muṇḍopaniṣadi - "plavā hy ete adṛḍhā yajñarūpā aṣṭādaśoktam avaraṃ yeṣu karma. etac chreyo ye 'bhinandanti mūḍhā jarāmṛtyuṃ te punar evāpi yanti" iti.
[86.11]     atra kecid evam ūcuḥ: "yajñasya rtvijaṣ ṣoḍaśa sadasyassaptadaśaḥ yajamāno 'ṣṭādaśaḥ"
[86.12-14]     iti śrutyanusāreṇa "aṣṭādaśoktam avaraṃ yeṣu karme"ty atra yajamānādaya eva vivakṣitā iti. tad asat. "aṣṭādaśoktam avaraṃ karmayeṣu" ity uktatvāt. ṛtvigyajamānādayo hi yāgakartāraḥ na tu karma. "yeṣu" ity asya padasya yeṣu sūtreṣv ity arthaḥ.
[86.15-18]     'avaraṃ karma'; jātakādayaḥ, smārtakarmatvāt. ātmaguṇarahitā yāgadayaḥ jātakarmādayaś ca. 'adṛḍhāḥ plavāḥ'; saṃsārottārakā na bhavanti. tathā ca atra adṛḍhaplavatvena ninditā saṃskārāḥ yāgādayaś ca ātmaguṇarahitā eva vivakṣitāḥ. tat sahitānāṃ teṣāṃ mokṣasādhakatvam. yathā:

     [ātmaguṇarahitānāṃ saṃskārāṇāṃ bandhakatvam]

[86.19-21]     gautamadharme: "yasya tu khalu catvāriṃśatsaṃskārā na cāṣṭāvātmaguṇāḥ na sa brahmaṇas sāyujyaṃ sālokyañ ca gacchati. yasya khalu catvāriṃśatsaṃskārāṇām ekadeśo py aṣṭāv ātmaṇāḥ atha sa brahmaṇas sāyujyaṃ sālokyañ ca gacchati gacchatī"ti.

     [aṣṭānām ātmaguṇānāṃ lakṣaṇāni]

[86.22-23]     'aṣṭāv ātmaguṇāḥ': "dayā samastabhūteṣu kṣāntir anasūyā śaucam anāyāso maṅgalyam akārpaṇyam aspṛhe" ti. tallakṣaṇāni tu:

     [tatra dayālakṣaṇaṃ]

[86.24]     "abandhau bandhuvarge vā mitre dveṣṭari vā tathā /
[86.25]     āpanne rakṣaṇaṃ yat tu dayaiṣā parikīrtitā //




     [tatra kṣamālakṣaṇam]

[87.1]     bāhye vā 'bhyantare vāpi duḥkha utpādite paraiḥ /
[87.2]     na prakupyati no hanti sā kṣamā parikīrtitā //

     [tatra anasūyālakṣaṇam]

[87.3]     saguṇān guṇi no hanti (?) stauti mandaguṇān api /
[87.4]     nānyadoṣeṣu ramate sā 'nasūyā prakīrtitā //

     [tatra śaucalakṣaṇam]

[87.5]     abhakṣyaparihāraś ca saṃsargaś cāpy aninditaiḥ /
[87.6]     svadharme ca vyavasthānaṃ śaucam etad udāhṛtam //

     [tatra anāyāsalakṣaṇam]

[87.7]     śarīraṃ pīḍyate yena suśubhenāpi karmaṇā /
[87.8]     atyantaṃ tannakartavyam anāyāsas sa ucyate //

     [tatra maṅgalyalakṣaṇam]

[87.9]     praśastācaraṇaṃ nityam apraśastavisarjanam /
[87.10]     etad dhi maṅgalaṃ proktam ṛṣibhis tattvadarśibhiḥ //

     [tatra akārpaṇyalakṣaṇam]

[87.11]     stokād api pradātavyam adīnenāntarātmanā /
[87.12]     ahanyahani yatkiñcid akārpaṇyaṃ tad ucyate //

     [tatra aspṛhālakṣaṇam]

[87.13]     yathotpanneṣu santoṣaḥ kartavyas svāgatair dhanaiḥ /
[87.14]     parārthān nābhibhāṣeta sā 'spṛhā parikīrtitā //" iti
