[87.15]     prasaṅgād idam uktam. prakṛtam anusarāmaḥ.

     [sāttvikarājasatāmasapurāṇāni]

[87.16-17]     atha aṣṭādaśasmṛtyuktāni aṣṭādaśapurāṇeṣūktānīti vā muṇḍakaśrutyartho 'stu iti cet. tad apy asat. smṛtipurāṇādiṣu aṣṭādaśakarmeti viśiṣyānuktatvāt.
[87.18-20]     atra "aṣṭādaśoktam avaraṃ karma yeṣv" iti sāmānyenoktatvāt tatroktānāṃ yogādīnām apy apavargaprāpakatvābhāvāt punar api jarāmṛtyuprāpakatvāc ca na smṛtipurāṇeṣūktānīti vaktuṃ yuktaṃ kiñ ca
[87.21]     pādmapurāṇe: "vaiṣṇavaḥ nāradīyañ ca tathā bhāgavataṃ śubhaṃ /
[87.22]     gāruḍañ ca tathā pādmaṃ vārāhaṃ śubhadarśane // [Padma.P uttarabhāga 236.19]




     [sātvikapurāṇaśraiṣṭhyam]

[88.1]     sāttvikāni purāṇāni vijñeyāni ca ṣaṭ pṛthak /
[88.2]     brahmāṇḍaṃ brahmakaivartaṃ mārkaṇḍeyaṃ tathaiva ca // [Padma.P uttarabhāga 236.20]
[88.3]     bhaviṣyad vāmanaṃ brāhmaṃ rājasāni ca ṣaḍvidhāḥ / [PadmaP uttarabhāga 236.21ab]
[88.4]     mātsyaṃ kaurmaṃ tathā laiṅgaṃ śaivaṃ skāndaṃ tathaiva ca /
[88.5]     āgneyañ ca ṣaḍ etāni tāmasāni nibodha me //" iti [PadmaP uttarabhāga 236.18]
[88.6]     mātsye: "saṅkīrṇās tāmasāś caiva rājasās sāttvikās tathā /
[88.7]     kalpāś caturvidhāḥ proktāḥ brahmaṇo divasāś ca te /
[88.8]     yasmin kalpe tu yatproktaṃ purāṇaṃ brahmaṇā purā // [MatsyaP]
[88.9]     tasya tasya tu māhātmyaṃ tena rūpeṇa vartate /
[88.10]     saṅkīrṇeṣu sarasvatyāḥ pitṝṇāñ ca nigadyate // [MatsyaP]
[88.11]     agneś śivasya māhātmyaṃ tāmaseṣu prakīrtyate /
[88.12]     rājaseṣu tu māhātmyam adhikaṃ brahmaṇo viduḥ // [MatsyaP]
[88.13]     sāttvikeṣv atha kalpeṣu māhātmyam adhikaṃ hareḥ /
[88.14]     teṣv eva yogasaṃsiddhā gamiṣyanti parāṃ gatiṃ //" iti [MatsyaP]
[88.15]     pādme: "vāsiṣṭhañ caiva hārītaṃ vyāsaṃ pārāśaraṃ tathā // [PadmaP uttarabhāga 236.23cd]
[88.16]     bhāradvājaṃ kāśyapīyaṃ smṛtiṣaṭkantu sāttvikam /
[88.17]     mānavaṃ yajñavalkyañ ca ātreyaṃ dākṣyam eva ca // [PadmaP uttarabhāga 236.24]
[88.18]     kātyāyanaṃ vaiṣṇavañ ca smṛtiṣaṭkantu rājasam /
[88.19]     gautamaṃ bārhaspatyañ ca sāṃvartañ ca yamasmṛtiḥ // [PadmaP uttarabhāga 236.25]
[88.20]     śāmbham auśanasañ caiva smṛtiṣaṭkantu tāmasam //" iti [PadmaP uttarabhāga 236.26ab]
[88.21]     tathā: "sāttvikā mokṣadā jñeyā rājasāḥ svargadāḥ smṛtāḥ / [PadmaP uttarabhāga 236.21cd]
[88.22]     tathaiva tāmasā devi nirayaprāptihetavaḥ //" [PadmaP uttarabhāga 236.22ab]
[88.23-24]     ityādi vacanasiddhasātvikapurāṇeṣu pratipāditānāṃ bhagavadārādhanādīnāṃ mokṣahetutvasmaraṇāt, sāmanyena aṣṭādaśapurāṇoktakarmaṇāṃ jīrṇaplavasādṛśyaṃ vaktuṃ na śakyam.





     [vaikhānase kriyābāhulyam]

[89.1-2]     anyathā svargamokṣanirayāṇām ekarūpatvāṅgīkārāpātāt. ataḥ śrīmadvaikhānasasūtroktāṣṭādaśasaṃskārā evety avagantavyam. bodhāyanasūtre saṃskārasaṅkhyā na kṛtā.
[89.3-5]     āpastambādināpi pañcamahāyajñānāṃ nityahomasya ca pākayajñatvenāṅgīkārāt ete ṣoḍasaṃskārā iti vivicyānuktatvāt aparasaṃskārapratipādanābhāvāc ca na tatroktāḥ gṛhītuṃ śakyāḥ.
[89.6-8]     śrīvaikhānase tu kriyābāhulyam apy asti. tathā hi. aṣṭādaśasaṃskārāḥ pākayajñāś ca pṛthaktvenopapaditāḥ. varṣavardhanādyāstu viśeṣāḥ. pañcamahāyajñasahitā dvāviṃśadyajñāḥ - pañcamahāyajñānām ekatvam. aparaś cāṣṭādaśavyatirikta iti.
[89.9]     kriyābāhulyena kim ādhikyam iti cet - ucyate. muṇḍopaniṣadi -
[89.10]     "kriyāvān eṣa brahmavidāṃ variṣṭhaḥ" iti "kriyāvantaḥ śrotriyā brahmaṇiṣṭhāḥ svayaṃ juhvata
[89.11]     ekarṣiṃ śraddhayantaḥ. teṣām evaitāṃ brahmavidyāṃ vadeta" iti ca śrūyate.
[89.12-15]     bodhāyanaḥ: "tasmād yaḥ kaścana kriyāvān satām anumatācāras sa śrotriyas sa eva vijñeyas sa eva vijñeyaḥ" iti. kiñca - karmabhūyastvāt phalabhūyastvañ ca "yathopāsanaṃ phalam" iti nyāyāt siddhyati. ataḥ: aṣṭādaśasaṃskārāpratipādakatvād asya sūtrasya śreṣṭḥatvaṃ etas sūtriṇāṃ sarvotkṛṣṭatvañ copapadyata iti nirūpitaḥ ṣaṣṭho hetuḥ.
[89.16]     iti ṣaṣṭhahetunirūpaṇam.





     [saptamahetunirūpaṇam]

[90.1-3]     atha śrīvaikhānasasūtrasya itarasūtrāpekṣābhāvāt svātantryam astīti jñāpayituṃ sāṅgakriyākalāpavattvād iti saptamo hetur nirūpyate. tathā hi: atrasūtre aṣṭādaśasaṃskārāḥ śārīrāḥ prasiddhās sāṅgāḥ eva pratipāditāḥ.
[90.4-8]     nanu - aṅkurārpaṇaśatābhiṣekāgnidvayasaṃsargaputraparigrahabrahmamedhavṛṣotsarjanādipratipādanābhavāt sāṅgakriyākalāpavattvaṃ nāstīti cet - tad asat. iyaṃ śaṅkā śrīvaikhānasasūtrasvarūpānabhijñatvakṛtā. idaṃ sūtram ekādaśapraśnātmakam. atra na pratipāditānīti uktiḥ, atiriktatvena gṛhyapariśiṣṭasadbhāvājñānāt. gṛhyapariśiṣṭasadbhāvaḥ katham avagamyate iti cet - ucyate.
[90.9]     "athāṅkurārpaṇavidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ" ity ārabhya khaṇḍadvayenāṅkurārpaṇam uktam.
[90.10-11]     "sāyaṃ sthaṇḍile sahasraṃ piṣṭena somarūpāṇi karotī"ty atra viśeṣeṇa sthaṇḍilādipratipādanam.
[90.12]     "śatābhiṣekaṃ pūrvāhṇe puṇyāhaṃ dvijabhojanam //" ity ārabhya [GṛhyapariśiṣṭaS]
[90.13]     "sāyaṃ gomayasaṃlipte sthaṇḍile prāg anunnate /
[90.14]     prācīrekhā dvipañcāśat saṃkhyayā tatra saṃlikhet // [GṛhyapariśiṣṭaS.]
[90.15]     udīcīś ca tathā rekhā dvatriṃśatsaṃkhyayā likhet //" [GṛhyapariśiṣṭaS]
[90.16]     ityādinā śatābhiṣekaprayogaś ca uktaḥ.
[90.17]     tathā "dhautavastradhāriṇau syātām" ity ārabhya [GṛhyapariśiṣṭaS]
[90.18]     "dīpādyalaṅkṛte gehe vrīhīn āstīrya tatra vai /
[90.19]     carmābhāve kaṭaṃ vāpi tad ūrdhve vastram āstared //" iti [GṛhyapariśiṣṭaS]
[90.20]     "śeṣahome 'ntahomānte āsīnau tatra carmaṇi /
[90.21]     visṛjāmi vratañ ceti tadvrataṃ carma santyajet //" [GṛhyapariśiṣṭaS]
[90.22]     ityādinā agnidvayasaṃsargaprakāraś ca pratipāditaḥ.





[91.1]     putraparigrahaprakāraś ca
[91.2]     "tyāgavikrayadāneṣu prokteṣv api tatas smṛtau /
[91.3]     ekaṃ na dadyān no gṛhyāt na strī bhartrananujñayā //" ityādinā [GṛhyapariśiṣṭaS]
[91.4]     brahmamedhavidhis tu
[91.5]     "saṃskāro brahmaniṣṭhānāṃ sadācāravatām api /
[91.6]     brahmamedho 'tiphalado na sarveṣāṃ dvijanmanām //" ityādinā [GṛhyapariśiṣṭaS]
[91.7]     vṛṣotsargavidhis tu
[91.8]     "vṛṣotsargavidhiṃ vakṣye yena pretatvamocanam /
[91.9]     snātvātha vāstuhomānte pretatvasya vimuktaye //" ityādibhiḥ [GṛhyapariśiṣṭaS]
[91.10]     evaṃ atrānuktāni sarvāṇi gṛhyapariśiṣṭe proktāni iti veditavyam.
[91.11-15]     bodhāyanādibhir apy ete sāṅgā eva pratipāditā iti cet - na. "sati kuḍye cikrakarme" ti nyāyena pradhānakarmāṇi pratipāditāni cet aṅgavicāraḥ kartavyaḥ. sandhyopāsane arghyapradānādikam anuktam. vānaprasthāśramasvīkaraṇādikam api na pratipāditam. vānaprasthāśramasvīkaraṇāsvīkaraṇāraṇyāharaṇapātralakṣaṇādiṣu vaikhānasasūtrāpekṣā asty eva. devatāpratiṣṭhādikam uktaṃ lakṣaṇam anuktam.
[91.16-18]     āpastambādibhiḥ sandhyopāsanāṅkurapratisaradevatārādhanayajñopavītadhāraṇādikam apy anuktam. āpastambādīnām anyonyāpekṣā prasiddhā. anyonyāpekṣā nāma asvātantryam aṅgahīnavat.
[91.19]     manu: "yad yat paravaśaṃ karma tat tad yatnena varjayet // [ManuDhŚ 4.159cd]
[91.20]     sarvaṃ paravaśaṃ duḥkhaṃ sarvam ātmavaśaṃ sukham /
[91.21]     etad vidyāt samāsena lakṣaṇaṃ sukhaduḥkhayoḥ //" [ManuDhŚ 4.160]
[91.22-23]     anena anantasthiraphalaprāptir darśitā. ataḥ sūtrāntaranairapekṣyāt sarvasūtrottamatvaṃ svātantryañ ca ghaṭata iti nirūpitas saptamo hetuḥ.
[91.24]     iti saptamahetunirūpaṇam





     [atha aṣṭamahetunirūpaṇam]

     [vaikhānasasūtrasya akhilaśiṣṭaparigṛhītatvam]

[92.1-3]     idānīṃ tāvat śrutismṛtipurāṇādibhiḥ sarvottaratvenāvagatasya śrīvaikhānasasūtrasya akhilaśiṣṭaparigṛhītatvam astīti darśayituṃ manvādyaiḥ svīkṛtatvād iti aṣṭamo hetuḥ nirūpyate. tathā hi
[92.5]     manu: "ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi dharmaṃ vaikhānasāśramam //" ity ārabhya
[92.6]     "puṣpamūlaphalair vāpi kevalair vartayet sadā /
[92.7]     kālapakvaiḥ svayaṃ śīrṇair vaikhānasamate sthitaḥ //" iti [ManuDhŚ 6.21]
[92.8]     vyāsa: "mūlair eke phalair eke puṣpair eke dṛḍhavratāḥ / [MBh 12.236.13cd]
[92.9]     vartayanti yathānyāyaṃ vaikhānasamate sthitāḥ //" iti [MBh 12.236.14ab]
[92.10]     gautama: śrāmaṇakenāgnim ādhāyāgrāmyabhojī" iti
[92.11]     yama: śrāmaṇakena vidhānena sāyaṃ prātar upaspṛśet. iti
[92.12-13]     śaṅkhalikhitau: śrāmaṇakenāgnim ādhāya kāle kuruvinda - veṇu - śyāmākanīvārādibhir vartayet. iti.
[92.14-16]     hārīta: vānaprastho grāmyā oṣadhī parivarjayet. tretāgnīnāṃ sthāne śrāmaṇakaṃ vāgnim ādhāya valkalaśāṇacarmakuśamuñjavidalakaṃ vā vasāno vaikhānasaproktena vidhinā vānaprastho vikhanā bhavati. anujñāyiko 'nuprasthāyikaś" ceti
[92.17]     vasiṣṭha: śrāmaṇakenāgnim ādhāyāhitāgnir vṛkṣamūlikaḥ. iti [VāsiṣṭhaDhŚ 9.10]
[92.18]     bodhāyana: "vānaprastho vaikhānasaśāstrasamudācāraḥ" [BaudhDhS 12.6.11.14]
[92.19-21]     āpastamba: "ekāgnir aniketaḥ syād" iti. asya dharmakarpardī "gārhapatyādīnāṃ tretāgnīnāṃ sthāne yasyaiko 'gniḥ aupāsana eva - vaikhānasasūtre dṛṣṭatvāt, pāṇigrahaṇanimitvadvādaupāsanasya.
[92.22-23]     jaiminīyasūtre saumikacāturmāsyaprakāraṇe. "bhāradvājapūrvaṃ yathā vaikhānasapūrvaṃ pañcaḥ" meti (?)





     [akhilaśiṣṭaparigrahasya prāmāṇyātiśayahetutvam]

[93.1-2]     atrobhayatra ātrivyākhyānam - ṣoḍaśartvijāṃ madhye bhāradvājasūtriṇaṃ prastotāraṃ vaikhānasasūtriṇaṃ pratihartāraṃ varayet" iti.
[93.3]     kapiñjalasaṃhitāyām:
[93.4]     "yājanādhyāpanayutaḥ śiṣyānugrahakārakaḥ /
[93.5]     ācārya iti vijñeyo mantratantraparāyaṇaḥ // [KapiñjalaS]
[93.6]     āśrame vā vane vā 'pi putradārasamāhitaḥ /
[93.7]     aṣṭākṣaraparo nityaṃ sa vaikhānasa ucyate // [KapiñjalaS]
[93.8]     grāmyadharmāṇi sarvāṇi varjayed vanavāsakaḥ /
[93.9]     valkalājinasaṃvītaḥ sa maunīty abhidhīyate //" iti [KapiñjalaS]
[93.10]     pādme dvādaśākṣaraprakāre
[93.11]     "..... putradārasamanvitaḥ /
[93.12]     vane vā pattane vāpi japed vaikhānasaḥ śuciḥ //
[93.13]     viyuktaḥ putradārādyaiḥ svayam eva vane sthitaḥ //" [PadmaP ]
[93.14]     anyair api evam evoktam.
[93.15-16]     akhilaśiṣṭaparigrahe ko viśeṣa iti cet - akhilaśiṣṭaparigrahāt prāmāṇyātiśayo 'stīty avagamyate.
[93.17]     āśvamedhike: "dharmaṃ jijñāsamānānāṃ pramāṇaṃ prathamaṃ śrutiḥ / [MBh 14, App. 4.2492]
[93.18]     dvitīyaṃ dharmaśāstraṃ hi tṛtīyaṃ lokasaṅgrahaḥ //" iti [MBh 14, App. 4.2493]
[93.19]     manu: "vidvadbhis sevitaṃ samyak nityam adveṣarāgibhiḥ /
[93.20]     hṛdayenābhyanujñāto yo dharmas taṃ nibodhata //" iti [ManuDhŚ 2.1]
[93.21]     yājñavalkya: "catvāro vedadharmajñāḥ parṣat traividyam eva vā /
[93.22]     sā brūte 'yaṃ sa dharmaḥ syād eko vādhyātmavittamaḥ // [YājñavalkyaDhŚ 1.9]
[93.23]     vedāḥ pramāṇaṃ smṛtayaḥ pramāṇaṃ dharmārthayuktaṃ vacanaṃ pramāṇaṃ /
[93.24]     yasya pramāṇaṃ na bhavet pramāṇaṃ kas tasya kuryād vacanaṃ pramāṇaṃ //





[94.1]     na yasya vedā na ca dharmaśāstraṃ
[94.2]     na vṛddhavākyaṃ ca bhavet pramāṇam /
[94.3]     so 'dharmakṛd duṣṭahato durātmā
[94.4]     svātmāpi tasyaiva bhavet pramāṇam (?) //" [YājñavalkyaDhŚ ]

     [smṛter vedamūlatve tredhā nirvāhaḥ]

[94.5-9]     smṛter api vedamūlatve tredhā nirvāhaḥ kṛtaḥ. nityānumeyaśrutimūlatvam prābhākarāḥ. "teṣām utsannāḥ pāṭhāḥ prayogād anumīyanta" ity utsannaśākhāmūlatvam āpastambādyāḥ. tat prābhākarādhibhiḥ dūṣitaṃ bhāṣyakārānabhimatañ ca. prābhākarapakṣe 'pi nityānumeyaśrutimūlatve akṣaraśo vā ānupūrvīviśeṣaviśiṣṭatvena vā. akṣaraśa iti yady ucyate tarhi kaṭatapayādīnām api nityānumeyaśrutimūlatvāt smṛtitvaṃ syāt.
[94.10-15]     ānupūrvīviśeṣaviśiṣṭatveneti cet nityānumeyatvaṃ bhajyet iti. utsannaśākhāmūlatvam iti pakṣe śākhāsu tatratatrotsannā vā utaikā śākhā utsannā vā. tatratatreti cet na - padakramādirūpeṇādhīyamānatvād utsannaśākhāmūlatvaṃ na ghaṭate. ekaivotsanneti cet - na. viṣṇor aṃśāvatārasya tapoyogabalopetasya sarvavedasākṣāt kāravato vyāsasya ajñātāśāsaṃbhavena ekasyāpi śiṣyasya tad adhyāpanasāmarthyasambhavāt tathā vaktum ayuktatvād iti. ato viprakīrṇaśākhāmūlatvaṃ vaktavyam. tathoktam.
[94.16]     "durbodhā vaidikāś śabdāḥ prakīrṇatvāc ca ye khilāḥ /
[94.17]     tadjñais ta eva sṣaṣṭārthāḥ smṛtitantre pratiṣṭhitāḥ //" iti
[94.18-20]     ataḥ śrutismṛtipurāṇādibhiḥ prāmāṇatvenāvagatasya śrīvaikhānasasūtrasya akhilaśiṣṭaparigrahāt prāmāṇyātiśayo 'stīti "manvādyais svīkṛtatvād" iti nirūpito 'ṣṭamo hetuḥ.
[94.21]     ity aṣṭamahetunirūpaṇam






     [navamahetunirūpaṇam]

     [vaikhānasasūtriṇāṃ nārāyaṇaikaparatvam]
[95.1-3]     athedānīm āpastabādisūtrāntaraniṣṭhānāṃ sūtrakārād ārabhya avicchinnatvena paramparayā ekāntitvaṃ nāstīti jñāpayituṃ vaikhānasasūtriṇām eva tat sambhavatīti darśayituṃ.
[95.4]     "pratyakṣaṃ anumānañ ca śāstrañ ca vividhāgamam /
[95.5]     trayaṃ suviditaṃ jñeyaṃ dharmasiddhim abhīpsatā //" [ManuDhŚ 12.105]
[95.6-7]     iti manusmaraṇānusāreṇa pratyakṣādibhir avagamayituñ ca akhilajagadekakāraṇabhūtaśrīmannārāyaṇaikaparatvād iti navamo hetur nirūpyate.
[95.8]     asya sūtrasya nārāyaṇaikaparatve:

     [tatra ṣaḍvidhatātparyaliṅgāni]

[95.9]     "upakramopasaṃhārāv abhyāso 'pūrvatā phalam /
[95.10]     arthavādopapattī ca liṅgaṃ tātparyanirṇaye //"

     [nārāyaṇasyaiva parabrahmaśabdavācyatvam]

[95.11-17]     ity uktāni ṣaḍvidhāni tātparyaliṅgāni santi. tathā hi ādyapraśne prathamakhāṇḍe "nārāyaṇaparāyaṇa" ity uktam. evaṃ "sadādhyātmarato dhyānayogī nārāyaṇaparaṃ brahma paśyan dhāraṇaṃ dhārayed akṣaraṃ paraṃ brahmāpnoti - "nārāyaṇaparaṃ brahmeti śrutiḥ" ity upasaṃhāre sannyāsavidhau pratipāditam. sandhyopāsanādi - puṇyāhāghārāntahoma - nāndīmukhopanayana - pāṇigrahaṇaparyanteṣu antakarmaṇi ca ato devādivaiṣṇavā mantrāḥ viniyuktāḥ. evaṃ āghāraprakaraṇe "śaro 'ṅgāre 'gnau juhuyād" iti sūtreṇa idhmādhānaṃ taittirīyabrāhmaṇavākyānusāreṇa parabrahmāgnau vihitam.






     [brahmarudrādīnāṃ yajñāṃśabhāktvaṃ bhagavatprasādalabdham]

[95.18-96.5]      parabrahmaśabdābhidheyaś ca bhagavān nārāyaṇa eveti vedānteṣu nirṇītam. tathāhi: "sad eva somyedamagra āsīt, ekam evādvitīyam" ityādibhiḥ pratipannasya abhinnanimittopādānakāraṇasya "yato vā imāni bhūtāni jāyante - tadbrahme"tyādinā jagatkāraṇatvaṃ brahmaśabdavācyatvañ ca pratipādyate. tasya "satyaṃ jñānam anantaṃ brahme" tyādinā śodhakavākyena svarūpaṃ nirūpyate. satyatvādiviśiṣṭasya tasya "ānando brahma" iti niratiśayānandarūpatvaṃ pratipādyate. etādṛśabrahmarūpaṃ vastu "nārāyaṇaparaṃ brahma" "tattvaṃ nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ" "eko ha vai nārāyaṇa āsīt" "apahatapāpmā divyo deva eko nārāyaṇaḥ" ityādi vākyaiḥ śrīmannārāyaṇa eveti niyamyate. evañ ca "adhyūhante" iti taittirīyavākyaśeṣasthabrahmaśabdo 'pi nārāyaṇapara eveti prakṛtasūtroktedhmādhānam api nārāyaṇaparam eva.
[96.6-9]     evam ādhāne - "dhyāyan nārāyaṇam upoṣya" iti, agnihotre - bhūmānaṃ viṣṇuṃ dhyāyet" iti, darśapūrṇamāse - "udita āditye dhyāyan nārāyaṇaṃ 'viṣṇor nu kam'; iti japitvā" iti, some ca - "nārāyaṇaparāyaṇas tūṣṇīm āste" iti ca sarvatrāpi abhyāsena nārāyaṇaparatvenoktatvāt idaṃ sūtraṃ nārāyaṇaparam eva.
[96.10-14]     nanu - atra sūtre pravāsāgamane āśvayujyāñ ca "pradakṣiṇam arcanaṃ praṇāmo guhasya" - "bhavaṃ devam āvāhya" ity uktatvāt sarvatra nārāyaṇaparatvam asyeti kathaṃ vaktuṃ śakyate iti cet - ucyate. "aṅgāny anyā devatā" iti aṅgabhūtānāṃ brahmarudrādīnām api yajñāṃśabhāktvaṃ bhagavatprasādalabdham iti bhāratādināvagamyate - tathāhi
[96.15]     "tatas te surās sarve brahmā te ca maharṣayaḥ // [MBh 12.327.48cd]
[96.16]     vedadṛṣṭena vidhinā vaiṣṇavaṃ kratum ārabhan /
[96.17]     tasmin satre tathā brahmā svayaṃ bhāgam akalpayat /
[96.18]     devā mahārṣayaś caiva sarve bhāgān akalpayan // [MBh 12.327.49]
[96.19]     te kārtayugadharmāṇo bhāgāḥ paramasaṃskṛtāḥ /
[96.20]     prāpur ādityavarṇaṃ taṃ puruṣaṃ tamasaḥ param // [MBh 12.327.50]
[96.21]     śrībhagavān: yena yaḥ kalpito bhāgaḥ sa tathā samupāgataḥ /
[96.22]     prīto 'haṃ pradiśāmy adya phalam āvṛttilakṣaṇam // [MB.h 12.327.52]
[96.23]     yajñīye cāpi yakṣyanti sarvalokeṣu vai surāḥ /
[96.24]     kalpayiṣyanti vo bhāgāṃs te narā vedakalpitān // [MBh 12.327.54]





     [rudrīdīnāṃ nārāyaṇāṅgatayā pūjārhatvam]

[97.1]     yo me yathā kalpitavān bhāgam asmin mahākratau /
[97.2]     sa mahāyajñabhāgārho vedasūtre mayā kṛtaḥ //" iti [MBh 12.327.55]
[97.3]     śrībhāgavate: "ahaṃ bhavo dakṣabhṛgupradhānāḥ prajeśabhūteśasureśamukhyāḥ /
[97.4]     sarve vayaṃ yanniyamaṃ prapannā mūrdhnārpitaṃ lokadhuraṃ vahāmaḥ //"
[97.5]     evaṃ ca bhavādīnām api nārāyaṇāṅgatvena pūjārhatvāvagamāt.
[97.6]     "aṅgabhāvena devānām arcanaṃ na niṣiddhyate /
[97.7]     svatantrabuddhyā kurvan hi brāhmaṇo narakaṃ vrajet //
[97.8]     brahmāṇam indram agniṃ vā harer āvaraṇaṃ vinā /
[97.9]     yas tu sampūjayed vipraḥ sa pāṣaṇḍī bhaved dhruvam //"
[97.10]     ityādinā aṅgabhāvena teṣām arcanaṃ kurvato doṣābhāvasmaraṇāc ca sūtre tathoktiḥ.
[97.11]     tathā: "anyatra tvāṃ samāropya yady upāsā vidhīṃyate /
[97.12]     sā vṛttiḥ pracyutā proktā tava tattvaṃ tathaiva ca // [KJ.K ]
[97.13]     tvayi sarvaṃ samāropya yady upāsā vidhīyate /
[97.14]     sā vṛttiḥ sakalā jñeyā tava tattvaṃ tavaiva hi //" [KJK ]
[97.15-18]     iti jñānakāṇḍe kaśyapenopāsanasvarūpabhedapradarśanāt "viṣṇor nityārcā sarvadevārcā bhavatī"ti mukhyatvena sūtreṇa pratipāditatvāt pracyutiphalapradatvābhāvāc ca teṣām aṅgabhāvena pūjanaṃ yujyate. āpastambādisūtreṣu sarvasaṃskārāṇāṃ sadvārakatvena pratipādanāt nārāyaṇaikaparatvena sakṛd api smaraṇābhavāt teṣāṃ na nārāyaṇaikaparatvam.

     [āpastambādisūtrāṇāṃ nārāyaṇaikaparatvābhāvaḥ]

[97.19-21]     nanu bodhāyanenāpi "athāto viṣṇupratiṣṭhākalpaṃ vyākhyasyāmo dvādaśyām ekādaśyāṃ śroṇāyāṃ vā yāni cānyāni śubhanakṣatrāṇi" ity ārabhya "dvādaśanāmabhiḥ amuṣmai svāhā amuṣmai svāhā" ityādinā homādikam uktā.
[97.22]     "tvām ekam ādyaṃ puruṣaṃ purātanaṃ
[97.23]     nārāyaṇaṃ viśvasṛjaṃ yajāmahe /
[97.24]     tvam eva yajño vihito vighneyaḥ
[97.25]     tvam ātmanātman pratigṛhṇīṣva havyam //" [BaudhGṛŚeṣS 2.13.36]





     [āpastambādīnāṃ nānādevatāparatvam]

[98.1-5]     iti nārāyaṇaikaparatvena pratipādanāt kathaṃ teṣāṃ nārāyaṇaikaparatvaṃ nāstīty ucyata iti cet - satyam. āpastambādīnām ācāryeṇānena bodhāyanena nārāyaṇaikaparatvena pratiṣṭhādikam anuktam. kintu. "atha rudrapratiṣṭhāvidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ. caturthyām aṣṭamyām ārdrāyām apabharaṇyāṃ vā yāni cānyāni śubhanakṣatrāṇi" iti prakṛtya "bhavāya devāya svāhe"tyādibhiḥ "bhavasya devasya patnyai svāhe"tyādibhiś ca homādikam uktvā [BaudhGṛŚeṣS 2.16.1-2]
[98.6]     "tvām ekam ādyaṃ puruṣaṃ purātanaṃ
[98.7]     rudraṃ śivaṃ viśvasṛjaṃ yajāmahe /
[98.8]     tvam eva yajño vihito vidheyas
[98.9]     tvam ātmanātman pratigṛhṇīṣva havyaṃ //" [BaudhGṛŚeṣS 2.16.39]
[98.10]     iti śivapratiṣṭhā, evaṃ "athāto mahādevasyāharahaḥ paricaryāvidhiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ"
[98.11-15]     ity ārabhya "mahādevam āvāhayet - āyātu bhagavān mahādeva" iti pṛthaktvena rudrapūjā ca pratipāditā. tathā - anyatra "athāto 'rdhamāse 'rdhamāse 'ṣṭamyāṃ brāhmaṇāḥ striyaś cāhuḥ" ity ārabhya "atha pradoṣe rudraṃ virūpākṣaṃ sapanīkaṃ sasutaṃ sapārṣadam" ityādibhiḥ rudrāvāhanam uktam. evaṃ "ādityam ambikāṃ viṣṇuṃ gaṇanāthaṃ maheśvaram" iti pañcapūjā ca. ataḥ bodhāyanasūtraṃ nārāyaṇaikaparaṃ na bhavati.
[98.16-18]     atha āpastambādayaḥ kiṃ nārāyaṇaikaparaḥ - ata rudraparāḥ āhosvit nānādevatāparāḥ?. nārāyaṇaikaparā iti cen na. jātikulācārādiṣv āgotraprathamād ārabhya:
[98.19]     "śvaśrūrasya digambaravratavatī sambandhinas saugatāḥ /
[98.20]     mātā cāsya pitā ca pāśupatinau vaiśeṣiko deśikaḥ /
[98.21]     bhrātā tiṣṭhati sāṅkhyayogasamaye cārvākaśiṣyas sakhā
[98.22]     mithyācārasamāhvayas svayam asau viplāviko vaidikaḥ //"



[98.23-99.4]     ity uktarītyā eteṣāṃ śaivapāśupatavaiṣṇavādyākariṇa vidyamānatvāt āpastambādisūtrāṇy api nārāyaṇaikaparāṇi na bhavanti. bhagavato nārāyaṇasya samārādhanavidhipratipādanābhāvāc ca. nārāyaṇaikaparañ ced āpastambādisūtraṃ tarhi tatsūtroktadharmānuṣṭhātāraḥ sarve 'pi nārāyaṇaikaparā eva syuḥ. na ca tathā dṛśyate. pāñcarātrādyuktamārgeṇa vaiṣṇavasaṃpādane "svasūtre vidyamāne tu" - "svasūtrasya parityāgāt" - "yas svadharmaṃ parityajya" "vidharmaḥ paradharmaś ca" - śreyā svadharmo viguṇaḥ" - ityādi vacanapratipāditasvasūtraparityāgaparadharmasvīkāraśākhāraṇḍatvādidoṣāḥ prasajyeran.
[99.5-6]     "svaśāstranirṇaye satye satyāḥ syur lokanirṇayā" iti svasūtrasya prāmāṇyabuddhiś ca teṣām avarjanīyā.

     [vaikhānasānāṃ avicchedena nārāyaṇaparatvam]

[99.7-9]     vaikhānasānāṃ sūtrakārād ārabhya avicchinnatvena śrīmannārāyaṇaikaparatvenārādhanādikaṃ pratyakṣasiddham. tathā ca sūtram, "gṛhe devāyatane vā bhaktyā bhagavantaṃ nārāyaṇam arcayet tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ gacchatīti vijñāyate" iti.
[99.10-12]     itareṣv āpastambādiṣu pitṛ pitāmaha mātula mātāmaha putra pautra bhrātṛ sambandhiṣu kecic chaivāḥ kecid pāśupatāḥ kecic chāktāḥ nānādevatāparāś cetyevamākāreṇa dṛśyate.
[99.13]     "janmāntarasahasreṣu tapojñānasamādhibhiḥ /
[99.14]     narāṇāṃ kṣīṇapāpānāṃ kṛṣṇe bhaktiḥ prajāyate //"
[99.15-16]     iti keṣāñcit svakṛtapūrvapuṇyaviśeṣān nārāyaṇaparatvasambhave 'pi svasūtrakāram ārabhya svaparyantam avicchinnatvena tad astīti vaktuṃ na śakyate. ataḥ -
[99.17]     "nānākāmahatajñānā nānādaivatayājinaḥ /
[99.18]     narā bhagavat aikantye na sthāsyanti kalau yuge // [VāyuP]
[99.19]     āgamād anumānāc ca pratyakṣād upapattitaḥ /
[99.20]     parīkṣya nipuṇaṃ buddhyā śraddhātavyaṃ vipaścitā //" [VāyuP]
[99.21-22]     iti vāyupurāṇādivacanād āgamādibhir nipuṇaṃ parīkṣya nirṇīta evārthaḥ vipaścidbhiḥ anuṣṭheyaḥ.

     [nārāyaṇasya pāramyam]

[99.23-100.10] nanu - kiṃ arthaṃ nārāyaṇaikaparatvena sūtraṃ praṇītam iti cet - ucyate. nārāyaṇa akhilajagadekakāraṇatvāt paraṃbrahmaparamātmādiśabdavācyatvāt apavargādiphalapradatvāt samābhyadhikarahitatvāc ca nārāyaṇaikaparatvena praṇītam. atra - "nārāyaṇād ru jāyate. nārāyaṇād indro jāyate. nārāyaṇād dvādaśādityāḥ rudrā vasavas sarvāṇi ca bhūtāni. nārāyaṇād eva samudpadyante. nārāyaṇāt pralīyante" ityādyāḥ "nārāyaṇaparaṃ brahme"ty ārabhya "antarbahiś ca tatsarvaṃ vyāpya nārāyaṇaḥ sthitaḥ" ity ādyāḥ, "tam eva vidvān amṛta iha bhavati. nānyaḥ panthā ayanāya vidyate" "utāmṛtatvasyeśānaḥ" ityādyāḥ, "na tasya kāryaṃ karaṇañ ca vidyate" "na tatsamaścābhyadhikaś ca dṛśyate" "parāsya śaktir vividhaiva śrūyate svābhāvikī jñānabalakriyā ca" ityādyāḥ, "eṣa sarvabhūtāntarātmā divyo deva eko nārāyaṇaḥ" ityādyāḥ, "eko ha vai nārāyaṇa āsīt" ityādyāḥ, "yato vā imāni bhūtāni jāyante. yena jātāni jīvanti. yatprayanty abhisaṃviśanti. tadvijijñāsasva. tad brahme"ti "patiṃ viśvasyātmeśvaram" ityādyāś ca śrutayaḥ pramāṇam.






     [śvetāśvatarādeḥ rudrapāramyaparatvābhāvaḥ]

[100.11-23]     nanu - śvetāśvatare - "eko hi rudro na dvitīyāya tasthe - ya imān lokān īśata īśanībhiḥ - viśvādhiko rudro maharṣiḥ - hiraṇyagarbhaṃ janayāmāsa pūrvaṃ sa no buddhyā śubhayā saṃyunaktu - "umāsahāyaṃ paramaṃ maheśvaraṃ triyambakaṃ nīlakaṇṭhaṃ praśāntam. jñātvā munir gacchati bhūtayoniṃ samastasākṣiṃ tamasaḥ parastāt" ityādibhiḥ rudrasyāpi jagatkāraṇatvādi pratipādyata iti cet - ucyate. āpātato rudraparatvenāvagamyamāne 'pi vicāryamāṇe nārāyaṇaparatvam eva. eka eva rudra ity anupapannam. "sahasrāṇi sahasraśo ye rudrā" ityādi śrutibhiḥ "ekādaśarudrā" ityādibhiś ca anekarudrāṇāṃ vidyamānatvāvagamāt krūrasya rudraśabdavācyasya "bṛhattvāt bṛṃhaṇatvāc ca tadbrahmeti prakīrtitam" iti brahmaśabdavācyatvāsambhavāt, "teṣām asurāṇāṃ tisraḥ pura āsann" ity ārabhya, "idam asiṣyatīti rudram abruvan rudro vai krūras so 'syatviti. so 'bravīd varaṃ vṛṇai aham eva paśūnām adhipatirasāv iti tasmād rudraḥ paśūnām adhipatir iti" "rudro vā akāmayata paśumān syām iti - "mātā rudrāṇāṃ duhitā vasūnām" iti. paśupatitvayācakatvāt. "naiva devo na martyaḥ. na rājā varuṇo vibhuḥ. nāgnirnendro na pavamānaḥ.






     [brahmarudrādīnāṃ nārāyaṇasāmyābhāvaḥ]

[100.24-101.7] mātṛkkaś ca na vidyate - ity ārabhya "etad rudrasya dhanuḥ. rudrasyatvena dhanurārtniḥ. śira utpipeṣa. sa pravargyo 'bhavat. tasmād yas sapravargyeṇa yajñena yajate. rudrasya sa śiraḥ pratidhāti. nainaṃ rudra āruko bhavati" ity uktatvāc ca rudrasya brahmaśabdavācyatvaṃ na sambhavati. rudra hara paśupati nīlagrīva śitikaṇṭha bhava śarva kapardītyādīnām ekatvena śruyamāṇānām ekatvaṃ na sambhavati. īśvara maheśvara paramamaheśvara iti paramamaheśvaraśabdaśravaṇāt. "śiva eko dhyeyaḥ śivaśśaṅkaraḥ sarvam anyatparityajye" tyādinā śivaśabdavācyād adhikatvena śivataraśivatamaśabdavācyasya vidyamānatvāt. śambhuśabdasya viśvaśambhutvaśravaṇāt īśānasya jagadīśānatvaśravaṇāt mahādevasya "tamīśvarāṇāṃ paramaṃ maheśvaraṃ taṃ devatānāṃ paramañ ca daivatam" iti śravaṇāc ca rudrādīnāṃ paraṃbrahmaśabdavācyatvaṃ na sambhavati.
[101.8-12]     nanu - śvetāśvatare - umāsahayaviśeṣita paramamaheśvaraśabdavācyasya rudratvasambhavāt paraṃbrahmaśabdavācyatvaṃ tasya sambhavatīti cet - na. paramamaheśvaraśabdasya umāsahāyam ity atra rudrādiṣv anupapannatvāt. ukārastvavadhāraṇārthaḥ. u - mā sahāyaṃ lakṣmīsahāyaṃ paramaṃ maheśvaram eva trilocanatvādiviśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭhaṃ lakṣmīnarasiṃhaṃ dhyātvetyarthaḥ. yadvā. devamanuṣyādyapekṣayā paramamaheśvaratvāt,
[101.13]     "sṛṣṭisthityantakaraṇīṃ brahmaviṣṇuśivātmikām /
[101.14]     sa saṃjñāṃ yāti bhagavān eka eva janārdanaḥ //"
[101.15-18]     iti bhagavaccharīrabhūtatvāc ca rudrasya paramamaheśvaratvam. evaṃ bhūtaṃ rudraṃ dhyātvā munir mananaśīlassan bhūtayoniṃ sarvakāraṇakāraṇaṃ samstarakṣakaṃ tamasaḥ parastāt gacchati. "ādityavarṇaṃ tamasaḥ parastād" ityādibhiḥ tamasaḥ pāravartinaṃ prakṛteḥ paraṃ paramātmānaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ gacchati - prāpnoti ity arthaḥ.
[101.19]     kiñca - atra: sano devaḥ śubhayā smṛtyā saṃyunaktu. ity anena
[101.20]     "ārogya bhāskarād icchet śriyam icched dhūtāśanāt /
[101.21]     śaṅkarāt jñānam anvicchet mokṣam icchej janārdanāt //"
[101.22-23]     iti jñānapradatvāt śaṅkaropāsanam ucyate. ato bhagavatā nārāyaṇena sāmyaṃ brahmarudrādīnāṃ nopapadyate.
[101.24]     bhārate: "ye tu sāmānyabhāvena manyante puruṣottamam /
[101.25]     te vai pāṣaṇḍano jñeyās sarvakarmabahiṣkṛtāḥ // [MB.h ]

     [rudrādisāmyena nārāyaṇāvamantṝṇām aniṣṭam]

[102.1]     yas tu nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ sāmānyenābhimanyate /
[102.2]     sa yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ yāvac candrādivākaram // [MB.h ]
[102.3]     yo mahādviṣṇum anyena hīnadevena durmati /
[102.4]     sādhāraṇaṃ sakṛd brūte so 'ntyajo nāntyajoṃ 'tyajaḥ //" [MBh ]
[102.5]     vārāhe: "anyadevasamaṃ ye tu manyante māṃ narādhamāḥ /
[102.6]     caṇḍālatāṃ vrajanty āśu janmani nava pañca ca //" iti [VarāhaP]
[102.7]     śrībhāgavate: "yas tu nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ samatvenāvamanyate /
[102.8]     sakṛttenāvamānena narakānnātivartate // [BhāgavataP ]
[102.9]     asmād anyaṃ paratvena cintayāno hy acetanaḥ /
[102.10]     sa pāṣaṇḍīti vijñeyas sarvakarmabahiṣkṛtaḥ //" iti [BhāgavataP ]
[102.11]     kaurme: "ye 'nyaṃ devaṃ paratvena vadanty ajñānamohitāḥ /
[102.12]     nārāyaṇāj jagannāthāt te vai pāṣaṇḍinaḥ smṛtāḥ // [KūrmaP ]
[102.13]     yas tu nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ brahmarudrādidaivataiḥ /
[102.14]     samatvenaiva vīkṣeta sa pāṣaṇḍī bhaved dvijaḥ //" iti [KūrmaP ]
[102.15]     bhāradvāja: "aśuddhā brahmarudrādyā jīvā viṣṇor vibhūtayaḥ /
[102.16]     tān vai kudṛṣṭayas samyak paratvenāpy upāsate //" iti
[102.17]     vārāhe: agastyaṃ prati rudraḥ:
[102.18]     "yo yajñair ijyate devo yasmāt sarvam idaṃ jagat /
[102.19]     utpannaṃ sarvadā yasmin līyate sacarācaram // [VarāhaP]
[102.20]     nārāyaṇaḥ paro devaḥ sattvarūpī janārdanaḥ /
[102.21]     tridhātmānaṃ sa bhagavān sasarja parameśvaraḥ // [VarāhaP]
[102.22]     śuddhasattvas svayaṃ jajñe rajassattvādikaṃ vibhuḥ /
[102.23]     sasarja nābhikamale brahmāṇaṃ kamalāsanam // [VarāhaP]
[102.24]     rajasā tamasā yuktaṃ so 'pi māṃ sasṛje prabhur //" iti [VarāhaP]





[103.1]     nanu: "sarvapāpaharañ ceha paścāt saṃsāranāśanam /
[103.2]     suvarṇaraupyatāmrādyaiḥ lohenāpi tathaiva ca // [VarāhaP]
[103.3]     tathā rayāṅgam aṣṭāṅgaṃ sunābhañ ca suvṛttakam /
[103.4]     jvālācatuṣkasaṃyuktaṃ kṛtvā caiva vidhānataḥ // [VarāhaP]
[103.5]     agnau pratāpya vidhivat dhārayed bhaktisaṃyutaḥ //" iti [VarāhaP]
[103.6]     "yajño dānaṃ tapo homo bhojanaṃ pitṛtarpaṇam /
[103.7]     cakralāñchanahīnasya viprasya viphalaṃ bhavet // [VarāhaP.]
[103.8]     śrāddhe dāne vrate yajñe vivāhe copanāyane /
[103.9]     cakrāṅkitaṃ vipram eva pūjayed aparaṃ na tu //" [VarāhaP]
[103.10-11]     ityādivacanaiḥ cakrādinānaṅkitasya vaiṣṇavatvābhāvāt vaikhānasānāṃ kathaṃ vā vaiṣṇavatvam iti cet - ucyate.

     [cakrādyanaṅkitānām api vaikhānsānāṃ vaiṣṇavatvam]

[103.12-13]     "yasya me śriyam amitāṃ dātuṃ garbha eva kare cakraṃ dhārayāmi sa cakravartī bhavati" iti śruteḥ
[103.14]     "vaikhānasānāṃ sarveṣāṃ garbhavaiṣṇavajanmanām /
[103.15]     nārāyaṇaḥ svayaṃ garbhe mudrāṃ dhārayate nijām //" iti
[103.16]     "sudarśanam abhīty uktvā dakṣiṇe tu sudarśanam /
[103.17]     ravipām iti vāme tu śaṅkhañ ca bibhṛyāt kare //"

     [vaikhānasānāṃ garbhato vaiṣṇavatvam]

[103.18]     iti bhṛguṇoktatvāc ca śrīviṣṇubalikarmaṇā vaikhānasānāṃ garbhavaiṣṇavatvādikaṃ pratipannam.
[103.19]     tathā: "indriyebhyaḥ parā hy arthā hy arthebhyaś ca paraṃ manaḥ /
[103.20]     manasas tu parā buddhir buddher ātmā mahān paraḥ //
[103.21]     mahataḥ param avyaktam avyaktāt puruṣaḥ paraḥ /
[103.22]     puruṣān na paraṃ kiñcit sā kāṣṭhā sā parā gatiḥ //"

     [garbhagatasya prapadanopapattiḥ]

[103.23]     iti śruteḥ paramaikāntitvaṃ paramapuruṣavaśīkaraṇadvārā garbhagatasya prapattir api sambhavati.
[103.24]     garbhagatasya prapattir api garbhopaniṣadi śrūyate. "jñānād dhyanād akṣaram oṅkāraḥ cintayati."





[104.1-2]     ity uktvā "atha navame māsi sarvalakṣaṇasampūrṇo bhavati. pūrvajātiṃ smarati. kṛtākṛtañ ca karma bhavati. śubhāśubhañ ca karma vindati."
[104.3]     "nānāyonisahasrāṇi dṛṣṭā caiva tato mayā /
[104.4]     āhārā vividhā bhuktāḥ pītāś ca vividhāḥ stanāḥ // [Garbha.U 4.1]
[104.5]     jātasyaiva mṛtasyaiva janma caiva punaḥ punaḥ /
[104.6]     aho duḥkho dadhau magno na paśyāmi pratikriyām //" ityuktvā [GarbhaU 4.2]
[104.7]     "yadi yonyāḥ pramucye 'haṃ taṃ prapadye nārāyaṇām /
[104.8]     aśubhakṣayakartāraṃ phalamuktipradāyakam //" iti [GarbhaU 4.6]
[104.9-14]     puruṣasūktabhāṣye - mudgalopaniṣadi - "vāmadevo 'py āṅgirasas san pūrvapūjāṃ samārātriṃ patnyanasūyāgarbha eva śayāno brahmaiva vedayāñ cakre sa garbhaṃ puro bhitvā brahmalokam upacakrāma tam utkrāmāntam āha madhye 'dhvānam indraḥ upaniṣada uvāca, bhagavan garbhapañjare evābhiniveśamāna anabhijñātopāyo 'smāt kiñcid dhādityā sa garbhas sarvo manyamāno 'dhvanaḥ pāram upagacchasī"tyādi. tathā ca garbhagatasya prapadanavicāraśravaṇādyupapadyata eva.

     [vaidikatāntrikabhedena prapatter dvaividyam]

[104.15-16]     vaidikatāntrikabhedena prapattir dvividhā - praṇavapūrvakatvena puruṣādyāvāhanādikaṃ vaidikam.

     [vaidikaprapatter lakṣaṇam]

[104.17]     śrutyantare: "akāreṇocyate viṣṇus sarvalokeśvaro hariḥ /
[104.18]     uddhṛtā viṣṇunā lakṣmīr ukāreṇa tathocyate /
[104.19]     makāras tu tayor dāsa iti praṇavalakṣaṇam //" iti
[104.20]     kiñca. praṇavoccāraṇamātreṇa śaṅkhacakrādidhāraṇam api sambhavatīti śruyate.
[104.21-24]     kaivalyopaniṣadi - "dhṛtordhvapuṇḍraḥ kṛtacakradhārī viṣṇuṃ paraṃ dhyāyati yo mahātmā. svareṇa mantreṇa sadā hṛdisthaṃ parāt paraṃ yanmahato mahāntam." iti. sarvakāraṇabhūtāya sarvarakṣakāya sarvaśeṣiṇe śriyaḥ pataye eva svābhāvikaśeṣabhūta iti sarvadānusandhānam eva vaidikī prapattiḥ.





[105.1]     "svojjīvanecchā yadi te svasattāyāṃ spṛhā yadi /
[105.2]     ātmadāsyaṃ hareḥ svāmyaṃ svabhāvañ ca sadā smara //"
[105.3]     ity eva sūtre pratipaditam.
[105.4]     pāñcarātre tu
[105.5]     "tyaktvā trayīṃ tantram eva prapadya śaraṇaṃ sthitāḥ //" iti [PādmaS caryāpāda 21.56cd]
[105.6]     "ananyasādhye svābhīṣṭhe mahāviśvāsapūrvakam /
[105.7]     tadekopāyatā yācñā prapattiḥ śaraṇāgatiḥ //"
[105.8-10]     iti ca upadiśyate. tasyāḥ prapatteḥ sakṛtkaraṇāt samantrakatvābhāvāt taccheṣagatyanusmaraṇābhāvāc ca tāṃ tāntrikaprapattiṃ vihāya "yad eva vidyayā karoti tad eva vīryavattaraṃ bhavatī"ti śrutyā vaidikaprapattim evoktavān sūtrakāraḥ.

     [taptacakrādyaṅkaṃ na dvijanmanām]

[105.11]     skānde: "viṣṇvāgamāditantreṣu dīkṣitānāṃ vidhīyate /
[105.12]     śaṅkhacakragadāpūrvair aṅkanaṃ nānyadehinām // [SkandaP ]
[105.13]     śivāgamādidīkṣāṇāṃ dhāryaṃ tiryak tripuṇḍrakam //" iti [SkandaP ]
[105.14]     viṣṇu: "śaṅkhacakrādyaṅkanañ ca gītanṛttādikaṃ tathā /
[105.15]     ekajāter ayaṃ dharmaḥ na jātu syād dvijanmanām //" iti [ViṣṇuP ]
[105.16]     śrībhāgavate daśamaskandhe:
[105.17]     "trivakrāyām upaślokaḥ putraḥ kṛṣṇam anuvrataḥ /
[105.18]     śiṣyas sākṣān nāradasya dadau cittam akhaṇḍitam //
[105.19]     tenoktaṃ sāttvataṃ tantraṃ yat jñātvā mokṣabhāg bhavet /
[105.20]     yatra strīśūdradāsānāṃ saṃskāro vaiṣṇavaḥ smṛtaḥ //" iti [BhāgavataP ]

     [tāntrikaprapatter lakṣaṇādi]

[105.21]     padmapurāṇe: "vedajñe brāhmaṇe nityaṃ sarvās tiṣṭhanti devatāḥ /
[105.22]     iti tittiriśākhāyāṃ śrūyate nṛpasattama // [PadmaP ]
[105.23]     dakṣiṇe 'ṃse brāhmaṇasya śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ /
[105.24]     haris tiṣṭhati vāme tu devakīsūnur ādarāt // [PadmaP ]





[106.1]     tato brāhmaṇadeho 'yaṃ devatāgāra ucyate /
[106.2]     taddāhe devatās sarve palāyante diśo daśa // [PadmaP ]

     [taptacakraṅkaṇādividhīnām adhikārī]

[106.3]     agāradāhī sa bhavet taddāhī brāhmaṇādhamaḥ /
[106.4]     śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ mṛdā yas tu kuryāt taptāyasena vā // [PadmaP ]
[106.5]     sa śūdravatbahiṣkāryaḥ sarvasmād dvijakarmaṇaḥ /
[106.6]     yathā śmaśānajaṃ kāṣṭham anarhaṃ sarvakarmasu // [PadmaP ]
[106.7]     tathā cakrāṅkito vipras sarvakarmasu garhitaḥ //" iti. [PadmaP ]
[106.8]     tatraiva: "mohād vā lobhato vāpi vipraś cakrāṅkito yadi /
[106.9]     anarhas sa hi vijñeyaḥ śrautasmārteṣu karmasu // [Padma.P ]
[106.10]     kriyāsv anarhatām eti yathā kāṣṭhaṃ śmaśānagam /
[106.11]     tathā cakrādinā dagdhāḥ sarvakarmasv anarhatām // [PadmaP ]
[106.12]     dagdhārdhakāyo yatrāsti grāme janapade 'pi vā /
[106.13]     śmaśānaṃ tad dhi vijñeyaṃ vāsānarhaṃ dvijanmanām //" [PadmaP ]
[106.14-16]     ityādinā dūṣaṇam uktam. etāni taptacakrāṅkanavidhāyakāni vacanāni "viṣṇvāgamāditantreṣu dīkṣitānām" ity uktatvāt ekajātiviṣayatvenoktatvāt "nānyadehinām" ityuktatvāc ca tāntrikāgamoktaprakāreṇa dīkṣitaviṣayāṇīty avagamyate.
[106.17-19]     yadvā vidhiniṣedhavacanānāṃ vaiyarthyaparihārāya "vapāśrapaṇībhyām anvārabhate tannaivānvārabdhaṃ naivānanvārabdhaṃ" "avaghreyam eva tat naiva prāśitaṃ naivāprāśitam" ityādi śrutinyāyena samantrakatvena bhāvanārūpeṇa śrīvaikhānasaśāstre pratipāditam.. yathā:
[106.20]     "sudarśanam abhīty uktvā dakṣiṇe tu sudarśanam /
[106.21]     ravipām iti vāme ca śaṅkhañ ca bibhṛyāt kare //" iti
[106.22]     mahopaniṣadi - brahmasūkte:
[106.23]     "dakṣiṇe tu bhuje vipro bibhṛyād vai sudarśanam /
[106.24]     savye tu śaṅkhaṃ bibhṛyād iti vedavido viduḥ //" iti.





     [pāñcarātroktataptacakradhāraṇasya sarvādhikārikatvābhāvaḥ]

     [pāñcarātrādīnāṃ mohanaśāstratvam]

[107.1]     mohaśāstratvāt śaptaviṣayatvāc ca pañcarātre tāpavidhānaṃ uktam iti kecit vadanti.
[107.2]     padmapurāṇe gautama: "yan mayi brāhmaṇābhāsāḥ ṛjau kaitavam īdṛśam /
[107.3]     anuṣṭhitaṃ tato vedamārgabhraṣṭhāś ca pāpinaḥ // [Padma.P ]
[107.4]     kālamukhe pāñcarātre kālapāle śāmbhave 'pi ca /
[107.5]     śākte ca dīkṣitā yūyaṃ bhavata brāhmaṇādhamāḥ //" iti [PadmaP ]
[107.6]     brahmā: "bauddhe bhāgavate tantre tṛtīye pāñcarātrake /
[107.7]     dīkṣitāś ca dvijā nityaṃ bhaveyur nirbhayā hare // [PadmaP ]
[107.8]     śrautasmārtasamācāre sadyomuktikare śubhe /
[107.9]     tvadbhaktivimukhā nityaṃ bhaveyuḥ parimohitāḥ // [Padma.P ]
[107.10]     śaṅkhvaikhanacakragadāpūrvavajrapāśāṅkuśādibhiḥ /
[107.11]     aṅkitāḥ śraddhayā yūyaṃ bhavata brāhmaṇādhamāḥ //" iti [PadmaP ]
[107.12]     skānde - "sūtasaṃhitāyām sarasvatīṃ prati rudraḥ:
[107.13]     "śrutir balīyasīty uktā pramāṇānāṃ sulocane" ity ārabhya [SkandaP ]
[107.14]     "pāñcarātrādimārgāṇāṃ vedamūlatvamāstike /
[107.15]     na hi svatantratas tena bhrāntimūlāni rūpiṇi // [SkandaP ]
[107.16]     tathāpi yo 'ṃśo mārgeṇa vaidikenāviruddhyate /
[107.17]     so 'ṃśaḥ pramāṇam ity uktaṃ keṣāñcid adhikāriṇām // [SkandaP ]
[107.18]     atyantas khalitānān tu prāṇiṇāṃ vedamārgataḥ /
[107.19]     pāñcarātrādayo mārgāḥ kālenaivopakārakāḥ /
[107.20]     tāntrikāṇāṃ mahādevi na labhyo 'vyavadhānataḥ //" iti pratipāditam. [SkandaP ]
[107.21]     kaurme: "purā dāruvane puṇye munayo gṛhamedhinaḥ //" [KūrmaP 16.97ab]
[107.22]     ity ārabhya māyayā gokalpanādi śāpaprāptiparyantam uktvā:
[107.23]     "kā no vṛttir mahādeva śāpānnaḥ trātum arhasi / [KūrmaP 16.112cd]
[107.24]     tathā pārśvasthitaṃ viṣṇuṃ samprekṣya vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ /






     [pāñcarātrasya vedabhraṣṭānuddiśya pravṛttatvam]

[108.1]     kim eteṣāṃ bhavet kāryaṃ prāha puṇyaiṣiṇām iti // [Kūrma.P 16.113]
[108.2]     tatas sa bhagavān viṣṇuḥ śaraṇyo bhaktavatsalaḥ /
[108.3]     gopatiṃ prāha viprendrān ālokya praṇatān hariḥ // [KūrmaP 16.114]
[108.4]     na vedabāhye śāstre ca puṇyaleśo 'pi śaṅkara /
[108.5]     saṅgacchate yato dharmo vedād eva hi nirbabhau // [KūrmaP 16.115]
[108.6]     tathāpi bhaktavātsalyāt rakṣaṇīyā maheśvara /
[108.7]     āvābhyāṃ sarva evaite viprā vai nātrasaṃśayaḥ // [KūrmaP 16.116]
[108.8]     tasmād vai vedabāhyānāṃ rakṣaṇārthañ ca pāpinām /
[108.9]     vimohanāya śāstrāṇi kariṣyāmi vṛṣadhvaja // [KūrmaP 16.117]
[108.10]     evaṃ sañcodito rudro mādhavenāsurāriṇā /
[108.11]     cakāra mohaśāstrāṇi keśavo 'pi śiveritaḥ // [KūrmaP 16.118]
[108.12]     kāpālaṃ yāmalaṃ vāmaṃ bhairavaṃ pūrvapaścimam /
[108.13]     pāñcarātraṃ pāśupataṃ tathānyāni sahasraśaḥ // [KūrmaP 16.119]
[108.14]     kṛtvā cārcya ca tad devān kurvāṇās tatra coditam /
[108.15]     patanti narake ghore bahūn kalpān punaḥ punaḥ //" ityādi coktam [KūrmaP 16.120]
[108.16]     skānde śaṅkarasaṃhitāyām
[108.17]     "nekṣeta pūjāvelāyāṃ naraṃ vatsa bahiṣkṛtam /
[108.18]     dadhīcinā gautamena ye śaptā brāhmaṇādhamāḥ // [SkandaP ]
[108.19]     kalāv avatariṣyanti ninditās te bahiṣkṛtāḥ //" iti [SkandaP ]
[108.20]     sāmbapurāṇe: "śrutibhraṣṭaḥ smṛtiprokta prāyaścitte bhayaṃ gataḥ /
[108.21]     krameṇa śrutisiddhyarthaṃ manuṣyas tantram āśrayet // [SāmbaP]
[108.22]     dharmaśāstre purāṇe ca proktaṃ hi maraṇāntikam /
[108.23]     prāyaścittaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ pāpiṣṭhānāṃ sudāruṇam // [SāmbaP]







     [pāñcarātramārgānusāriṇāṃ śrautasmārtabāhyatvam]

[109.1]     bhayaṃ durbalacittānāṃ maraṇe jāyate bhṛśam /
[109.2]     teṣām evābhirakṣārthaṃ tad ahaṃ tantram uktavān // [SāmbaP]
[109.3]     pāñcarātraṃ bhāgavataṃ tantraṃ sāttvatanāmakam /
[109.4]     vedabhraṣṭān samuddiśya kamalāpatir abravīt //" iti [SāmbaP]
[109.5]     anyatra: "athāṃśoḥ sāttvato nāma viṣṇubhaktaḥ pratāpavān /
[109.6]     mahātmā dānanirato dhanurvedavidāṃ varaḥ //
[109.7]     sa nāradasya vacanād vāsudevārcane rataḥ /
[109.8]     śāstraṃ pravartayāmāsa kuṇḍagolādibhiḥ śritam //
[109.9]     tasya nāmnā tu vikhyātaṃ sāttvataṃ nāma śobhanam /
[109.10]     pravartate mahacchāstraṃ kuṇḍādīnāṃ hitāvaham //" iti
[109.11]     vāsiṣṭhe: "bṛddhaśāvaka nirgandhāḥ pāñcarātravido janāḥ /
[109.12]     kāpālikāḥ pāśupatāḥ pāṣaṇḍā ye ca tadvidhāḥ // [VāsiṣṭhaDhŚ ]
[109.13]     yasyāśnanti havīṃśy ete durātmānas tu tāmasāḥ /
[109.14]     na tasya tad bhavec chāstraṃ pretyeha ca na tatphalam //" iti. [VāsiṣṭhaDhŚ ]
[109.15]     laiṅge - navamādhyāye yugadharme
[109.16]     "aṅkitāś ca bhaviṣyanti devatāyudhalāñchanaiḥ /
[109.17]     nārāyaṇam aśṛṇvanti yugānte samupasthite // [LiṅgaP]
[109.18]     anyāni yāni karmāṇi śrautāni munisattama /
[109.19]     smārtāni nācariṣyanti kalau brahman narās sadā // [LiṅgaP]
[109.20]     āmnāyaṃ dharmaśāstrañ ca purāṇaṃ bhārataṃ mune /
[109.21]     alpamātram iti brahman vadiṣyanti kalau yuge // [LiṅgaP]
[109.22]     na kuryuḥ śrautakarmāṇi śraddhayā munisattama /
[109.23]     svadharme rucitā nāsti brāhmaṇānāṃ kalau yuge // [LiṅgaP]
[109.24]     pāñcarātraṃ praśaṃsanti kecid bhāgavataṃ mune /
[109.25]     kecit kāpālam icchanti kecit pāśupataṃ mune // [LiṅgaP]






     [cakrāṅkanasya bhāvanārūpeṇaiva kartavyatā]

[110.1]     kecid bauddhaṃ praśaṃsanti kecid daigambaraṃ tathā /
[110.2]     kecil lokāyataṃ brahman kecit saumaṃ mahāmune // [LiṅgaP]
[110.3]     lākulaṃ kecid icchanti tathā kecit tu bhairavam /
[110.4]     kecid vāmaṃ praśaṃsanti kecic chāktaṃ tathaiva ca // [LiṅgaP]
[110.5]     śāmbhavaṃ kecid icchanti yāmalaṃ bhuvi kecana /
[110.6]     anyāni yāni śāstrāṇi viruddhāni mahāmune // [LiṅgaP]
[110.7]     tīrthavikrayiṇaḥ kecid devavikrayiṇaḥ pare /
[110.8]     kṣīravikrayiṇaḥ kecid ājyavikrayiṇaḥ pare // [LiṅgaP]
[110.9]     māṃsavikrayiṇaḥ kecit surāvikrayiṇaḥ pare /
[110.10]     putravikrayiṇaḥ kecid dāravikrayiṇaḥ pare // [LiṅgaP]
[110.11]     bhartṛvikrayiṇaḥ kecid bhaviṣyanti kalau narāḥ //" iti [LiṅgaP]
[110.12]     ataḥ pāñcarātoktaṃ taptacakradhāraṇaṃ sarvasādhāraṇaṃ na bhavantīti siddham.
[110.13-16]     atha yad uktaṃ sarvasādhāraṇaṃ na bhavatīti tan nopapadyate - ātharvaṇe "cakraṃ bibharti vapuṣābhitaptaṃ balaṃ devānāmamitasya viṣṇoḥ. sa eti nākaṃ duritā vidhūya prayānti yadyatayo vītarāgāḥ, "caraṇaṃ pavitraṃ vitataṃ purāṇaṃ" ityādi śrutibhiḥ sarvasādhāraṇatvena śrūyamāṇatvāt iti cet - na.
[110.17-20]     taptacakradhāraṇe prāyaścittavidhānāt. ataḥ yathoktamārgeṇa bhāvanārūpeṇaiva cakrāṅkanaṃ na tu taptarūpeṇa. sarvasādhāraṇaśrutis tu vaikhānasetaraviṣayā. "yasya me śriyam" ityādi śrutyavirodhena arthavyavasthāyāḥ kāryatvāt. ataḥ taptacakrāṅkanaṃ sarvasādhāraṇaṃ na bhavati.
[110.21]     kiñ ca: "yatra śāstragatir bhinnā sarvakarmasu bhārata /
[110.22]     udite 'nudite caiva homabhede yathā bhavet /
[110.23]     sa garīyān mahābāho sarvaśāstroditād api //"
[110.24]     iti sumantusmaraṇāc ca vyavasthitavikalpotra vaktavyaḥ.







     [viṣṇor eva saṃhārakartṛtvam]

[111.1-2]     kiñca brahmarudrādīnām api saṃhārakartā harir eveti śrūyate. yajuṣi - hariṃ harantam anuyanti devāḥ viśvasyeśānaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ matīnām" iti.ab hier Telugu überprüfen

     [viṣṇukartṛkarudropāsanasya kāraṇam]

[111.3]     brahmapurāṇe: "brahmāṇam indraṃ rudrañ ca yamaṃ varuṇam eva ca /
[111.4]     nigṛhyāharate yasmāt tasmād dharir ihocyate // [Brahma.P ]
[111.5]     brahmā śambhus tathaivārkaś candramāś ca śatakratuḥ /
[111.6]     evam ādyās tathaivānye yuktā vaiṣṇavatejasā // [Brahma.P ]
[111.7]     jagatkāryāvasāne tu viyujyante ca tejasā /
[111.8]     tejasaś caiva te sarve pañcatvam upayānti ca//" iti [BrahmaP ]
[111.9-14]     nanu - "hariṃ harantaṃ" iti pūrvopāttayajuṣi īśānaśabdaśravaṇāt rudra eva saṃhārakarteti śrūyate iti cet - tad asat. tatra "viśvasyeśāna," iti jaganniyāmakatvam ucyate. bis hier telugu noch überprüfentathā ca "patiṃ viśrasyātmeśvara," itivat nārāyaṇa eva atra pratipādyaḥ. "asyeśānā jagato viṣṇupatnī" sa hariḥ suvittamaḥ, "perur indrāya pinvata" "virāḍ asi", "bṛhatī śravasīndrapatnī dharmapatnī", "sa brahmā sa śivas sendraḥ", ityādi śrutayotra vibhāvanīyāḥ.
[111.15]     nanu kaurme aṣṭamādhyāye - rāmāyaṇasaṃkṣepe:
[111.16]     "sa kṛtvā vānaraśataiḥ laṅkādvāraṃ mahodadhau // [KūrmaP 21.44cd]
[111.17]     setuṃ paramadharmātmā rāvaṇaṃ hatavān prabhuḥ //" [KūrmaP 21.45ab]
[111.18]     iti rāvaṇavadhādikaṃ pratipādya:
[111.19]     "setumadhye mahādevam īśānaṃ kṛttivāsasam // [KūrmaP 21.46cd]
[111.20]     sthāpayāmāsa liṅgasthaṃ pūjayāmāsa rāghavaḥ /
[111.21]     tasya devo mahādevaḥ pārvatyā saha śaṅkaraḥ // [KūrmaP 21.47]
[111.22]     pratyakṣam eva bhagavān dattavān varam uttamam /" [KūrmaP 21.48ab]







     [rudrasya varadātṛtvaṃ viṣṇuprasādalabdham]

[112.1-2]     iti bhagavate rudropāsanam ucyate iti cet - satyam. rudrasya tad api bhagavadvaraprasādalabdham. evaṃ hi vārāhe prāgitihāse rudragītāsu ucyate, yathā -
[112.3]     agastyaṃ prati rudraḥ:
[112.4]     "brahmaṇāhaṃ purā sṛṣṭaḥ proktaḥ sṛja iti prajāḥ /
[112.5]     avijñātāsamartho 'haṃ nimagnassalile dvija //" ity ārabhya [VarāhaP]
[112.6-7]     jalamadhye kālamedhasaṅkāśaḥ atiśobhanaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ kaścit puruṣo rudreṇa dṛṣṭaḥ kastvam iti rudreṇa pṛṣṭasya tasya prativacanam:
[112.8]     "ahaṃ nārāyaṇo devo jalaśāyī sanātanaḥ /
[112.9]     divyaṃ cakṣur bhavatu te tena māṃ paśya yatnataḥ //" iti pratipādya [VarāhaP]
[112.10]     "evam uktas tadā tena yāvat paśyāmm ahaṃ tanum /
[112.11]     tāvad aṅguṣṭhamātran tu jvaladbhāskaratejasam // [VarāhaP]
[112.12]     tam evāhaṃ prapaśyāmi tasya nābhau tu paṅkajam /
[112.13]     brahmāṇaṃ tatra paśyāmi hy ātmānañ ca tadaṅkataḥ // [VarāhaP]
[112.14]     evaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahātmānaṃ tato harṣam upāgataḥ /
[112.15]     taṃ stotuṃ dvijaśārdūla matir me samajāyata //" [VarāhaP]
[112.16-17]     ity upakramya mahatstotram uktvā ante rudreṇa bhagavantaṃ pratyabhīṣṭanivedanaṃ pratipāditam. yathā:
[112.18]     "iti stuto me bhagavannanāde juṣasva bhaktasya viśeṣataś ca /
[112.19]     sṛṣṭiṃ sṛjasveti tu coditasya sarvajñatāṃ dehi namo 'stu viṣṇo //" iti [VarāhaP]
[112.20]     evaṃ stotre parisamāpite
[112.21]     "varaṃ varava bhadraṃ te devadeva umāpate //" [VarāhaP]
[112.22]     iti bhagavatā niyuktaḥ rudra:
[112.23]     "brahmaṇā cāham uktas tu prajās sṛja iti prabho /
[112.24]     tatra jñānaṃ prayacchasva trividhaṃ bhūtabhāvana //" iti prārthayāmāsa. [VarāhaP]






     [viṣṇoḥ śarabharūparudrādisaṃhārakatvam]

[113.1]     tadā śrībhagavān:
[113.2]     "sarvajñas tvaṃ na sandeho jñānarāśisanātanaḥ /
[113.3]     devānāñ ca sadā pūjyaḥ sarvadā tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi // [VarāhaP.]
[113.4]     evam ukte punarvākyam uvācomāpatir mudā /
[113.5]     anyaṃ dehi varaṃ deva prasiddhaṃ sarvajantuṣu // [VarāhaP]
[113.6]     martyo bhūtvā bhavān eva māmārādhaya keśava /
[113.7]     māṃ vahasya ca deveśa varaṃ matto gṛhāṇa ca // [VarāhaP.]
[113.8]     yenāhaṃ sarvadevānāṃ pūjyāt pūjyataro 'bhavat //" iti punaḥ tena prārthitaḥ [VarāhaP]
[113.9]     śrībhagavān: "devakāryāvatāreṣu mānuṣyatvam upāgataḥ /
[113.10]     tvām evārādhayiṣyāmi tvañ ca me varado bhava // [VarāhaP]
[113.11]     yattvayoktaṃ vahasveti devadeva umāpate /
[113.12]     sa tvāṃ vahāmi deva tvāṃ megho bhūtvā śataṃ samāḥ //" iti varam api dadau.
[113.13]     "evam eva harir devaḥ sarveśas sarvabhāvanaḥ /
[113.14]     varado 'bhūt purā mahyaṃ tenāhaṃ daivatair vṛtaḥ // [VarāhaP.]
[113.15]     nārāyaṇāt paro devo na bhūto na bhaviṣyati /
[113.16]     etad rahasyaṃ devānāṃ purāṇānāñ ca sattama //" iti [VarāhaP]
[113.17]     kiñca
[113.18]     śrīviṣṇupurāṇe: "devatiryaṅmanuṣyeṣu śarīragrahaṇātmikā /
[113.19]     līleyaṃ sarvabhūtasya tava ceṣṭopalakṣaṇā // [ViṣṇuP ]
[113.20]     devatiryaṅmanuṣyākhyā ceṣṭāvanti svalīlayā /
[113.21]     jagatām upakārāya na sā karmanimittajā //" iti [ViṣṇuP ]
[113.22-23]     evaṃ nṛsiṃharūpiṇā bhagavatā śarabharūpeṇāgatānāṃ brahmarudrādīnām api saṃhārādikaṃ nārasiṃhapurāṇādiṣv avagamyate. yathā:

     [śarabhanirmāṇādiprakāraḥ]

[114.1]     hiraṇyakavadhānantaraṃ: tatra saptatriṃśādhyāye
[114.2]     "hiraṇyakaśipos trastān sendrān devān bṛhaspatiḥ /
[114.3]     kṣīrodasyottaraṃ gatvā stūyatāṃ tatra keśavaḥ // [NarasiṃhaP]
[114.4]     yuṣmābhis saṃstuto viṣṇuḥ prasanno bhavati kṣaṇāt//" ity ārabhya [NarasiṃhaP]
[114.5]     "yuṣmad āgamanaṃ sarvaṃ jānāmy asuramardanāḥ /
[114.6]     hiraṇyakavināśārthaṃ stuto 'haṃ śaṅkareṇa ca // ity uktvā [NarasiṃhaP]
[114.7]     hiraṇyakavadhānantaraṃ
[114.8]     "tasya kopābhibhūtasya nṛsiṃhasya jagatpateḥ /
[114.9]     dṛṣṭvā bhayānakaṃ rūpaṃ vitresur devadānavāḥ //" [NarasiṃhaP]
[114.10]     ity ārabhyoktastotrānantaraṃ brahmasamīpagamanādikaṃ pratipādya:
[114.11]     "tasmin bhagavati kruddhe nṛsiṃhe paramātmani /
[114.12]     pravepitaṃ jagad idaṃ deveśe kupite bhṛśam // [NarasiṃhaP]
[114.13]     tvatto hi nānyaś śaraṇaṃ devānām iha vidyate /
[114.14]     narasiṃhasamudbhūtaṃ bhayaṃ nāśaya me hare //" [NarasiṃhaP]
[114.15]     ityādinā rudraprārthanādikam uktvā
[114.16] "hato hiraṇyakaśipuḥ yena daityo mahābalaḥ /
[114.17]     ko naś śamayitā tasya kopasya harimedhasaḥ // [NarasiṃhaP.]
[114.18]     tvaṃ me janayitā deva sa te janayitā hariḥ /
[114.19]     tasya devasya kaś śakto viṣṇor vai nigrahe bhavet // [NarasiṃhaP]
[114.20]     yad bhayāt pavate vāyuḥ sūryas tapati yad bhayāt /
[114.21]     yad bhayād dharaṇī dhatte nigrahe tasya kaḥ prabhuḥ /
[114.22]     tathāpy upāyo dṛśyo me parameṇa samādhinā // [NarasiṃhaP]
[114.23]     kṛte tasmin bhavec chreyaḥ tūṣṇīṃ bhāvo na rocate /
[114.24]     aśvānāṃ mahiṣaḥ śatruḥ vāraṇānāṃ mṛgādhipaḥ // [NarasiṃhaP.]
[115.1]     vānarāṇāṃ tathā meṣaḥ phaṇīnāṃ garuḍaḥ smṛtaḥ /
[115.2]     mūṣakānān tu mārjāro mṛgāṇāṃ śvā prakīrtitaḥ // [NarasiṃhaP.]
[115.3]     vāyasānāṃ divābhītaḥ siṃhānāṃ śarabhas tathā /
[115.4]     tato nirmāpayiṣyāmaḥ śarabhaṃ bhayaśāntaye // [NarasiṃhaP.]
[115.5]     śarabho 'dhiṣṭhito 'smābhiḥ nṛsiṃhaṃ śamayiṣyati /
[115.6]     ity evam uktvā bhagavān sasarja śarabhaṃ tathā // [NarasiṃhaP.]
[115.7]     yasya sandarśanād eva trastamāsīj jagattrayam /
[115.8]     tatas tasya bhavānīśaḥ tuṇḍasthānam arocata // [NarasiṃhaP]
[115.9]     pṛṣṭhabhāge caturvaktaṃ tasya rudro nyaveśayat /
[115.10]     somasūryau nayanayoḥ mārutaṃ pakṣayor dvayoḥ // [NarasiṃhaP]
[115.11]     pādeṣu bhūdharān sarvān śivas tasya nyaveśayat /
[115.12]     evaṃ nirmāya śarabhaṃ bhavaḥ pramathanāyakaḥ // [NarasiṃhaP]
[115.13]     jagarja narasiṃhaṃ taṃ samuddiśya bhayānakam //" [NarasiṃhaP]
[115.14]     iti śarabhanirmāṇādikaṃ pratipādya
[115.15]     "tataḥ kṣaṇena śarabho nādapūritadiṅmukhaḥ /
[115.16]     abhyāśam agamad viṣṇoḥ ninadan bhairavaṃ svanam // [NarasiṃhaP]
[115.17]     tam abhyāśagataṃ dṛṣṭvā nṛsiṃhaḥ śarabhaṃ ruṣā /
[115.18]     jaghāna niśitair ugraiḥ nakhair nakhavarāyudhaḥ // [NarasiṃhaP]
[115.19]     nihate śarabhe tasmin raudre madhuvighātinā /
[115.20]     tuṣṭubuḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ devā devarṣayas tathā //" [NarasiṃhaP]
[115.21]     iti bhagavatā brahmarudrādyadhiṣṭhitaśarabhahananaṃ pratipāditam.
[115.22]     gāruḍe aṣṭanavatitamādhyāye:
[115.23]     "hantuṃ abhyāgataṃ raudraṃ śarabhaṃ narakesarī /
[115.24]     nakhair vidārayāmāsa hiraṇyakaśipuṃ yathā // [GaruḍaP ]
[116.1]     nikṛttabāhūruśirāḥ vajrakalpamukhair nakhaiḥ /
[116.2]     merupṛṣṭhe nṛsiṃhena śarabhas sahasāpatat //" [GaruḍaP ]
[116.3]     pādme: "tau yudhyamānau tu ciraṃ vegena balavattarau /
[116.4]     vināśaṃ jagmatur devau nṛsiṃhaśarabhāv iti // [Padma.P ]
[116.5]     tataḥ kruddho mahābāhuḥ nṛsiṃho bhīmanissvanaḥ /
[116.6]     sahasrakarapannetraḥ tasya gātrāṇy akartayat // [Padma.P ]
[116.7]     patitaṃ bhīmam atyugraṃ gatāṃsuṃ draṣṭum āgatāḥ /
[116.8]     ṛṣayo devagandharvā yatra śete bhavo haraḥ // [Padma.P ]
[116.9]     taṃ dṛṣṭvā paramaṃ jagmuḥ vismayantu divaukasaḥ /
[116.10]     paśaśaṃsus tathā karma nṛsiṃhasya mahādbhutam //" iti [PadmaP ]
[116.11]     śrībhāgavate: "tatas tvaritam ādāya rudraṃ śarabharūpiṇam /
[116.12]     vidadāra nakhais tīkṣṇaiḥ hiraṇyakaśipuṃ yathā //" iti [BhāgavataP ]

     [rudropāsakānāṃ śūdratulyatvam]

[116.13-14]     kiñca ānuśāsanike umāmaheśvarasaṃvāde bhagavato 'ṅgabhāvena vinā rudropāsanaṃ kurvatāṃ śudratulyatvam uktam. yathā dakṣādhvare:
[116.15]     rudrāṇī: ahaṃ jyeṣṭhā viśiṣṭā ca tasmāt tvaṃ māṃ supūjaya /
[116.16]     dakṣa: na tu jyeṣṭhā viśiṣṭā tvaṃ mama pūjyā imās surāḥ //" [MBh ]
[116.17]     ityādinā rudrāṇīdūṣaṇam adhvarabhaṅgādikaṃ ca pratipādya rudraṃ prati śāpotsargaḥ kriyate.
[116.18]     "etad vaṃśasamudbhūtair aspṛśyas tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi /
[116.19]     naitad vaṃśeṣu yaḥ kaścit tvadbhakto hi janiṣyati // [MBh ]
[116.20]     ajānāt tvāṃ hi yaḥ kaścit munir vā brāhmaṇo 'pi vā /
[116.21]     anujīvati cet tasmāt tulyaś śūdreṇa garhitaḥ // [MBh ]
[116.22]     bhaved devalakaś caiva rudrakālyupajīvakaḥ //" iti [MBh ]




     [bodhāyanādīnāṃ paramaikāntitvābhāve hetavaḥ]

     [kātyāyanasūtriṇāṃ paramaikāntitvābhāvaḥ]

[116.23-117.2]     ato nārāyaṇasya rudreṇa samānatayā bodhāyanena pratipāditvāt bodhāyanāpastambādisūtreṣu ṣadvidhatātparyaliṅgābhāvāt teṣāṃ sṛṣṭikālād ārabhya nārāyaṇaikaparatvābhāvāt nānādevatopāsakatvadarśanāc ca paramaikāntitvaṃ na sambhavati. evaṃ kātyāyanasūtriṇām api:
[117.3]     "brāhmavaiṣṇavaraudrais tu sāvitrair maitravāruṇaiḥ /
[117.4]     talliṅgair eva mantrais tu arcayet tu samāhitaḥ //" [Kātyāyanasūtra]
[117.5]     iti pratipādanāt na paramaikāntitvam.
[117.6]     drāhyāyaṇasūtre tu rudraviṣayatvena karmārambhe prapadanam uktam.
[117.7-9]     ataḥ śrīmannārāyaṇaikaparatvāt paramaikāntitvaṃ śrīmadvaikhānasānām eveti pratijñā kartum ucitā. evaṃ "akhilajagadekakāraṇaśrīmannārāyaṇaikaparatvāt" iti navamahetur nirūpitaḥ.
[117.10]     iti navamahetunirūpaṇam.

     [daśamahetunirūpaṇam]

     [vaikhānasānāṃ bhagavatpriyatamatvam]

[118.1-3]     athāsya śrīvaikhānasasūtrasya śīmannārāyaṇaikaparatvād tatsūtrānuṣṭhānavatām eva bhagavatpriyatamatvam upapadyata iti pratipādanāya "bhagavatpriyatamatvopapatter" iti daśamahetur nirūpyate.
[118.4-5]     chandogabrāhmaṇe: "vaikhānasā vā ṛṣaya indrasya priyā āsan" iti. atra indraśabdaḥ paramātmapara iti pūrvam evoktam.
[118.6]     vārāhe: "aśvatthaḥ kapilā gāvaḥ tulasī vikhanās tathā /
[118.7]     catvāro matpriyā rājan teṣāṃ vaikhānaso varaḥ // [VarāhaP]
[118.8]     yatra vaikhānasā viprā yatra santi gavāṃ gaṇāḥ /
[118.9]     yatra bilvāḥ palāśāś ca tatra sannihito hariḥ //" iti [VarāhaP]
[118.10]     kaurme: "maccitā madgataprāṇā mayi saṅgatamānasāḥ /
[118.11]     ananyaśaraṇā rājan tasmād vaikhānasā varāḥ //" [KūrmaP ]
[118.12]     pāñcarātre pauṣkare: "viprā vaikhānasākhyā ye te bhaktās tattvam ucyate // [PauṣkaraS 36.260cd]
[118.13]     ekantinaḥ susatvasthā dehāntaṃ nānyayājinaḥ /
[118.14]     kartavyam iti deveśaṃ saṃyajante phalaṃ vinā // [PauṣkaraS 36.261]
[118.15]     prāpnuvanti ca dehānte vāsudevatvam abjaja // [PauṣkaraS 36.262ab]

     [devārcanaparāṇāṃ śraiṣṭhyam]

[118.16]     bṛhannāradīye: "devārcanaparā ye ca ye ca tatsādhakā narāḥ /
[118.17]     pūjāṃ dṛṣṭvānumodante te vai bhāgavatottamāḥ // [BṛhannāradaP.]
[118.18]     yas tu bhogatayā viṣṇoḥ satkṛtyaṃ kurute sadā /
[118.19]     sa bhavet paramaikāntī mahābhāgavatottamaḥ // [BṛhannāradaP.]
[118.20]     ya aikāntyagatā viṣṇau bhagavatyātmabhāvane /
[118.21]     te vaiṣṇavā bhāgavatās santa ity api kīrtitāḥ // [BṛhannāradaP]






     [viṣṇuniveditānnādeḥ bhojyatvam]

[119.1]     manmānasāś ca madbhaktā mama pūjāsu lolupāḥ /
[119.2]     matkathāśravaṇe sattās te vai bhāgavatāḥ smṛtāḥ //" iti [BṛhannāradaP]
[119.3]     "ye 'rcayanti narā bhaktyā nārāyaṇam anāmayam /
[119.4]     tān arcayanti vibudhā brahmādyā devatāgaṇāḥ //
[119.5]     mayi bhaktiparo yas tu madyājī matparāyaṇaḥ /
[119.6]     maddhyānī svakulaṃ sarvaṃ nayaty acyutarūpatām //
[119.7]     ye 'rcayanti sadā viṣṇuṃ na te prākṛtamānuṣāḥ /
[119.8]     viṣṇulokāt samutpannās te devā nātra saṃśayaḥ // [ĀS 14.58]
[119.9]     nāviṣṇur jayate viṣṇur nāviṣṇur viṣṇum arcayet /
[119.10]     rūpadvayaṃ hareḥ proktaṃ bimbam arcaka eva ca // [KrA 36.59cd]
[119.11]     bimbe tv āvāhanād ūrdhvaṃ sadā sannihito 'rcake / [KrA 36.60ab]
[119.12]     arcakas tu prasannātmā harir eva na saṃśayaḥ //
[119.13]     kaliḥ kṛtayugas teṣāṃ kleśāś caiva sukhāvahāḥ /
[119.14]     yeṣāṃ śarīram aniśaṃ hariśuśrūṣaṇe ratam //" iti
[119.15]     bhāgavate: "sā vāg anantarasya guṇān gṛṇīte karau ca tatkarmakarau manaś ca /
[119.16]     smared vasantaṃ sthirajaṅgameṣu śruṇoti tatpuṇyakathās sa karṇaḥ //
[119.17]     śiraś ca tasyāṅghriṣu namramāṇaṃ tam eva yaḥ paśyati taddhi cakṣuḥ /
[119.18]     aṅgāni viṣṇor atha tajjanānāṃ pādodakaṃ yāni vahanti nityam // [BhāgavataP 10.80.4]
[119.19]     hṛdi rūpaṃ mukhe nāma naivedyam udare hareḥ /
[119.20]     pādodakañ ca nirmālyaṃ yasya mūrdhni sa vaiṣṇavaḥ //" iti [BhāgavataP ]





[119.21-120.3]     śrutir api: "tad asya priyam abhipātho aśyām naro yatra devayavo madanti urukramasya sa hi bandhur itthā viṣṇoḥ pade parame madhva utsaḥ" iti. asyārthaḥ: viṣṇoḥ 'priyaṃ'; tatpāthaḥ niveditam annādikam 'abhyaśyām'. 'devayavo narāḥ'; devārādhakāḥ 'yatra madanti'; yasmin niveditatīrthaprasādādike svīkṛte 'madanti'; hṛṣṭā bhavanti. yadvā: brahmādīn api na gaṇayanti. 'itthā'; itthaṃ pratidinaṃ vartamānaḥ 'urukramasya viṣṇor bandhuḥ'; jātyekavacanam. sa evātīvābhimataḥ 'parame'; sarvotkṛṣṭe 'madhve'; madhuvat bhogyatame viṣṇoḥ pade 'utsa'; utsukaḥ. yadvā utkṛṣṭaḥ.
[120.4-5]     śrutyantare: "viṣṇunāśitam aśnanti viṣṇunā pītaṃ pibanti viṣṇuna ghrātaṃ jighranti viṣṇunā rasitaṃ rasayanti tasmād vidvāṃso viṣṇūpahṛtaṃ bhakṣayeyuḥ" iti.
[120.7]     bhāgavate: "tvayopabhuktasraggandha vāso 'laṅkāracarcitāḥ /
[120.8]     ucchiṣṭabhojino dāsās tava māyāṃ taremahi //" iti [BhāgavataP 11.6.46]
[120.9]     hārīta: "kṛpādattaṃ hastagataṃ viṣṇubhuktojjhitantu yat /
[120.10]     upavāsachalānnātti tena bhuktaṃ suropamam //" iti
[120.11]     bhṛgu: "haviḥ kṛtvā caturbhāgam ūrdhvabhāgau nivedayet /
[120.12]     adhastād ekabhāgena homa balim athācaret //
[120.13]     yadaṃśaṃ pātrasaṃśiṣṭaṃ pūjakāyaiva nirmitam /
[120.14]     agnikāryāvaśiṣṭañ ca baliśiṣṭañ ca yad dhaviḥ /
[120.15]     sarvaṃ tatpūjakāyaiva proktam evaṃ manīṣibhiḥ //" iti
[120.16]     yajñādhikāre bhṛgu: "ātmanaś ca caturthāṃśaṃ vaiśvadevārtham arcakaḥ /
[120.17]     ādāya vaiśvadevānte śiṣṭānnaṃ bhojayet punaḥ // [Y.A ]
[120.18]     baliśeṣaṃ homaśeṣaṃ vaiśvadeve viśeṣataḥ /
[120.19]     gṛhṇīyād vaiśvadevārthaṃ bhojanārthañ ca ṛtvijaḥ //" iti [YA ]
[120.20-23]     kāśyapa: "sarvahaviḥ pātreṣu śiṣṭam annaṃ sarvaṃ bhagavanniveditam apūpādikañ ca pūjakā gṛhṇīyuḥ. yathā guror ucchiṣṭaṃ putraśiṣyabhṛtyānāṃ bhojyaṃ. tathā sarvasya rakṣituḥ saumyamūrte sarvavyāpino viṣṇoḥ jagadguror niveditam annādyaṃ viśvaṃ caturvarṇānāṃ bhaktimatāṃ sarveṣāṃ bhojyam, abhaktimatām abhojyam" iti.
[120.24]     śrīpāñcarātre īśvarasaṃhitāyāṃ samārādhanādhyāye
[120.25]     skanda: "tvayā niṣedha ākhyāto mantradattasya vastunaḥ /
[120.26]     sarvasya patrapuṣpānna pūrvasya parameśvara // [ĪśvaraS ]





     [arcāvatārasya sakalalokojjīvanārthatā]

[121.1]     tasyedānīṃ pradānañ ca prāśanañ ca praśaṃsasi /
[121.2]     kim etad atra me jātas saṃśayaḥ parameśvara // [ĪśvaraS ]
[121.3]     īśvara:pradānaṃ prāśanaṃ putra upabhogyatvam eva ca /
[121.4]     śaive pāśupate dṛṣṭam acirād eva pāpakṛt //
[121.5]     tatpunar vaiṣṇave mārge vartate vyatyayena tu /
[121.6]     anantaphaladaṃ dānāt prāśānāt koṣṭaśuddhikṛt //" iti [ĪśvaraS ]
[121.7]     tatraiva devatārcane: "karṣaṃ nayati pāpāni puṇyavṛddhiṃ karoti ca /
[121.8]     dānair dharmaiḥ tathā puṇyais tapobhiś ca na tatphalam // [ĪśvaraS ]
[121.9]     bhagavadbhaktipūtānāṃ yatphalaṃ prāpaṇādanāt //" iti [ĪśvaraS ]
[121.10]     anyatra: "satsaṅgadevārcanasatkathāsu paropadeśe ca rato manuṣyaḥ /
[121.11]     sa yāti viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ yaddehāvasāne 'cyutatulyatejāḥ //" iti
[121.12]     anyatra: "nārāyaṇaikaniṣṭhā ye sāttvikās tān nibodhata /
[121.13]     puruṣā rājasāś caiva nānādaivatayājinaḥ //
[121.14]     bāhyā nirdevatāś caiva tāmasāḥ parikīrtitāḥ /
[121.15]     rajastamo 'bhibhūtānāṃ na tu mokṣaḥ kathañcana //" iti
[121.16]     purāṇāntare: "yatraiva pūjyate viṣṇur vidhinā prayatair naraiḥ /
[121.17]     na tatra hy ādhidaurgatya vyādhicaurādikaṃ bhayam //" iti
[121.18]     kiñca: "nityamuktopabhogyatvāt paravyūhātmano hareḥ /
[121.19]     tatkālasannikṛṣṭaika lakṣyatvād vibhavātmanaḥ // [Ā.S 14.14]
[121.20]     viśuddhair yogasaṃsiddhaiś cintyatvād antarātmanaḥ /
[121.21]     arcātmany eva sarveṣām adhikāro niraṅkuśaḥ // [Ā.S 14.15]
[121.22]     arcāvatāraviṣaye mamāpy uddeśatas tathā /
[121.23]     uktā guṇā na śakyante vaktuṃ varṣaśatair api // [Ā.S 14.16]
[122.1]     evaṃ pañcaprakāro 'ham ātmanāṃ patatāmadhaḥ /
[122.2]     pūrvasmād api pūrvasmāt jyāyāṃś caivottarottaraḥ // [Ā.S ]
[122.3]     saulabhyataṃ jagatsvāmī sulabho hy uttarottaraḥ //" [ĀS ]
[122.4-7]     iti pratipāditarityā bhagavataḥ paratvādiṣu saulabhyābhāvāt akhilalokasamujjīvanārtham arcāvatāraḥ. tadekaparatvād vaikhānasāḥ tatpriyatamāḥ. etadṛśanārāyaṇāyaṇaikaparatvābhāvād bodhāyanasya āpastambādīnāñ na kathañcad api paramaikāntitvaṃ bhagavatpriyatamatvañ ca sambhavati.
[122.8-9]     evaṃ ca vaikhānasānām eva paramaikāntitvaṃ bhagavatpriyatamatvañ copapadyate iti sarvaṃ samañjasam iti daśamo hetur nirūpitam.
[122.10]     iti daśamahetunirūpaṇam
[122.11-14]     iti śrīramaṇaveṅkaṭācaleśvarapādāravindasaparyāniratasya sarvatantrasvatantrasya śrīnivāsamakhivedāntadeśikasya kṛtiṣu śrīvaikhānasasūtratātparyacintāmaṇau daśavidhahatunirūpaṇam upodghātabhāgaḥ samāptaḥ.
